## TOPIC 00501: Curve Parameters: Characteristic Diagram » Points » Measurement Points » Markers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_point_measpoint_marker_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_point_measpoint_marker_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) > [Characteristic Diagram](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_general_dialog.htm) > [Points](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_cdiagrampoints_general.htm) > [Measurement Points](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_points_measpoints_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: Characteristic Diagram » Points » Measurement Points » Markers

Curve Parameters: Characteristic Diagram » Points » Measurement Points » Markers

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays measurement points of a characteristic diagram in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAdditionalMarker](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3markeradditionalint.htm) object.

| Measurement points | Specifies whether DIAdem also selects the measurement points. DIAdem only displays valid points and peak values without NoValues as x- or y-values. |
| --- | --- |
| Marker style | Specifies the symbol for the markers on the curve. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the markers. |
| Size | Specifies the size of the markers. |
| Marker color | Specifies the color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the markers in the same color as the curve. |
| Filling color | Specifies the filling color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the marker filling in the same color as the curve. |

## TOPIC 00502: Curve Parameters: Characteristic Diagram » Points » Minimum » Labels

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_point_minpoint_label_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_point_minpoint_label_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) > [Characteristic Diagram](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_general_dialog.htm) > [Points](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_cdiagrampoints_general.htm) > [Minimum](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_points_minimum_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: Characteristic Diagram » Points » Minimum » Labels

Curve Parameters: Characteristic Diagram » Points » Minimum » Labels

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays minimum values of a characteristic diagram in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DCharacteristicDiagramPointsLabel](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3characteristicdiagrampointslabelint.htm) object.

|  | Minimum | Specifies whether DIAdem also selects the minimum measurement points. DIAdem only displays valid points, which are points without NoValues as x- or y-values. In a differential characteristic diagram, the minimum measurement points do not lie exactly on the actual measurement points because the data is interpolated. The more grid points you use for the interpolation, the more exactly the minimum points lie on the actual minimum points in the interpolation field. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Z-value at point | Specifies that DIAdem labels the additional minimum measurement points in characteristic diagrams with the z-value of the measurement points. |
|  | Data reduction value | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the measured value or the value of the data reduction. This setting is only available if the data has a triplet structure and if the display type is not a differential characteristic diagram. |
|  | Font | Specifies the font for the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Font size | Specifies the font size for the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Format | Specifies the format definition of the minimum measurement points. You can include subscript and superscript in text, format numbers, include variable contents, or use scripts for complex formats. Refer to the page on Formatting Text for more information. |
|  | Format Numbers | Opens the dialog box where you select or enter the format specification. |
|  | Angle | Specifies the angle of the label of the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Position | Specifies the position of the minimum measurement points in relation to the curve data points. |
|  | Font color | Specifies the color of the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Highlighting color | Specifies the color in which you highlight the labels. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
|  | Color Palette | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color assignments for the font color Palette. |
|  | Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the minimum measurement points. |
|  | Frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames each minimum measurement point. |

#### Further Settings

| Line width | Specifies the line width of the markers. |
| Size | Specifies the size of the markers. |
| Marker color | Specifies the color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the markers in the same color as the curve. |
| Filling color | Specifies the filling color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the marker filling in the same color as the curve. |

## TOPIC 00504: Generate Isolines

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_generate_isolines_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_generate_isolines_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) > [Characteristic Diagram](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_general_dialog.htm) > [Isolines](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_parameters_isolines_general.htm) > [Contour Table](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_contour_table_dialog.htm) > Generate Isolines

Generate Isolines

Use this dialog box to generate isolines in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

| Method | Specifies whether DIAdem separates the contour lines into ranges with fixed step widths or into a certain number of intervals. |
| --- | --- |
| Start value | Specifies the minimum isoline value. For a differential characteristic diagram, DIAdem determines the displayed minimum within the overlap range of the two characteristic diagrams. |
| Step width | Specifies the step width DIAdem separates the contours into. |
| Number of intervals | Specifies the number of intervals that DIAdem separates the contours into. |
| End value | Specifies the maximum isolines value. For a differential characteristic diagram, DIAdem determines the displayed maximum within the overlap range of the two characteristic diagrams. |
| Color | Specifies the color of the isolines. |
| Line style | Specifies the line style of the isolines. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the isolines. |
| Line interval | Specifies the interval and the length of the line sections for broken line display. |
| Continue color count automatically | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically uses the next color in the list when you generate several isolines simultaneously. |

|  | Note The line properties are only available if you select the color Palette on the Isoline»General tab. |
| --- | --- |

#### Examples

[3D Axis System with Isolines and 3D Curves](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av17.htm) | [3D Axis System with Surface and Isolines](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av15.htm)

## TOPIC 00505: Curve Parameters: Isolines » Labels » Text Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_isolines_symbol_textpar_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_isolines_symbol_textpar_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) > [Isolines](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_isolines_general_dialog.htm) > [Labels](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_isolinessymbols_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: Isolines » Labels » Text Parameters

Curve Parameters: Isolines » Labels » Text Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays labels in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAdditionalIsolineLabel](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3labelisolineadditionalint.htm) object.

| Label | Specifies whether DIAdem displays additional labels. |
| --- | --- |
| Font | Specifies the font for the labels. |
| Font size | Specifies the font size for the labels. |
| Font color | Specifies the color of the labels. |
| Highlighting color | Specifies the font color with which you highlight the labels. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
| Color Palette | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color assignments for the font color Palette. |
| Angle | Specifies the angle of the symbol label. |
| Position | Specifies the position of the labels in relation to the curve data points. |
| Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the labels. |
| Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the labels. |
| Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the labels. |
| Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the labels. |
| Frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames each label. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_isolines_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels » Text](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_isolines_symbol_dialog.htm) | [Labels » Position](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_isolines_symbol_position_dialog.htm) | Labels » Text Parameters

#### Other Curve Displays

## TOPIC 00506: Curve Parameters: 2D Matrix » General

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_matrix_general_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_matrix_general_dialog.htm

- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: 2D Matrix » General

Curve Parameters: 2D Matrix » General

Use this dialog box to specify the curve display in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DMatrix2DSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3shapeobjmatrix2dsettingsint.htm) object.

| Hidden line calculation | Specifies whether DIAdem displays hidden lines. |
| --- | --- |
| Plot bars with a height of 0 | Specifies whether DIAdem plots bars with a height of 0. |
| Width |  |
| X-direction | Specifies the width of the 3D bars. |
| Y-direction | Specifies the height of the 3D bars. |
| Offset |  |
| X-direction | Specifies the percentage offset in x-direction from the middle of the rectangles. |
| Y-direction | Specifies the percentage offset in y-direction from the middle of the rectangles. |
| Line color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
| Palette | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color assignments for the line color Palette. |
| Line style | Specifies the line style of the curve. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the curve. |
| Line interval | Specifies the interval and the length of the line sections for broken line display. |

#### Further Settings

Curve Parameters: 2D Matrix » Labels » Position

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays labels in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DLabelPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3labelpositionint.htm) object.

| Label | Specifies whether DIAdem displays additional labels. |
| --- | --- |
| Label plane | Specifies how DIAdem positions the curve label in relation to the curve point. |
| Offset in x-direction [%] | Specifies the fixed x-position of the curve label in relation to the axis origin. |
| Offset in y-direction [%] | Specifies the fixed y-position of the curve label in relation to the axis origin. |
| Offset in z-direction [%] | Specifies the fixed z-position of the curve labels in relation to the axis origin. |
| Every n points | Specifies that DIAdem only displays the labels at every nth point on the curve. |

Curve Parameters: 2D Matrix » Labels » Text Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays labels in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAdditionalLabel](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3labeladditionalint.htm) object.

| Label | Specifies whether DIAdem displays additional labels. |
| --- | --- |
| Font | Specifies the font for the labels. |

| Font color | Specifies the color of the labels. |

| Color Palette | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color assignments for the font color Palette. |
| Angle | Specifies the angle of the symbol label. |
| Position | Specifies the position of the labels in relation to the curve data points. |
| Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the labels. |
| Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the labels. |
| Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the labels. |
| Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the labels. |
| Frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames each label. |

## TOPIC 00509: Curve Parameters: Spikes » Markers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spike_marker_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spike_marker_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) > [Spikes](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spikes_general_dialog.htm) > Curve Parameters: Spikes » Markers

Curve Parameters: Spikes » Markers

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays markers in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAdditionalMarker](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3markeradditionalint.htm) object.

| Markers | Specifies whether DIAdem also displays markers. DIAdem plots the markers in the order of the measurement values regardless of visibility. |
| --- | --- |
| Marker style | Specifies the symbol for the markers on the curve. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the markers. |
| Size | Specifies the size of the markers. |
| Size from channel | Specifies the channel whose values DIAdem uses for the size of the markers. |
| Display from [%] | Specifies the minimum size from which DIAdem draws the marker. |
| Marker color | Specifies the color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, DIAdem displays the markers the same color as the curve. |
| Filling color | Specifies the filling color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the marker filling the same color as the curve. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spikes_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels » Text](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spikes_symbol_dialog.htm) | [Labels » Position](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spikes_symbol_position_dialog.htm) | [Labels » Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spikes_symbol_textpar_dialog.htm) | Markers

## TOPIC 00510: Curve Parameters: Points » Labels » Text

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_symbol_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_symbol_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) | [Points](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_symbols_general.htm)) > [Labels](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_symbols_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: Points » Labels » Text

Curve Parameters: Points » Labels » Text

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays labels in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAdditionalLabel](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3labeladditionalint.htm) object.

| Label | Specifies whether DIAdem displays additional labels. |
| --- | --- |
| Free text | Specifies the labels. Refer to Displaying Points and Symbols in Axis Systems for more information about label formats. |
| Text | Specifies that DIAdem displays the x-coordinates at the curve points. |
| X-value | Specifies the format specifications for the x-values of the 3D curve labels. |
| Format | Specifies that DIAdem displays the y-coordinates at the curve points. |
| Y-value | Specifies the format specifications for the y-values of the 3D curve labels. |
| Format | Specifies that DIAdem displays the z-coordinates at the curve points. |
| Z-value | Specifies the format specifications for the z-values of the 3D curve labels. |
| Format | Specifies that DIAdem displays the point numbers at the curve points. |
| Value index | Specifies the format specifications for the x-values of the 3D curve labels. |
| Format | Specifies whether the text of the 3D curve labels contains values from a different channel. |
| From channel | Specifies the additional channel from which DIAdem takes the labels for the 3D curve. |
| Channel | Specifies the format specifications for the curve label when DIAdem takes the values from an additional channel. |
| Format | Specifies the index channel for the additional channel from which DIAdem takes the curve labels of the 3D curve. |
| Index channel | Specifies the separators that DIAdem uses between the text of the curve label. |

#### Further Settings

Labels » Text | [Labels » Position](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_symbol_symbol_position_dialog.htm) | [Labels » Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_symbol_textpar_dialog.htm) | [Markers](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_symbol_marker_dialog.htm)

#### Other Curve Displays

[Surface](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_surface_general_dialog.htm) | [Isolines](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_isolines_general_dialog.htm) | [Waterfall](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_waterfall_general_dialog.htm) | [Bars](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_bar_general_dialog.htm) | [2D matrix](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_matrix_general_dialog.htm) | [Spikes](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_spikes_general_dialog.htm) | [3D curve](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_3dcurve_general_dialog.htm) | [Vector](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_vector_dialog.htm) | Points | [Characteristic diagram](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_tab_cdiagram_general_dialog.htm) | [Coordinate](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curve_par_coordinate_marker_dialog.htm)

- bundle_id: `diadem`

- content_type: ``

([Curve parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_curveparameters_general.htm) | [Points](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_symbols_general.htm)) > [Labels](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_symbols_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: Points » Labels » Text Parameters

Curve Parameters: Points » Labels » Text Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays labels in 3D axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAdditionalLabel](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3labeladditionalint.htm) object.

| Label | Specifies whether DIAdem displays additional labels. |
| --- | --- |
| Font | Specifies the font for the labels. |
| Font size | Specifies the font size for the labels. |
| Font color | Specifies the color of the labels. |
| Highlighting color | Specifies the font color with which you highlight the labels. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
| Color Palette | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color assignments for the font color Palette. |
| Angle | Specifies the angle of the symbol label. |
| Position | Specifies the position of the labels in relation to the curve data points. |
| Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the labels. |
| Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the labels. |
| Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the labels. |
| Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the labels. |
| Frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames each label. |

#### Further Settings

## TOPIC 00515: Data Check

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_cd_partialload_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_cd_partialload_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Data Check

Data Check

Use this dialog box to specify whether the triplet is distributed freely or in a partial load structure, how to define the partial loads, and which data is valid, in a 3D axis system for the **Characteristic Diagram** display type.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties of the [D3PartialLoad](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3partialloadint.htm) object.

| Partial load structure | Specifies whether the triplet data is distributed free or in a partial load structure. This setting specifies the interpolation mode of the z-values. If you enable this setting, DIAdem lays y-z-splines with regular interpolation points in y-direction through the points of every partial load. Then DIAdem lays x-z-splines through the interpolation points in x-direction. A partial load is made up of points with x-values that lie in the specified tolerance range. |
| --- | --- |
| Relative tolerance as % / Absolute tolerance | Specifies whether you define the tolerance as a percent of the entire x-area or as the absolute x-area. Points whose x-values lie outside the tolerance are invalid values of the partial load. |
| Relative tolerance | Specifies the maximum deviation of the x-value in the partial load as a percentage of the complete x-area. |
| Absolute tolerance | Specifies the maximum absolute deviation of the x-value within a partial load. |
| Display tolerance bands | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the tolerance band. |
| Minimum number for tolerance | Specifies the minimum number of measurement points that must belong to a partial load so that this value is valid. |
| Check z-value | Specifies whether DIAdem checks the z-value. If the z-value lies outside the specified limits, the value is invalid. |
| Minimum value | Specifies the bottom limit of the z-value to check. |
| Maximum value | Specifies the top limit of the z-value to check. |

#### Further Settings

[Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Displaying 3D Curves in 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_spacecurves.htm) | [Displaying Surfaces in 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_plains.htm) | [Moving Coordinate Planes in 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_layers.htm) | [Rotating 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_angle.htm)

#### Examples

[2D Axis Systems and 3D Axis Systems with Legends](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av34.htm) | [3D Axis System with a Matrix Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av4.htm) | [3D Axis System with Bar and Waterfall Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av14.htm) | [3D Axis System with Different Surface Displays](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av41.htm) | [3D Axis System with Isolines and 3D Curves](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av17.htm) | [3D Axis System with Logarithmic Scaling](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av18.htm) | [3D Axis System with Spike Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av19.htm) | [3D Axis System with Surface and Isolines](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av15.htm) | [3D Axis System with Surface Display and a Color Legend](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av20.htm) | [3D Axis System with Surface Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av16.htm) | [3D Axis Systems with Different Displays](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av40.htm) | [3D Axis Systems with Different Grid Displays](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av42.htm) | [3D-Axis System with Filled Bar Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av47.htm) | [3D-Axis System with Scalable Background Graphics](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_d3map_scalablebackgroundimage.htm) | [ASCII File Loading and 3D Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av20.htm) | [Characteristic Diagram Display](../../exploff/examples/report_characteristic_diagram.htm) | [Different Display Modes in DIAdem REPORT](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av46.htm) | [Grouping and Aligning Objects and Rotating Comments](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_formsheet.htm) | [Loading Excel Files with a DataPlugin](../../exploff/examples/expl_excel_plugin.htm) | [Rotating 3D Axis Systems](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av44.htm)

## TOPIC 00517: Curve Transformation

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_curvetransform_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_curvetransform_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Curve Transformation

Curve Transformation

Use this dialog box to specify the name of a curve transformation function. Use the curve transformation function to change the displayed channels while they are being plotted. DIAdem does not modify the original data. The transformed channels have the same display format as the original channels. For example, you cannot create a numeric channel from a time channel using the curve transformation. If you do not specify an x-channel and the y-channel is an xy-channel and you have selected the setting [When plotting xy-channels, determine x-channel automatically if not populated](../../varoff/applicationchnxyrelationbinding.htm) in the [General DIAdem Settings](../../dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm), you can also transform the x-channel that belongs to the y-channel. The display format remains the same.

#### Settings

| Name of user command for curve transformation | Specifies the name of the transformation function. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note Follow the instructions in Working with Events in DIAdem when you use curve transformation functions. |
| --- | --- |

#### See Also

[OnCurveTransformation](../../reportapi/events/report_event_oncurvetransformation_irepd3curveint.htm)

3D Axis Definition: Axis System

3D Axis Definition: Planes » Isometry

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the planes in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAxisSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3axissettingsint.htm) object.

| Isometric axis adaptation | Specifies whether DIAdem uses the same scale to display all axes or selected axes. |
| --- | --- |
| Axis adaptation | Specifies the axes that DIAdem displays with the same scale. DIAdem adjusts the display of the third axis to the greater of the two other value ranges to be displayed. |
| Length of 3rd axis | Specifies the scaling factor of the third axis as a percentage if you have two isometric axes. |
| Full screen mode | Specifies whether DIAdem fills the entire selected area, or whether DIAdem displays the xy-axes at right angles. If you do not select this setting, you only can resize the axis system proportionally. |

## TOPIC 00520: 3D Axis Definition: Planes

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_plane_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_plane_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Layers](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axissystem_general.htm) > 3D Axis Definition: Planes

3D Axis Definition: Planes

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the planes in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DAxisSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3axissettingsint.htm) object.

|  | Planes XY, XZ, YZ |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Display mode | Specifies whether DIAdem only displays axes, or whether DIAdem also displays frames and grid lines. Depending on the plane, you specify the Type for 3DPlaneXY, the Type for 3DPlaneXZ, or the Type for 3DPlaneYZ. |
|  | Background color | Specifies the background color for the plane of the 3D axis system. Depending on the plane, you specify BackgroundColor for 3DPlaneXY, BackgroundColor for 3DPlaneXZ, or BackgroundColor for 3DPlaneYZ. |
|  | Background graphic | Specifies the background graphic for the plane of the 3D axis system. Depending on the plane, you specify BackgroundImage for 3DPlaneXY, BackgroundImage for 3DPlaneXZ, or BackgroundColor for 3DPlaneYZ. |
|  | Open Dialog Box | Opens the dialog box where you select the background graphic. |
|  | Offset along the 3rd axis (%) | Specifies the relative offset of the planes along the axis that is vertical to the plane. Depending on the plane, you specify the Offset for 3DPlaneXY, the Offset for 3DPlaneXZ, or the Offset for 3DPlaneYZ. |
|  | Line color | Specifies the Color of the frame and of the grid lines for the selected plane.Depending on the plane, you use the objects 3DPlaneXY, 3DPlaneXZ, and 3DPlaneYZ and the property Borderline to access the frame, and the property Grid to access the gridlines. |
|  | Line style | Specifies the Line type of the frame and of the grid lines for the selected plane.Depending on the plane, you use the objects 3DPlaneXY, 3DPlaneXZ, and 3DPlaneYZ and the property Borderline to access the frame, and the property Grid to access the gridlines. |
|  | Line width | Specifies the Line width of the frame and of the grid lines for the selected plane.Depending on the plane, you use the objects 3DPlaneXY, 3DPlaneXZ, and 3DPlaneYZ and the property Borderline to access the frame, and the property Grid to access the gridlines. |
|  | Line partitioning | Specifies the interval and the length of the Line sections for broken frame lines and grid lines.Depending on the plane, you use the objects 3DPlaneXY, 3DPlaneXZ, and 3DPlaneYZ and the property Borderline to access the frame, and the property Grid to access the gridlines. |

#### Further Settings

[Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) | [Axis System](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_dialog.htm) | Planes | [Planes » Isometry](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_iso_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Scaling](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_scale_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Numbers](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_value_dialog.htm) |[Axis Parameters » Labels](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Displaying 3D Curves in 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_spacecurves.htm) | [Displaying Surfaces in 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_plains.htm) | [Moving Coordinate Planes in 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_layers.htm) | [Rotating 3D Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_3daxis_angle.htm)

## TOPIC 00521: 3D Axis Definition: Curve List

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > 3D Axis Definition: Curve List

3D Axis Definition: Curve List

Use this dialog box to generate or to delete curves in 3D axis systems or to modify the display.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DCurve](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3curveint.htm) object.

|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you define a new curve. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Copy Entry | Copies the selected curve to the end of the list. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected curve. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected curve one position up. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected curve one position down. |
|  | Curve Transformation | Opens the transformation dialog box, if you used Enable Curve Transformation to show this button.DIAdem opens a dialog box where you enter the name of a user command that DIAdem executes when plotting the curve. With the curve transformation function you can edit the displayed channels while they are being plotted. You can use the OnCurveTransformation property to define your own command which DIAdem calls when you click the curve transformation button. |
|  | Configure Curve Transformation | If you do not assign the standard command to the CurveTransformationConfiguration for Settings variable and you click Curve Transformation, an additional triangle appears to the right of the Curve Transformation button. Click the triangle to specify the name of the command that DIAdem calls when you click the Curve Transformation button in the 3D curve and axis definition dialog box. |
|  | No. | Displays the number of the curve. Click the number to select a curve. |
|  | Type | Specifies the display mode. Depending on the display mode, you specify different channels and structures. |
|  | Set Curve Parameters | Opens the dialog box for the display mode, where you can set more curve parameters. Possible display types are: Surface, Isolines, Waterfall, Bars, 2D matrix, Spikes, 3D curve, Vector, Points, Characteristic diagram, and Coordinate. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
|  | Set Palette | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color assignments for the line color Palette. |
|  | Channels | Displays the channels of the curve. You change the curve channels at the bottom of the dialog box. |
|  |  |  |
|  | Characteristic diagram | Specifies whether DIAdem displays a simple or a differential characteristic diagram for the Characteristic diagram display mode. |
|  | Differential characteristic diagram | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type whether DIAdem displays a relative or an absolute differential characteristic diagram. If you set Absolute, DIAdem subtracts the values of the first characteristic diagram from the second characteristic diagram. If you set Relative, DIAdem divides the difference of the characteristic diagrams by the values of the first characteristic diagram. |
|  | Triplet / Matrix | Specifies for the display modes Surface, Spikes, Points, Characteristic diagram, and Coordinate whether the data is in triplet or matrix form. Depending on the display type, you specify the various properties: Triplet / Matrix for Surface, Triplet / Matrix for Spikes, Triplet / Matrix for Points, Triplet / Matrix for Characteristic diagram, and Triplet / Matrix for Coordinate.A triplet consists of three channels of the same length, which contain the x, y, or z-values. A matrix consists of one x-channel, one y-channel, and several z-channels. The number of z-channels corresponds with the length of the y-channel. The length of the z-channels corresponds with the length of the x-channel. The z-channels must be in consecutive order in the data area. The x-channel and the y-channel can be anywhere in the data area. Refer to the DIAdem Help page Organizing 3D Data as Value Triplets and as Matrices for further information about organizing 3D data. |
|  | Isoline type | Specifies the plane in which DIAdem displays the contour lines in the Isolines display mode. |
|  | 4D vector / 6D vector | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the vectors four-dimensionally or six-dimensionally in the Vector display mode. |
|  | Vector plane | Specifies the plane that contains the vectors in the 4D vector display mode. |
|  | Display 3D curve | Specifies for the 3D curve whether DIAdem displays the 3D curve. |
|  | Project to XY plane | Specifies for the 3D curve whether DIAdem projects the 3D curve onto the XY plane. |
|  | Project to YZ plane | Specifies for the 3D curve whether DIAdem projects the 3D curve onto the YZ plane. |
|  | Project to XZ plane | Specifies for the 3D curve whether DIAdem projects the 3D curve onto the XZ plane. |
|  | X-channel | Specifies the channel containing the x-values of the curve.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the x-channel to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers. |
|  | Y-channel | Specifies the channel containing the y-values of the curve.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the y-channel to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers. |
|  | Z-channel | Specifies the channel containing the z-values of the curve.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the z-channel to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers.A triplet consists of three channels of the same length, which contain the x, y, or z-values. Refer to the DIAdem Help page Organizing 3D Data as Value Triplets and as Matrices for further information about organizing 3D data. |
|  | Z-matrix | Specifies which channels span the z-matrix.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the z-channels to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers.A matrix consists of one x-channel, one y-channel, and several z-channels. The number of z-channels corresponds with the length of the y-channel. The length of the z-channels corresponds with the length of the x-channel. The z-channels must be in consecutive order in the data area. The x-channel and the y-channel can be anywhere in the data area. Refer to the DIAdem Help page Organizing 3D Data as Value Triplets and as Matrices for further information about organizing 3D data. |
|  | X-channel starting points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the channel with the values of the first coordinate of the start of the vector. |
|  | Y-channel starting points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the channel with the values of the second coordinate of the start of the vector. |
|  | Z-channel starting points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the channel with the values of the third coordinate of the start of the vector. |
|  | X-channel end points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the channel with the values of the first coordinate of the end of the vector. |
|  | Y-channel end points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the channel with the values of the second coordinate of the end of the vector. |
|  | Z-channel end points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the channel with the values of the third coordinate of the end of the vector. |
|  | 1st X-channel | Specifies for the Isolines display type the first channel with the x-values of the first isoline. Each additional contour line needs an additional channel pair. |
|  | 1st Y-channel | Specifies for the Isolines display type the first channel with the y-values of the first isoline. Each additional contour line needs an additional channel pair. |
|  | 1st Z-channel | Specifies for the Isolines display type the first channel with the z-values of the first isoline. Each additional contour line needs an additional channel pair. |
|  | 1st X-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channel with the x-values of the first characteristic diagram. |
|  | 1st Y-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channel with the y-values of the first characteristic diagram. |
|  | 1st Z-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channel with the z-values of the first characteristic diagram. |
|  | 1st Z-matrix | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channels which span the z-matrix of the first characteristic diagram. |
|  | 2. X-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channel with the x-values of the second characteristic diagram. |
|  | 2. Y-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channel with the y-values of the second characteristic diagram. |
|  | 2. Z-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channel with the z-values of the second characteristic diagram. |
|  | 2. Z-matrix | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the channels which span the z-matrix of the second characteristic diagram. |
|  | Number of contour lines | Specifies the number of the contour lines to be drawn in the Isolines display mode. Every contour line must have a channel pair that uses the channels which follow the first channel pair. |
|  | Position freely / Bound to channel | Specifies whether you can freely select the coordinate, or whether it is bound to a channel in the Coordinate display mode. |
|  | X | Specifies the x-value of the coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. If you select the Position freely setting for the position of the coordinate, this value specifies the actual value of the coordinate. If you select the Bound to channel setting for the position of the coordinate, this value only specifies an approximate value. DIAdem searches for the closest possible value that best meets the condition that you have given in the Position setting. |
|  | Y | Specifies the y-value of the coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. If you select the Position freely setting for the position of the coordinate, this value specifies the actual value of the coordinate. If you select the Bound to channel setting for the position of the coordinate, this value only specifies an approximate value. DIAdem searches for the closest possible value that best meets the condition that you have given in the Position setting. |
|  | Z | Specifies the z-value of the coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. If you select the Position freely setting for the position of the coordinate, this value specifies the actual value of the coordinate. If you select the Bound to channel setting for the position of the coordinate, this value only specifies an approximate value. DIAdem searches for the closest possible value that best meets the condition that you have given in the Position setting. |
|  | Position | Specifies how DIAdem determines the position of a channel-bound coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. |
|  | Legend | Specifies whether DIAdem displays a legend. |
|  | Legend: Settings | Opens the dialog box where you specify the legend. |
|  | Color legend | Specifies whether DIAdem displays a color legend. |
|  | Color legend: Settings | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color legend. |
|  | Data Check | Opens the dialog box where you specify the settings for the partial load structure in the Characteristic Diagram display type. |

#### Further Settings

Curve List | [Axis System](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_dialog.htm) | [Planes](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_plane_dialog.htm) | [Planes » Isometry](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_iso_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Scaling](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_scale_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Numbers](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_value_dialog.htm) |[Axis Parameters » Labels](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_position_dialog.htm)

|  | Note You can enter different Channel types in the channel lists.If an x-channel or a y-channel is a text channel, DIAdem plots the other channels against the index and uses the texts of the text channel to label the axes. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00522: 3D Axis Definition: Axis Parameters » Labels

- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Axis Parameters](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisparameters_general.htm) > 3D Axis Definition: Axis Parameters » Labels

3D Axis Definition: Axis Parameters » Labels

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the axis labels in the selected 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [AxisLabel](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepaxislabelint.htm) object.

|  | Text | Specifies the axis text. For example, the text @@ChnName(CurrChnNo)@@ [@@chndim(CurrChnNo)@@] returns the channel name and the channel unit of the current channel. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Text Input Tool | Opens the dialog box where you enter text that includes DIAdem variables and formulas. |
|  | Font | Specifies the font for the axis text. |
|  | Font size | Specifies the font size of the axis text. |
|  | Font color | Specifies the color of the axis text. |
|  | Highlighting color | Specifies the color in which you highlight the axis text. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
|  | Angle automatic | Specifies whether DIAdem specifies the label angle of the X-axis, the Y-axis or the Z-axisautomatically. |
|  | Angle | Specifies the angle of the axis labels. |
|  | Distance1 | Specifies the position of the axis labels in relation to the selected axis. |
|  | Distance2 | Specifies the relative distance from the axis label to the selected axis. |
|  | Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the axis text. |
|  | Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the axis text. |
|  | Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the axis text. |
|  | Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the axis labels. |
|  | Frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames each axis text individually. |

|  | Note You can include subscript and superscript in text, format numbers, include variable contents, or use scripts for complex formats. Refer to the page on Formatting Text for more information. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00523: Add Curve

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_newcurve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_newcurve_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Add Curve

Add Curve

Use this dialog box to generate or to delete curves in 3D axis systems or to modify the display.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DCurve](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepd3curveint.htm) object.

| Type | Specifies the display mode. Depending on the display mode, you specify different channels and structures. |
| --- | --- |
| X-channel | Specifies the channel containing the x-values of the curve.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the x-channel to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers. |
| Y-channel | Specifies the data channel that contains the y-values of the curve.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the y-channel to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers. |
| Z-channel | Specifies the data channel containing the z-values of the curve.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the z-channel to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers.A triplet consists of three data channels of the same length, which contain the x, y, or z-values. Refer to the DIAdem Help page Organizing 3D Data as Value Triplets and as Matrices for further information about organizing 3D data. |
| Z-matrix | Specifies which data channels span the z-matrix.In the Coordinate display mode, specifies the z-channels to which the Position setting of a channel-bound coordinate refers.A matrix consists of one x-channel, one y-channel, and several z-channels. The number of z-channels corresponds with the length of the y-channel. The length of the z-channels corresponds with the length of the x-channel. The z-channels must be in consecutive order in the data area. The x-channel and the y-channel can be anywhere in the data area. Refer to the DIAdem Help page Organizing 3D Data as Value Triplets and as Matrices for further information about organizing 3D data. |
| 1st channel starting points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the data channel with the values of the first coordinate of the start of the vector. |
| 2nd channel starting points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the data channel with the values of the second coordinate of the start of the vector. |
| 3rd channel starting points | In the Vector display mode, specifies the data channel with the values of the third coordinate of the start of the vector. |
| 1st channel end point | In the Vector display mode, specifies the data channel with the values of the first coordinate of the end of the vector. |
| 2nd channel end point | In the Vector display mode, specifies the data channel with the values of the second coordinate of the end of the vector. |
| 3rd channel end point | In the Vector display mode, specifies the data channel with the values of the third coordinate of the end of the vector. |
| 1st X-channel | Specifies for the Isolines display type the first data channel with the x-values of the first isoline. Each additional contour line needs an additional channel pair. |
| 1st Y-channel | Specifies for the Isolines display type the first data channel with the y-values of the first isoline. Each additional contour line needs an additional channel pair. |
| 1st Z-channel | Specifies for the Isolines display type the first data channel with the z-values of the first isoline. Each additional contour line needs an additional channel pair. |
| 1st Z-matrix | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the data channels which span the z-matrix of the first characteristic diagram. |
| 2nd X-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the data channel with the x-values of the second characteristic diagram. |
| 2nd Y-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the data channel with the y-values of the second characteristic diagram. |
| 2nd Z-channel | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the data channel with the z-values of the second characteristic diagram. |
| 2nd Z-matrix | Specifies for the Characteristic diagram display type the data channels which span the z-matrix of the second characteristic diagram. |
| Triplet/Matrix | Specifies for the display modes Surface, Spikes, Points, Characteristic diagram, and Coordinate whether the data is in triplet or matrix form. Depending on the display type, you specify the various properties: Triplet / Matrix for Surface, Triplet / Matrix for Spikes, Triplet / Matrix for Points, Triplet / Matrix for Characteristic diagram, and Triplet / Matrix for Coordinate.A triplet consists of three data channels of the same length, which contain the x, y, or z-values. A matrix consists of one x-channel, one y-channel, and several z-channels. The number of z-channels corresponds with the length of the y-channel. The length of the z-channels corresponds with the length of the x-channel. The z-channels must be in consecutive order in the data area. The x-channel and the y-channel can be anywhere in the data area. Refer to the DIAdem Help page Organizing 3D Data as Value Triplets and as Matrices for further information about organizing 3D data. |
| Characteristic diagram type | Specifies whether DIAdem displays a simple or a differential characteristic diagram for the Characteristic diagram display mode. |
| Isoline type | Specifies the plane in which DIAdem displays the contour lines in the Isolines display mode. |
| Number | Specifies the number of the contour lines to be drawn in the Isolines display mode. Every contour line must have a channel pair that uses the channels which follow the first channel pair. |
| 4D vector/6D vector | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the vectors four-dimensionally or six-dimensionally in the Vector display mode. |
| Plane that contains vectors | Specifies the plane that contains the vectors in the Vector display mode. |
| Position freely / Bound to channel | Specifies whether you can freely select the coordinate, or whether it is bound to a channel in the Coordinate display mode. |
| Position | Specifies how DIAdem determines the position of a channel-bound coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. |
| X | Specifies the x-value of the coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. If you select the Position freely setting for the position of the coordinate, this value specifies the actual value of the coordinate. If you select the Bound to channel setting for the position of the coordinate, this value only specifies an approximate value. DIAdem searches for the closest possible value that best meets the condition that you have given in the Position setting. |
| Y | Specifies the y-value of the coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. If you select the Position freely setting for the position of the coordinate, this value specifies the actual value of the coordinate. If you select the Bound to channel setting for the position of the coordinate, this value only specifies an approximate value. DIAdem searches for the closest possible value that best meets the condition that you have given in the Position setting. |
| Z | Specifies the z-value of the coordinate for the Coordinate display mode. If you select the Position freely setting for the position of the coordinate, this value specifies the actual value of the coordinate. If you select the Bound to channel setting for the position of the coordinate, this value only specifies an approximate value. DIAdem searches for the closest possible value that best meets the condition that you have given in the Position setting. |
| Color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
| Color Palette | Opens the dialog box where you specify the color assignments for the line color Palette. |
| Curve parameters | Opens the dialog box for the display mode, where you can set more curve parameters. Possible display types are: Surface, Isolines, Waterfall, Bars, 2D matrix, Spikes, 3D curve, Vector, Points, Characteristic diagram, and Coordinate. |

#### Further Settings

Curve List | [Axis System](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_dialog.htm) | [Planes](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_plane_dialog.htm) | [Planes » Isometry](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_axis_iso_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Scaling](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_scale_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Numbers](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_value_dialog.htm) |[Axis Parameters » Labels](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_position_dialog.htm)

|  | Note Refer to the DIAdem Help page Organizing 3D Data as Value Triplets and as Matrices for further information about organizing 3D data. |
| --- | --- |

Color Legend: General

Use this dialog box to specify the color legend display in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [ColorLegend](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcolorlegendint.htm) object.

| Frame entire legend | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the legend. |
| --- | --- |
| Frame symbols | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the color legend symbols. |
| Frame color | Specifies the color of the frame. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the frame. |
| Background color | Specifies the background color for the color legend. Use the setting Filling Effects to plot color shading. |
| Legend symbols | Specifies how DIAdem displays the symbols in the color legend. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

General | [Color Labels](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

|  | Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the title. |
|  | Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the title. |

- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > [Color Legend](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Color Legend: Position

Color Legend: Position

Use this dialog box to specify the position of the color legend display in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionint.htm) object.

| Position freely / Bound to axis system | Specifies whether the color legend is bound to an axis system, or whether you can position it freely. When the legend is bound to an axis system, DIAdem also moves the legend when you move the axis system. |
| --- | --- |
| X | Specifies the x-coordinates of the legend reference point, for color legends. Specify x for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify x for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Y | Specifies the y-coordinates of the legend reference point, for color legends. Specify y for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify y for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Reference point | Specifies the legend point the coordinates refer to in color legends. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Color Labels](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | Position

## TOPIC 00528: Color Legend: Size

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_size_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_size_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > [Color Legend](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Color Legend: Size

Color Legend: Size

Use this dialog box to specify the size of the color legend in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcolorlegendsettingsint.htm) and [ColorLegendSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionint.htm) objects.

| Fixed legend size / Automatic legend size | Specifies whether the height and width refer to the entire color legend or only to single curve entries. If you select the setting Fixed legend size, the legend size is unrelated to the number of legend entries. If you select the setting Automatic legend size, DIAdem adapts the legend size to the number of legend entries. |
| --- | --- |
| Height of entire legend in % | Specifies the height of the entire legend if you select Fixed legend size. |
| Height of entry in % | Specifies the height of a curve entry in the legend if you select Automatic legend size. |
| Width of entire legend in %. | Specifies the width of the entire legend if you select Fixed legend size. |
| Width of entry in % | Specifies the width of a curve entry in the legend if you select Automatic legend size. |
| Distance between rectangles (as % of rectangle diagonals) | Specifies the distance between the colored rectangles, as a percentage of the rectangle diagonals, for the color legend, in the Rectangle display mode. |
| Orientation | Specifies how DIAdem aligns the components of the color legend. |
| Portion of color field (as a % | Specifies the size for the color fields of the color legend as a percentage of the entire legend size. |
| Angle | Specifies the angle at which the color legend is displayed. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

|  | Note DIAdem ignores the setting Automatic legend size if the setting Orientation has the value Automatic. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Color Labels](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | Size | [Position](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_colorlegend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00530: Legend: General

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Legend: General

Legend: General

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the legend in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [CurveLegend](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendint.htm) object.

| Frame entire legend | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the legend. |
| --- | --- |
| Separators between legend columns | Specifies whether DIAdem displays separators in the legend. |
| Frame symbols | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the legend symbols. |
| Frame color | Specifies the color of the frame. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the frame. |
| Background color | Specifies the background color for the legend. Use the setting Filling Effects to plot color shading. |
| Legend only for first expanding curve | In the name-oriented mode, this setting specifies whether DIAdem only displays the legend for the first curve if several channels have the same name. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

General | [Labels](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00531: Legend: Position

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/3daxissystems_general.htm) > [3D Axis Definition](../graph_dlg_3d_curve/d3axis_axisdefinition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_3d_tab/d3axis_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > [Legend](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Position

Legend: Position

Use this dialog box to specify the size and position of the legend in a 3D axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionint.htm) object.

| Position freely / Bound to axis system | Specifies whether the legend is bound to an axis system, or whether you can position it freely. When the legend is bound to an axis system, DIAdem also moves the legend when you move the axis system. |
| --- | --- |
| X | Specifies the x-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify x for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify x for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Y | Specifies the y-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify y for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify y for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Reference point | Specifies the legend point the coordinates refer to. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm)| [Size](../graph_dlg_3dlegend_tab/d3axis_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | Position

## TOPIC 00534: 3D Table Definition: Contents

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dtable_tab/d3table_tab_oview_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_3dtable_tab/d3table_tab_oview_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [3D Tables](../graph_dlg_3dtable_tab/d3table_tab_general.htm) > 3D Table Definition: Contents

3D Table Definition: Contents

Use this dialog box to create or to delete columns in 3D tables, or to modify the table display.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [3DTableXValues](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireptable3dxvaluesint.htm), [3DTableYValues](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireptable3dyvaluesint.htm) and [3DTableZValues](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireptable3dzvaluesint.htm) objects.

| X-channel | Specifies the data channel whose contents DIAdem displays as x-values in the table. |
| --- | --- |
| Y-channel | Specifies the data channel of which DIAdem displays the contents as y-values in the table. |
| 1. Z-channel | Specifies the first data channel of which DIAdem displays the contents as z-values in the table. |
| Autoscaling | Specifies whether DIAdem scales the X-values, the Y-values or the automatically. |
| Begin | Specifies the first row of the x-data channel or the y-data channel which DIAdem displays in the table. |
| End | Specifies the first row of the x-data channel or the y-data channel which DIAdem displays in the table. |
| Interval | Specifies the step width between two consecutive values of the x-data channel or they-data channel. |

#### Further Settings

Contents | [Display](../graph_dlg_3dtable_tab/d3table_tab_disp_dialog.htm) | [Values](../graph_dlg_3dtable_tab/d3table_tab_values_dialog.htm) | [Headings](../graph_dlg_3dtable_tab/d3table_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_3dtable_tab/d3table_tab_pos_dialog.htm)

|  | Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the table entries. |

- bundle_id: `diadem`

Comment: Frame

Use this dialog box to specify the frame display.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [ArrowElement](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcomformulasubarrowint.htm) object.

| Frame inside the comment line / Frame centered on the comment line | Specifies whether DIAdem draws the frame inside the comment line or centered on the comment line. If you use several frames in your report and the frames touch and use the same line style, draw the frames centered so that no frame is displayed double. If several frames use different line styles and they touch, draw the frame inside so that the various lines do not overlap. |
| --- | --- |
| Specify individual line styles | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the frames in different colors, line styles, and line widths. Click the preview to select the frame line to configure. |
| Line color | Specifies the color of the frame. Use the Color for BorderLine property to specify the line color for the individual line style, otherwise use the Color for FrameLine property. |
| Line style | Specifies the line style of the frame. Use the LineType for BorderLine property to specify the line style for the individual line style, otherwise use the LineType for FrameLine property. |
| Line width | Specifies the width of the frame. Use the Width for BorderLine property to specify the line width for the individual line style, otherwise use the Width for FrameLine property. |
| Background color | Specifies the background color for the text. Use the setting Filling Effects to plot color shading. |
| Distance of text to comment edge | Specifies the distance of the text from the comment edge as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |

#### Further Settings

## TOPIC 00544: Layout Parameters: Events

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutevents_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutevents_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [DIAdem REPORT Settings](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgconfgraph_dialog.htm) > [Layout Parameters](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgarea_dialog.htm) > Layout Parameters: Events

Layout Parameters: Events

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem reacts to an event.

An event occurs as soon as a specific action is executed in DIAdem. Refreshing a worksheet, refreshing a report, or transforming a curve in a 2D axis system of DIAdem REPORT can be an event. If an event occurs, you can call commands which you can use to manipulate data.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties of the [Events](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepreporteventsint.htm) object.

| Before refresh | Specifies which user commands DIAdem executes before it updates a report. You must first register the commands in the user commands dialog box. |
| --- | --- |
| After refresh | Specifies which user commands DIAdem executes after it updates a report. You must first register the commands in the user commands dialog box. |

|  | Note To open this dialog box in the DIAdem REPORT panel, select Settings»Layout Setup»Layout Parameters»Events. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

[Worksheet](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgarea_dialog.htm) | [Display (Layout)](../graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutdisplay_dialog.htm) | [Display (Master Layout)](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgmlayoutdisplay_dialog.htm) | Events | [Custom Properties](../graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutproperties_dialog.htm) | [Master Layout](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgmasterlayout_dialog.htm)
