## TOPIC 00545: Layout Parameters: Custom Properties

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutproperties_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutproperties_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [DIAdem REPORT Settings](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgconfgraph_dialog.htm) > [Layout Parameters](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgarea_dialog.htm) > Layout Parameters: Custom Properties

Layout Parameters: Custom Properties

Use this dialog box to specify the custom properties of a DIAdem REPORT layout. If you export the layout as an Office file in XML format, or as a PDF-, JPEG-, PNG- or TIFF-file, DIAdem saves these properties as meta properties in the document. Use the [Document <Data>](../../filetagging/objects/diacmpnt_objects_idiademdocument.htm) object to access the meta properties in exported documents.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [Export](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepsettingsexportint.htm) object.

|  | New Entry | Adds a new custom property to the end of the list. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes a custom property. |
|  | Name | Specifies the name of the custom property. If you use the same name in the layout and the associated master layout, DIAdem saves the properties of the layout as meta properties in the exported document instead of the properties of the master layout. |
|  | Value | Specifies the value of the custom property. The value can also be a DIAdem expression. |
|  | Text Input Tool | Opens the dialog box where you enter text that includes DIAdem variables and formulas. |
|  | Preview | Displays the evaluated DIAdem expression of the custom property. If you export the layout, DIAdem saves the evaluated expression as a meta property in the exported document. |
|  | Type | Specifies the type of custom property.You cannot specify the type for the following names of custom properties: The type for the property names name, title, description, and author must be String, and the type for the property name datetime must be Time. If you assign the incorrect type to a property name, an error occurs when you export the documents. |

|  | Note To open this dialog box in DIAdem REPORT, select Settings»Layout Setup»Layout Parameters»Custom Properties. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

[Worksheet](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgarea_dialog.htm) | [Display (Layout)](../graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutdisplay_dialog.htm) | [Display (Master Layout)](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgmlayoutdisplay_dialog.htm) | [Events](../graph_dlg_menu/dlglayoutevents_dialog.htm) | Custom Properties | [Master Layout](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgmasterlayout_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00547: Manage Worksheets

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlgreportsheets_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlgreportsheets_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Load, Save, Export, and Manage](../graph_dlg_menu/reportopensave_overview.htm) > Manage Worksheets

Manage Worksheets

Use this dialog box to manage worksheets. You can create new worksheets, and copy, move, and delete existing worksheets. Double-click on the right side of the last tab in DIAdem REPORT to create a new worksheet.

Click in a row to select a worksheet. At the same time press the shift or Ctrl key to select several worksheets.

#### Settings

|  | Add New Worksheet to the End | Adds a new worksheet to the end of the list. In DIAdem, the new worksheet is now the current worksheet. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Insert New Worksheet | Inserts a new worksheet after the selected worksheet. In DIAdem, the new worksheet is now the current worksheet. |
|  | Copy Worksheet | Copies the selected worksheets and inserts the respective copy after the template into the list. The first copied worksheet is now the current worksheet. |
|  | Delete Worksheet | Deletes the selected worksheets. |
|  | Move Worksheet Up | Moves the selected worksheets one position up. You also can select one or more rows and move them with the mouse. |
|  | Move Worksheet Down | Moves the selected worksheets one position down. You also can select one or more rows and move them with the mouse. |
|  | Print All Worksheets | Specifies that DIAdem prints and exports all worksheets. |
|  | Print No Worksheet | Specifies that DIAdem does not print and export any worksheets. |
|  | Filter Enabled | Filters the displayed worksheets. DIAdem only displays those worksheets in the list whose names contain the entered text.Note The filter does not use wildcards but searches for * and ? in the name just like it does for any other character. |
|  | Note The filter does not use wildcards but searches for * and ? in the name just like it does for any other character. |  |
|  | Filter Disabled | DIAdem displays all worksheets in the list. |
| Settings of the individual worksheets |  |  |
|  | Index | Specifies the order of the worksheets. If you move, copy, or delete worksheets, DIAdem updates the index. |
|  | Worksheet Name | Specifies the name of a worksheet. You can change the name of a worksheet with a double-click on the row, or press <F2>. |
|  | Worksheet Enabled | Specifies the current worksheet in the DIAdem workspace. |
|  | Worksheet Disabled | Specifies that the worksheet in the workspace is not in the foreground. If you click the checkbox, the worksheet in this row becomes the current worksheet. |
|  | Print Worksheet | Specifies that DIAdem prints and exports the worksheet . Click the symbol to disable the print procedure. |
|  | Do Not Print Worksheet | Specifies that DIAdem does not print and export the worksheet. Click the symbol to enable the print procedure. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/report_layout_save_compatible.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00550: Save REPORT Layout As Compatible Version

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/report_layout_save_compatible.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/report_layout_save_compatible.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Load, Save, Export, and Manage](../graph_dlg_menu/reportopensave_overview.htm) > Save REPORT Layout As Compatible Version

Save REPORT Layout As Compatible Version

As of DIAdem 2019 SP1, DIAdem REPORT offers additional options in the settings of 2D axis systems that simplify the positioning of axis scales. If you use one of these new options, you can no longer load these layouts in DIAdem 2018 and earlier versions. Moreover, DIAdem 2019 may display the layout differently than DIAdem 2019 SP1.

The function group bar with the predefined 2D axis systems also contains the new options as of DIAdem 2019 SP1. You can change the default settings of the function groups using the context menu to create compatible layouts.

The following settings have been extended in DIAdem 2019 SP1:

- **Tick style** in [Axis Parameters » X-Scaling](../graph_dlg_2d_tab/d2axis_tab_xscale_dialog.htm) and [Axis Parameters » Y-Scaling](../graph_dlg_2d_tab/d2axis_tab_yscale_dialog.htm)
- **Position** in [Axis Parameters » X-Numbers](../graph_dlg_2d_tab/d2axis_tab_xvalue_dialog.htm) and [Axis Parameters » Y-Numbers](../graph_dlg_2d_tab/d2axis_tab_yvalue_dialog.htm)

To change an existing layout so that you can load it in earlier versions of DIAdem, open the layout in the current DIAdem version and run the following script. DIAdem may then display individual ticks or axis scales differently:

| VBScript | Python |
| --- | --- |

[Copy script](javascript:void(0);)

```text
Dim oSheet, oObject, oYAxis
' Loop over all layout pages
For Each oSheet in Report.Sheets
  ' Loop over all objects of a layout page
  For Each oObject in oSheet.Objects
    If (oObject.ObjectType = eReportObject2DAxisSystem) then 
      ' Only for 2D axis systems
      If ((oObject.XAxis.TickDisplay.Type = e2DAxisXTickInside) or (oObject.XAxis.TickDisplay.Type = e2DAxisXTickOutside)) then
        ' X-axis: If ticks are "Inside" or "Outside", change to "Bottom"
        oObject.XAxis.TickDisplay.Type = e2DAxisXTickBottom1
      End If  
      If (oObject.XAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition = eRelativePositionNumericLabelAutomatic) then
        ' X-axis: If the label position is "Automatic", change to "Bottom"
        oObject.XAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition = eRelativePositionNumericLabelBottom
      End If  
      ' Loop over all y-axes of a 2D axis system
      For Each oYAxis in oObject.YAxisList
        If ((oYAxis.TickDisplay.Type = e2DAxisXTickInside) or (oYAxis.TickDisplay.Type = e2DAxisXTickOutside)) then
          ' Y-axis: If ticks are "Inside" or "Outside", change to "Left"
          oYAxis.TickDisplay.Type = e2DAxisYTickLeft
        End If
        If (oYAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition = eRelativePositionNumericLabelAutomatic) then
          ' Y-axis: If the label position is "Automatic", change to "Left"
          oYAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition = eRelativePositionNumericLabelLeft
        End If  
      Next
    End If
  Next
Next
```

[Copy script](javascript:void(0);)

```text
# Loop over all layout pages
for oSheet in dd.Report.Sheets: 
# Loop over all objects of a layout page
    for oObject in oSheet.Objects: 
        if (oObject.ObjectType == dd.eReportObject2DAxisSystem) : 
# Only for 2D axis systems
            if ((oObject.XAxis.TickDisplay.Type == dd.e2DAxisXTickInside) or (oObject.XAxis.TickDisplay.Type = dd.e2DAxisXTickOutside)) : 
# X-axis: If ticks are "Inside" or "Outside", change to "Bottom"
                oObject.XAxis.TickDisplay.Type = e2DAxisXTickBottom1 
            if (oObject.XAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition == dd.eRelativePositionNumericLabelAutomatic) : 
# X-axis: If the label position is "Automatic", change to "Bottom"
                oObject.XAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition = dd.eRelativePositionNumericLabelBottom 
# Loop over all y-axes of a 2D axis system
            for oYAxis in oObject.YAxisList: 
                if ((oYAxis.TickDisplay.Type == dd.e2DAxisXTickInside) or (oYAxis.TickDisplay.Type = dd.e2DAxisXTickOutside)) : 
# Y-axis: If ticks are "Inside" or "Outside", change to "Left"
                    oYAxis.TickDisplay.Type = dd.e2DAxisYTickLeft 
                if (oYAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition == dd.eRelativePositionNumericLabelAutomatic) : 
# Y-axis: If the label position is "Automatic", change to "Left"
                    oYAxis.Numbers.RelativePosition = dd.eRelativePositionNumericLabelLeft 
```

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/report_layout_save_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00551: Save REPORT Layout As

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/report_layout_save_dialog.htm`

- source_language: `enus`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Load, Save, Export, and Manage](../graph_dlg_menu/reportopensave_overview.htm) > Save REPORT Layout As

Save REPORT Layout As

Use this dialog box to save a REPORT layout.

#### Settings

| Filename | Specifies the name of the file that DIAdem is to save. |
| --- | --- |
| File type | Specifies which type of file DIAdem is to save. |

Select **Settings»DIAdem Settings»Select Path** to predefine the paths from which DIAdem loads files or to which DIAdem saves files. As soon as you load a file from a different path into a load dialog box or save a file to a different path in a save dialog box, DIAdem changes the respective user paths. The default setting that DIAdem uses when the program launches remains unchanged.

#### Script Call

[SaveLayout for Report](../../reportapi/methods/report_method_savelayout_irepreportint.htm)

## TOPIC 00554: PDF Export

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/report_pdf_save_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/report_pdf_save_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Load, Save, Export, and Manage](../graph_dlg_menu/reportopensave_overview.htm) > [Export](../graph_dlg_menu/report_export.htm) > PDF Export

PDF Export

Use PDF export to save your report as a Portable Document Format file. DIAdem generates a PDF file with the same number of pages as there are sheets in your report. If you do not select pages as printable in the [Manage Worksheets](../graph_dlg_menu/dlgreportsheets_dialog.htm) dialog box, DIAdem does not export these pages to the PDF file. If you select an existing PDF file you want to save, you can attach these pages to the existing file.

The **PDF Export** function is available only in DIAdem REPORT. If you want to use the **DIAdem PDF Export** printer in other DIAdem panels, select this printer in the printer dialog box through **Printer**.

You can sign a PDF file after exporting to secure your copyrights and to meet the increased security standards. Click here for further information about signing PDFs.

#### Settings

| Filename | Specifies the name of the file DIAdem saves. |
| --- | --- |
| File type | Specifies which type of file DIAdem saves. |

Select **Settings»DIAdem Settings»Select Path** to predefine the paths from which DIAdem loads files or to which DIAdem saves files. When you load a file from another path into a load dialog box or save a file to another path in a save dialog box, DIAdem changes the respective user paths. The default setting that DIAdem uses when the program launches remains unchanged.

|  | Note You can use the DIAdem PDF Export printer in DIAdem only. The printer is installed automatically when DIAdem starts.If you delete the DIAdem PDF Export printer, start DIAdemStart.Exe on the DIAdem program path as Administrator in order to reconfigure the printer. |
| --- | --- |

#### Script Call

[ExportToPDF for Sheets](../../reportapi/methods/report_method_exporttopdf_irepsheetlistint.htm)

#### Examples

[Automatically Creating a PowerPoint Presentation](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_layout_to_powerpoint.htm) | [Crash Evaluation Based on the MME Standard](../../exploff/examples/exp_analysis_ab_1.htm) | [Customized User Interface](../../exploff/examples/example_application.htm) | [Printing Reports Automatically as PDF](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av19.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Extended Table](../../exploff/examples/expl_weather_info.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/reportreplacetext_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00557: Find and Replace Text

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/reportreplacetext_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/reportreplacetext_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Load, Save, Export, and Manage](../graph_dlg_menu/reportopensave_overview.htm) > Find and Replace Text

Find and Replace Text

Use this dialog box to find and replace text in a REPORT layout. If you modify a search condition or the replacement text, click **Search** again before you can replace the search text. If you double-click an object in the list, DIAdem displays this object in the report. This helps you check that you have selected the text you need.

#### Settings

|  | Find | Specifies the text you want to search for. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | REPORT object | Defines the type of REPORT objects in which DIAdem searches for the text. |
|  | Replace with | Specifies the replacement text. |
|  | Match case | Specifies whether the search is case-sensitive. |
|  | Match whole words | Specifies whether DIAdem only searches for whole words and not parts of words. |
|  | All worksheets/Current worksheets/Selected objects | Specifies whether DIAdem searches all worksheets, the current worksheets, or only the selected objects. |
|  | Labels | Specifies whether DIAdem searches only in free text and axis labels. |
|  | Channel names | Specifies whether DIAdem searches only in the channel names of the curve definitions. |
|  | Expressions only | Specifies whether DIAdem searches only in DIAdem expressions that contain the @@ characters. |
|  | Select All/Select Individuals | Selects all found objects when you enable “Select All” in the table heading, or selects only some of the found objects for replacement. |
|  | Worksheet | Displays the name of the worksheet. |
|  | Subobject | Displays the subobject type. |
|  | Found Text | Displays the found text. |
|  | Preview | Displays the found text with the replacement. |
|  | Find | Searches for all search text locations in the current layout. |
|  | Replace | Replaces the search text with the replacement text in all selected search locations. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00558: Legend: General

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > Legend: General

Legend: General

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the legend in a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendFrame](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendframeint.htm) and [CurveLegendSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendsettingsint.htm) objects.

| Extended legend settings | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically specifies the best possible display for the legend or whether you can edit all legend settings. For pie charts DIAdem only supports the extended legend setting. Therefore, you cannot disable the setting for this chart type. |
| --- | --- |
| Frame entire legend | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the legend. |
| Separators between legend columns | Specifies whether DIAdem displays separators in the legend. |
| Frame color | Specifies the color of the frame. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the frame. |
| Background color | Specifies the background color for the legend. Use the setting Filling effects to define color shading. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

General | [Labels](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Pie Charts](../../exploff/examples/expl_pie_chart.htm)

## TOPIC 00559: Legend: Title Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm

- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > [Legend: General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Title Parameters

Legend: Title Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the legend title in a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [CurveLegendHeader](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendheaderint.htm) object.

| Text field size as % | Specifies the size of the field for the legend title as a percentage of the page size. |
| --- | --- |
| Text field boundary | Specifies whether a line separates the text field from the symbol section. |
| Text field position | Specifies the relative position of the text field within the legend. |
| Label angle | Specifies the label angle. |
| Font | Specifies the font for the title. |
| Font size automatic | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically adjusts the font size of the title to the space available. If you do not select the property, DIAdem specifies the font size automatically. |
| Font size | Specifies the font size for the title. |
| Font color | Specifies the color for the title. |
| Highlighting color | Specifies the color with which you highlight the title. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
| Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the title. |
| Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the title. |
| Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the title. |
| Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the title. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | Title Parameters | [Size](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00560: Legend: Labels

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > [Legend: General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Labels

Legend: Labels

Use this dialog box to specify the label text for the legend in a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [CurveLegendColumn](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendcontentcolumnint.htm) object.

|  | Enable Display for All Curves | Selects all legend displays. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Disable Display for All Curves | Deselects all the legend displays. |
|  | New Entry | Adds a new legend column. |
|  | Text Input Tool | Opens the dialog box where you enter text that includes DIAdem variables and formulas. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected legend column. |
|  | Move Entry to the Left | Moves the selected legend column to the left. |
|  | Move Entry to the Right | Moves the selected legend column to the right. |
|  | No. | Displays an incrementing number for the curve. |
|  | Type | Displays the type of curve. |
|  | Color | Displays the color of the curve. |
|  | Display | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the legend for the selected curve. Select Enable Display for All Curves or Disable Display for All Curves to show or hide the legends for all curves. |
|  | Legend Column | Specifies the Title, the Relative Width, and the Mode for each legend column. |
|  | Title | Specifies the text of the general label of the legend. |
|  | Relative Width | Specifies the relative width of the individual legend texts. |
|  | Mode | Specifies whether DIAdem labels the legend of the pie chart with user defined text or with default text. If you select Free text, you only can enter text in the first line. Use the Text property to specify texts in the script. If you select Slice-related text, you can enter an individual text for each slice. In the script you use the Name property to specify slice related text. |
|  | Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | Labels | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Pie Charts](../../exploff/examples/expl_pie_chart.htm)

## TOPIC 00561: Legend: Position

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > [Legend: General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Position

Legend: Position

Use this dialog box to specify the position of the legend in a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPositionAnchor](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionanchorint.htm) object.

| Position freely / Bound to axis system | Specifies whether the legend is bound to an axis system, or whether you can position it freely. When the legend is bound to an axis system, DIAdem also moves the legend when you move the axis system. |
| --- | --- |
| X | Specifies the x-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify x for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify x for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Y | Specifies the y-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify y for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify y for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Reference point | Specifies the legend point the coordinates refer to. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm)| [Size](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | Position

#### Examples

[Pie Charts](../../exploff/examples/expl_pie_chart.htm)

## TOPIC 00562: Legend: Size

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > [Legend: General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Size

Legend: Size

Use this dialog box to specify the size of the legend in a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionint.htm) and [CurveLegendSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendsettingsint.htm) objects.

| Fixed legend size / Automatic legend size | Specifies whether the height and width refer to the entire color legend or only to single curve entries. If you select the setting Fixed legend size, the legend size is unrelated to the number of legend entries. If you select the setting Automatic legend size, DIAdem adapts the legend size to the number of legend entries. |
| --- | --- |
| Height of entire legend in % | Specifies the height of the entire legend if you select Fixed legend size. |
| Height of entry in % | Specifies the height of a curve entry in the legend if you select Automatic legend size. |
| Width of entire legend in %. | Specifies the width of the entire legend if you select Fixed legend size. |
| Width of entry in % | Specifies the width of a curve entry in the legend if you select Automatic legend size. |
| Orientation | Specifies how DIAdem aligns the elements. |
| Portion of symbol field | Specifies the size of the color field as a percentage of the entire legend size. |
| Angle | Specifies the angle at which DIAdem displays the legend. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

|  | Note DIAdem ignores the setting Automatic legend size if the setting Orientation has the value Automatic. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | Size | [Position](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Pie Charts](../../exploff/examples/expl_pie_chart.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00563: Legend: Text Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > [Legend: General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Text Parameters

Legend: Text Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the legend labels display in a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [CurveLegendSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendsettingsint.htm) object.

| Font | Specifies the font for the legend labels. |
| --- | --- |
| Font size automatic | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically adjusts the font size of the legend labels to the space available. If you do not select the property, DIAdem specifies the font size automatically. |
| Font size | Specifies the font size for the legend labels. |
| Font color | Specifies the color of the legend labels. If you select Same Color as Curve, DIAdem adjusts the label colors to the curve colors. |
| Highlighting color | Specifies the color with which you highlight the legend labels. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
| Text position | Specifies the position of the labels in relation to the symbols. |
| Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the legend labels. |
| Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the legend labels. |
| Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the legend labels. |
| Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the legend labels. |
| Truncate text | Specifies whether DIAdem truncates the legend label at the edge of the legend column. |
| Word wrap | Specifies whether DIAdem wraps the legend label at the edge of the legend column. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting appears only if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | Text Parameters | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_piechart_legend_tab/piechart_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Pie Charts](../../exploff/examples/expl_pie_chart.htm)

## TOPIC 00565: Pie Chart Definition: Data Channel

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_curve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_curve_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > Pie Chart Definition: Data Channel

Pie Chart Definition: Data Channel

Use this dialog box to specify the display of a pie chart. In pie charts or doughnut charts, you display individual values from a channel as a section of the whole pie or doughnut. DIAdem calculates the percentage of each channel value with respect to the sum of all channel values.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PieChart](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppiechartint.htm) object.

| Channel | Specifies the channel whose values DIAdem REPORT displays in a pie chart. |
| --- | --- |
| Slice label | Specifies whether DIAdem extracts the slice labels from a channel or whether you specify the slice labels manually. |
| Label channel | Specifies the channel from which DIAdem REPORT takes the labels for the slices. |
| No. | Specifies the serial number of the slice. |
| Labels | Specifies the manual entry of the slice. |
| Absolute Values | Specifies the absolute values of the channel displayed in the pie chart. DIAdem does not display negative values. |
| Percentage | Specifies the share of the channel value as a percentage of the channel total. |
| Filling color | Specifies the filling color of a slice. |
| Point Explosion | Specifies a slice displacement. |

Pie Chart Definition: Data Channel | [Pie Chart Definition: Display](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_display_dialog.htm) | [Pie Chart Definition: Labels](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_description_dialog.htm) | [Pie Chart Definition: Position](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Pie Charts](../../exploff/examples/expl_pie_chart.htm)

## TOPIC 00566: Pie Chart Definition: Labels

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_description_dialog.htm`

- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > [Data Channel](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Pie Chart Definition: Labels

Pie Chart Definition: Labels

Use this dialog box to specify the labels of a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PieChartSliceLabel](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppiechartslicelabelint.htm) object.

| Font | Specifies the font for the axis text. |
| --- | --- |
| Font size | Specifies the font size of the axis text. |
| Font color | Specifies the color of the axis text. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the font in the same color as the curve. |
| Highlighting color | Specifies the color in which you highlight the labels. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity.For user-defined colors, select the value eColorIndexOtherColors, and use the RGB property or the SetRGBColor method to select the color. |
| Alignment | Specifies the relative position of the slice labels in a pie chart in DIAdem REPORT. |
| Physical value | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays the physical values in the slice labels of a pie chart. |
| Format | Specifies the format in which DIAdem displays the physical value. |
| Relative value | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays the relative values in the slice labels of a pie chart. |
| Format | Specifies the format in which DIAdem REPORT displays the relative value. |
| Slice label | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays slice labels in a pie chart. |
| Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem REPORT displays axis texts in bold font. |
| Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem displays axis texts in italics. |
| Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the axis texts in underlined font. |
| Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the axis texts in strikethrough font. |

#### Further Settings

## TOPIC 00567: Pie Chart Definition: Display

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_display_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_display_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Pie Charts](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_general.htm) > [Data Channel](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Pie Chart Definition: Display

Pie Chart Definition: Display

Use this dialog box to specify the display of a pie chart.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PieChartSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppiechartsettingsint.htm) object.

| Display mode | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the pie chart as a filled pie or as a doughnut. |
| --- | --- |
| Show slice frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the slice. |
| Hole size [%] | Specifies the percentage the hole has of the total doughnut when the display mode setting is Doughnut. |
| Inclination angle [°] | Specifies the inclination angle of the pie chart. |
| Angle of the first slice [°] | Specifies the angle at which DIAdem displays the first slice. |
| Pie explosion [%] | Specifies that the slices are separated. |
| Aperture angle | Specifies the aperture angle of the pie slice in degrees. |

[Pie Chart Definition: Data Channel](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_curve_dialog.htm) | Pie Chart Definition: Display | [Pie Chart Definition: Labels](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_description_dialog.htm) | [Pie Chart Definition: Position](../graph_dlg_piechart_system_tab/piechart_tab_position_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00568: Legend: General

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Polar Definition](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Legend: General

Legend: General

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the legend in a polar axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendFrame](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendframeint.htm) and [CurveLegendSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendsettingsint.htm) objects.

| Extended legend settings | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically specifies the best possible display for the legend or whether you can edit all legend settings. For polar axis systems DIAdem only supports the extended legend setting. Therefore, you cannot disable the setting for this chart type. |
| --- | --- |
| Frame entire legend | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the legend. |
| Separators between legend columns | Specifies whether DIAdem displays separators in the legend. |
| Frame color | Specifies the color of the frame. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the frame. |
| Background color | Specifies the background color for the legend. Use the setting Filling effects to define color shading. |
| Legend only for first expanding curve | In the name-oriented mode with curve expansion, this setting specifies whether DIAdem only displays the legend for the first curve, if several channels have the same name. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

General | [Labels](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00570: Legend: Position

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Polar Definition](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > [Legend](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Position

Legend: Position

Use this dialog box to specify the position of the legend in a polar axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPositionAnchor](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionanchorint.htm) object.

| Position freely / Bound to axis system | Specifies whether the legend is bound to an axis system, or whether you can position it freely. When the legend is bound to an axis system, DIAdem also moves the legend when you move the axis system. |
| --- | --- |
| X | Specifies the x-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify x for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify x for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Y | Specifies the y-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify y for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify y for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Reference point | Specifies the legend point the coordinates refer to. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm)| [Size](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | Position

## TOPIC 00571: Legend: Size

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Polar Definition](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > [Legend](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Size

Legend: Size

Use this dialog box to specify the size of the legend in a polar axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionint.htm) and [CurveLegendSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendsettingsint.htm) objects.

| Fixed legend size / Automatic legend size | Specifies whether the height and width refer to the entire color legend or only to single curve entries. If you select the setting Fixed legend size, the legend size is unrelated to the number of legend entries. If you select the setting Automatic legend size, DIAdem adapts the legend size to the number of legend entries. |
| --- | --- |
| Height of entire legend in % | Specifies the height of the entire legend if you select Fixed legend size. |
| Height of entry in % | Specifies the height of a curve entry in the legend if you select Automatic legend size. |
| Width of entire legend in %. | Specifies the width of the entire legend if you select Fixed legend size. |
| Width of entry in % | Specifies the width of a curve entry in the legend if you select Automatic legend size. |
| Orientation | Specifies how DIAdem aligns the elements. |
| Portion of symbol field | Specifies the size of the color field as a percentage of the entire legend size. |
| Angle | Specifies the angle at which DIAdem displays the legend. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

|  | Note DIAdem ignores the setting Automatic legend size if the setting Orientation has the value Automatic. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | Size | [Position](../graph_dlg_polar_legend_tab/polar_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Displaying Curves in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_defining.htm) | [Specifying Circle Sectors in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_circle.htm)

#### Examples

[Different Display Modes in DIAdem REPORT](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av46.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Different Aperture Angles](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av22.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Different Aperture Angles](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av37.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Line and Markers and with Differential Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av23.htm)

## TOPIC 00572: Curve Parameters: Differential

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_diff_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_diff_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve Parameters](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_curveparameters_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: Differential

Curve Parameters: Differential

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays curves in polar axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PolarDifferentialDimension](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppolardifferentialspikeint.htm) object.

| Line color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
| --- | --- |
| Line style | Specifies the line style of the curve. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the curve. |
| Line interval | Specifies the interval and the length of the line sections for broken line display. |
| Width | Specifies the width of the upper and lower lines as a percentage of the minimum interval of the lines. If these lines are very close in the middle of the circle, this interval is very small. |
| Offset | Specifies the offset of the upper and lower lines. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Other Curve Displays

## TOPIC 00575: Curve Parameters: Line and Points » Markers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_linesym_marker_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_linesym_marker_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve Parameters](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_curveparameters_general.htm) > [Line and Points](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_linesymbols_general.htm) > Curve Parameters: Line and Points » Markers

Curve Parameters: Line and Points » Markers

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays curves in polar axis systems.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PolarAdditionalMarker](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppolarmarkeradditionalint.htm) object.

| Marker style | Specifies the symbol for the markers on the curve. |
| --- | --- |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the markers. |
| Size | Specifies the size of the markers. |
| Size from channel | Specifies the channel whose values DIAdem uses for the size of the markers. |
| Display from [%] | Specifies the minimum size from which DIAdem draws the marker. |
| Marker color | Specifies the color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the curve end labels the same color as the curve. |
| Filling color | Specifies the filling color of the markers. If you select Same Color as Curve, you specify that DIAdem displays the marker filling the same color as the curve. |
| Repeat marker | Specifies the frequency of the markers. |
| Every n points | Specifies that DIAdem only displays the markers at every nth point on the curve. |
| Every n percent | Specifies that DIAdem displays the markers at every n percent. First DIAdem specifies the distance that corresponds with the percentage value of the diagonal of the diagram area. DIAdem applies this distance along the curve and plots the labels at the next point. |
| Maximum n points | Specifies that DIAdem displays a maximum of n markers. |
| Also at curve begin | Specifies that DIAdem displays a marker at the beginning of the curve. |
| Also at curve end | Specifies that DIAdem displays a marker at the end of the curve. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_linesym_line_dialog.htm) | Markers | [Labels](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_linesym_text_dialog.htm) | [Text parameters](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_linesym_textpar_dialog.htm)

#### Other Curve Displays

[General](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_line_dialog.htm) | Line and points | [Spikes](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_spike_dialog.htm) | [Differential](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_par_diff_dialog.htm)

Curve Parameters: Line and Points » Labels

Use this dialog box to specify how DIAdem displays curves in polar axis systems.

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PolarPoints](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppolarpointsint.htm) object.

|  | At every n-th value | Specifies that DIAdem only displays the label at every n-th point on the curve. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Free text | Specifies whether the curve label contains free text. Free text includes symbols or texts that DIAdem displays at the curve points. |
|  | ... | Opens the dialog box where you enter text that includes DIAdem variables and formulas. |
|  | X-value | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the x-coordinates at the curve points. |
|  | Y-value | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the y-coordinates at the curve points. |
|  | Format | Specifies the format instructions of the y-coordinates. |
|  | Format Numbers | Opens the dialog box where you select or enter the format specification. |
|  | Value index | Specifies that DIAdem displays the point numbers at the curve points. |
|  |  |  |
|  | Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

Curve and Polar Definition: Position

Use this dialog box to specify the position and size of the polar axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [ObjectPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppositionint.htm) object.

| Distance from top edge | Specifies the distance from the top edge of the page, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| --- | --- |
| Distance from left edge | Specifies the distance from the left side of the page, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| Distance from right edge | Specifies the distance from the right edge of the page, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| Distance from bottom edge | Specifies the distance from the bottom edge of the page, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| Width | Specifies the width of the axis system, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. In scaled display you use the Width property to specify the width in cm or inches. |
| Height | Specifies the height of the axis system, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. In scaled display you use the Height property to specify the height in cm or inches. |

|  | Note To specify the unit, select Settings»DIAdem Settings»General. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00580: Curve and Polar Definition: Display

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_axis_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_axis_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Polar Definition](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_general.htm) > Curve and Polar Definition: Display

Curve and Polar Definition: Display

Use this dialog box to specify the polar axis system display.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PolarSectors](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppolarsectorsint.htm) and [PolarSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppolarsettingsint.htm) objects.

| Angle direction | Specifies the direction of the circle labeling. |
| --- | --- |
| Background Color | Specifies the background color of the polar axis system. |
|  |  |
| Circle partitions | Specifies whether the subsequent settings refer to the ticks, miniticks, sectors, or to the minisectors. |
| Color | Specifies the color for the circle partitions. |
| Line style | Specifies the line style of the circle partitions. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the circle partitions. |
| Line interval | Specifies the interval and the length of the line sections for broken line display. |
| Minitick style | For Minitick circle partitions, you can specify which side of the axis the miniticks are on, or display circles at the minitick positions. |
|  |  |
| Autoscaling | Specifies whether DIAdem scales the polar axes automatically. |
| Zero angle alignment | Specifies the direction angle for the beginning of the circle segment, in degrees. |
| Aperture angle | Specifies the aperture angle of the circle segment in degrees. |
| Labeling origin | Specifies the value where DIAdem starts labeling the circle segment. |
| Number of sectors | Specifies the number of circle sectors in the circle segment. |
| Number of minisectors | Specifies the number of divisions in the circle sector. |
| Start minisectors | Specifies the number of the circle on the radial axis at which DIAdem starts displaying the minisectors. |
| Hide center | Specifies whether DIAdem starts the sector display from the beginning of the radial axis or from the center point of the radial axis. The setting does not influence the scaling. DIAdem also plots data in the center. |

[Curve List](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_curve_dialog.htm) | Display| [Axis Parameters » Scaling](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xscale_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Numbers](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xvalue_dialog.htm) |[Axis Parameters » Labels](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xlabel_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Circle Numbers](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_yvalue_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_position_dialog.htm)

|  | Note If you select Predefine Setting from the context menu of a function group to open this dialog box, not all the settings are available. |
| --- | --- |

#### Procedures

[Displaying Curves in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_defining.htm) | [Specifying Circle Sectors in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_circle.htm)

#### Examples

[Different Display Modes in DIAdem REPORT](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av46.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Different Aperture Angles](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av22.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Different Aperture Angles](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av37.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Line and Markers and with Differential Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av23.htm)

## TOPIC 00581: Curve and Polar Definition: Curve List

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_curve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_curve_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Polar Definition](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_general.htm) > Curve and Polar Definition: Curve List

Curve and Polar Definition: Curve List

Use this dialog box to create, to delete, or to modify the display of curves in a polar axis system.

You can enter all [Channel types](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_channeltypes.htm) in the channel lists of the polar axis system. You always enter [xy-channels](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_channeltypes.htm) as y-channels, since DIAdem automatically completes the associated x-channel. If you enter [Waveform channels](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_waveforms.htm), you do not need to specify x-channels because waveform channels contain the x-part and the y-part of a curve. If you specify an x-channel, DIAdem plots the y-part of the waveform channel against this x-channel. If the channels are numeric channels and you do not specify a radius channel or an angle channel, DIAdem plots these channels against the index. If a radius channel is a text channel, DIAdem plots the other channel against the index and uses the texts of the text channel to label the axes.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PolarCurve](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppolarcurveint.htm) object.

|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you select channels for new curves. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Copy Entry | Copies the selected curve to the end of the list. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected curve. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected curve one position up. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected curve one position down. |
|  | No. | Displays the number of the curve. Click the number to select a curve. |
|  | Display curve | Specifies whether DIAdem plots the selected curve. |
|  | Type | Opens the dialog box where you specify the curve display mode and the curve parameters.Depending on the type of curve, the dialog box for Line, Line and points, Spikes, or Differential opens. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the curve.You specify different properties according to the display type: Line color, Differential curve color, or Spike color. Use the Type to specify the appearance. |
|  | Angle | Specifies the channel that contains the angles of the curve. Click in the entry field to select another angle. You do not need to specify the angle channel if the radius channel is a waveform channel or if the radius channel is an xy-channel and you have selected the When plotting xy-channels, automatically determine x-channel if not populated setting in the General DIAdem Settings. |
|  | Radius | Specifies the data channel that contains the distances of the curve points from the origin. Click in the entry field to select a different radius channel. |
|  | Radius 1 | Specifies the data channel that contains the distances of the second curve points from the origin, for the Differential display mode. Click in the entry field to select a different radius channel. |
|  | Legend | Specifies whether DIAdem displays a legend. |
|  | Legend: Settings | Opens the dialog box where you specify the legend. |

#### Further Settings

Curve List | [Display](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_axis_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Scaling](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xscale_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Numbers](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xvalue_dialog.htm) |[Axis Parameters » Labels](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xlabel_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Circle Numbers](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_yvalue_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_position_dialog.htm)

|  | Note If you select Predefine Setting from the context menu of a function group to open this dialog box, not all the settings are available. |
| --- | --- |

#### Procedures

[Displaying Curves in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_defining.htm) | [Specifying Circle Sectors in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_circle.htm)

#### Examples

[Different Display Modes in DIAdem REPORT](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av46.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Different Aperture Angles](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av22.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Different Aperture Angles](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av37.htm) | [Polar Axis System with Line and Markers and with Differential Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_av23.htm)

## TOPIC 00582: Add Curves

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_newcurve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_newcurve_dialog.htm

- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Polar Definition](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Add Curves

Add Curves

Use this dialog box to generate new curves in a polar axis system, and to define the curve display.

#### Settings

| Angle | Specifies the data channel that contains the angle values of the curve. |
| --- | --- |
| Radii | Specifies the data channel that contains the distances of the curve points from the origin. Select several data channels to generate several curves simultaneously. |
| Line color | Specifies the color of the curve. You specify different properties according to the display type: Line color, Differential curve color, or Spike color. Specify the exact appearance in the Display mode dropdown menu. |
| Display mode | Specifies the display mode of the curve. |
| Curve Parameters | Opens the dialog box where you specify the curve display mode and the curve parameters. Depending on the type of curve, the dialog box for Line, Line and points, Spikes, or Differential opens. |
| Assign color automatically | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically uses the next color in the list when you generate several curves simultaneously. You specify in the dialog box Settings»DIAdem Settings»Colors whether DIAdem uses user-defined colors or the default colors. |
| Assign line style automatically | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically uses the next line style in the list when you generate several curves simultaneously. |

#### Procedures

[Displaying Curves in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_defining.htm) | [Specifying Circle Sectors in Polar Axis Systems](../../procpresent/axis_systems/procpres_polar_circle.htm)

|  | Y-position | Specifies the distance of the axis text in horizontal direction. |

|  | Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the axis text. |
|  | Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the axis text. |
|  | Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the axis labels. |
|  | Frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames each axis text individually. |

## TOPIC 00584: Curve and Polar Definition: Axis Parameters »Scaling

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xscale_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_tab_xscale_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Polar Definition](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_general.htm) > [Axis Parameters](../graph_dlg_polarsystem_tab/polar_definition_axisparameters_general.htm) > Curve and Polar Definition: Axis Parameters »Scaling

Curve and Polar Definition: Axis Parameters »Scaling

Use this dialog box to specify the scaling for the radial axis in a polar axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [PolarAxisScaling](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppolaraxisscalingint.htm) and [AxisTickObject](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepaxistickint.htm) objects.

| Scaling type | Specifies the type of polar scaling. |
| --- | --- |
| Time Axis | Specifies how DIAdem displays the time axis when the Scaling type is Date/Time. If you selected Automatic for the time axis, DIAdem displays the time part of the waveform channels with a relative time axis and displays other time channels with an absolute time axis. |
| Autoscaling | Specifies whether DIAdem scales the radial axis automatically. |
| Begin | Specifies the lowest value on the radial axis. |
| End | Specifies the highest value on the radial axis. |
| Center | Specifies which value DIAdem starts labeling from. If you click the Display tab and select the Hide center checkbox, DIAdem displays the sectors starting from this value. |
| Tick interval | Specifies the distance of the grid circles around the center. |
| Tick channel | Specifies the tick channel from which DIAdem takes the tick positions. |
| Number of miniticks | Specifies the number of miniticks between the ticks. |

#### Further Settings

## TOPIC 00587: Legend: General

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Spider Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Category Definition](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_general.htm) > Legend: General

Legend: General

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the legend in a spider axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendFrame](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendframeint.htm) and [CurveLegendSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendsettingsint.htm) objects.

| Extended legend settings | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically specifies the best possible display for the legend or whether you can edit all legend settings. For spider axis systems DIAdem only supports the extended legend setting. Therefore, you cannot disable the setting for this chart type. |
| --- | --- |
| Frame entire legend | Specifies whether DIAdem frames the legend. |
| Separators between legend columns | Specifies whether DIAdem displays separators in the legend. |
| Frame color | Specifies the color of the frame. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the frame. |
| Background color | Specifies the background color for the legend. Use the setting Filling effects to define color shading. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

General | [Labels](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Spider Axis System as Radar and Spider Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_spider_1.htm) | [Spider Axis System with different Lines Types](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_spider_2.htm)

Legend: Title Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the display of the legend title in a spider axis system.

#### Settings

| Text field size as % | Specifies the size of the field for the legend title as a percentage of the page size. |
| --- | --- |
| Text field boundary | Specifies whether a line separates the text field from the symbol section. |
| Text field position | Specifies the relative position of the text field within the legend. |
| Label angle | Specifies the label angle. |
| Font | Specifies the font for the title. |
| Font size automatic | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically adjusts the font size of the title to the space available. If you do not select the property, DIAdem specifies the font size automatically. |
| Font size | Specifies the font size for the title. |
| Font color | Specifies the color for the title. |
| Highlighting color | Specifies the color with which you highlight the title. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
| Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the title. |
| Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the title. |
| Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the title. |
| Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the title. |
|  |  |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

## TOPIC 00589: Legend: Labels

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Spider Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Category Definition](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_general.htm) > [Legend](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Labels

Legend: Labels

Use this dialog box to specify the label text for the legend in a spider axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [CurveLegendColumn](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepcurvelegendcontentcolumnint.htm) object.

|  | Enable Display for All Curves | Selects all legend displays. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Disable Display for All Curves | Deselects all the legend displays. |
|  | New Entry | Adds a new legend column. |
|  | Text Input Tool | Opens the dialog box where you enter text that includes DIAdem variables and formulas. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected legend column. |
|  | Move Entry to the Left | Moves the selected legend column to the left. |
|  | Move Entry to the Right | Moves the selected legend column to the right. |
|  | No. | Displays an incrementing number for the curve. |
|  | Type | Displays the type of curve. |
|  | Color | Displays the color of the curve. |
|  | Display | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the legend for the selected curve. Select Enable Display for All Curves or Disable Display for All Curves to show or hide the legends for all curves. |
|  | Legend Column | Specifies the Title, the Relative Width, and the Mode for each legend column. |
|  | Title | Specifies the text of the general label of the legend. |
|  | Relative Width | Specifies the relative width of the individual legend texts. |
|  | Mode | Specifies whether DIAdem labels the legend of the spider axis system with user defined text or with default text. If you select Free text, you only can enter text in the first line. Use the Text property to specify texts in the script. If you select Curve-related text, you can enter an individual text for each curve. In the script you use the RelatedLegendText property to specify curve related text. |
|  | Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | Labels | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm) | [Size](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm)
