## TOPIC 00590: Legend: Position

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_position_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Spider Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Category Definition](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_general.htm) > [Legend](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) > Legend: Position

Legend: Position

Use this dialog box to specify the position of the legend in a spider axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [LegendPositionAnchor](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireplegendpositionanchorint.htm) object.

| Position freely / Bound to axis system | Specifies whether the legend is bound to an axis system, or whether you can position it freely. When the legend is bound to an axis system, DIAdem also moves the legend when you move the axis system. |
| --- | --- |
| X | Specifies the x-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify x for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify x for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedX property. Specify the x value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Y | Specifies the y-coordinate of the legend reference point. Specify y for the setting Position freely with the PageRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the worksheet. Specify y for the setting Bound to axis system with the SystemRelatedY property. Specify the y value as a percentage of the axis system. |
| Reference point | Specifies the legend point the coordinates refer to. |
| Curve List | Opens the dialog box where you create or delete the curves or change the display. This setting is only available if you open this dialog box as a main dialog box, not as a subdialog box. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_general_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Text Parameters](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_textparameter_dialog.htm) | [Title Parameters](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_header_dialog.htm)| [Size](../graph_dlg_spider_legend_tab/spider_legend_tab_size_dialog.htm) | Position

#### Examples

[Spider Axis System as Radar and Spider Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_spider_1.htm) | [Spider Axis System with different Lines Types](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_spider_2.htm)

|  |  |  |

## TOPIC 00598: Curve Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_curveparameters_general.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_curveparameters_general.htm

## TOPIC 00603: Spider Axis System: Position

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_position_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_position_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Spider Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Category Definition](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_general.htm) > Spider Axis System: Position

Spider Axis System: Position

Use this dialog box to specify the position and size of the spider axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [ObjectPosition](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_ireppositionint.htm) object.

| Distance from top edge | Specifies the distance from the top edge of the page, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| --- | --- |
| Distance from left edge | Specifies the distance from the left edge of the worksheet, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| Distance from right edge | Specifies the distance from the right edge of the page, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| Distance from bottom edge | Specifies the distance from the bottom edge of the page, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. |
| Width | Specifies the width of the axis system, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. In scaled display you use the Width property to specify the width in cm or inches. |
| Height | Specifies the height of the axis system, as a percentage of the worksheet, in centimeters or inches. In scaled display you use the Height property to specify the height in cm or inches. |

|  | Note To specify the unit, select Settings»DIAdem Settings»General. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

[Curve List](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_curve_dialog.htm) | [Display](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_axis_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Scaling](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_scale_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Numbers](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_value_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Labels](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Line](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_line_dialog.htm) | Position

#### Examples

- bundle_id: `diadem`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

Spider Axis Definition: Display

Use this dialog box to specify the display of a spider axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [SpiderSettings](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepspidersettingsint.htm) object.

| Angle direction | Specifies the direction of the spider axis label. |
| --- | --- |
| Display mode | Specifies whether DIAdem displays a spider axis system or a radar axis system. |
| Display frame | Specifies that DIAdem frames the spider axis system. |
| Color | Specifies the color of the frame. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the frame. |
| Background color | Specifies the background color of the frame. |
| Display grid | Specifies whether DIAdem connects the ticks between the axes with a grid. You can only enable this setting if the setting Individual category axes is enabled on the Axis Parameters tab. |
| Color | Specifies the color of the grid. |
| Line width | Specifies the width of the grid lines. |
| Show minitick grid | Specifies whether DIAdem displays grid lines at the miniticks. Specify the number of miniticks on the Axis Parameters tab in the Scaling area. You can only enable this setting if the setting Individual category axes is enabled on the Axis Parameters tab. |
| Color | Specifies the color of the minitick grid. |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the minitick grid. |

#### Further Settings

[Curve List](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_curve_dialog.htm) | Display | [Axis Parameters » Scaling](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_scale_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters » Numbers](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_value_dialog.htm) |[Axis Parameters » Labels](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_label_dialog.htm) | [Axis Parameters »Line](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_line_dialog.htm) | [Position](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_position_dialog.htm)

|  | Note If you select Predefine Setting from the context menu of a function group to open this dialog box, not all the settings are available. |

## TOPIC 00606: Add Curves

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_newcurve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_newcurve_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Spider Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Category Definition](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_general.htm) > [Curve List](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_curve_dialog.htm) > Add Curves

Add Curves

Use this dialog box to generate new curves in a spider axis system, and to define the curve display.

#### Settings

| Display mode | Specifies the display mode of the curve. |
| --- | --- |
| Curve Parameters | Opens the dialog box where you specify the curve display mode and the curve parameters. Depending on the selected curve type, the dialog box for Line or Line and points opens. |
| Channels | Specifies the data channel that contains the values. Select several data channels to generate several curves simultaneously. The spider axis system displays the data linewise so that the first line corresponds to the first category and the second line corresponds to the second category and so on. A spider axis system only displays numeric channels and a maximum of 250 values per channel. |
| Line color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
| Assign color automatically | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically uses the next color in the list when you generate several curves simultaneously. You specify in the dialog box Settings»DIAdem Settings»Colors whether DIAdem uses user-defined colors or the default colors. |
| Assign line style automatically | Specifies whether DIAdem automatically uses the next line style in the list when you generate several curves simultaneously. |

#### Examples

[Spider Axis System as Radar and Spider Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_spider_1.htm) | [Spider Axis System with different Lines Types](../../exploff/examples/expl_report_spider_2.htm)

| Tick style | Specifies the position of the scaling ticks on the axes. |

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgpresent/graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_tab_value_dialog.htm`

- content_type: ``

[DIAdem REPORT](../reportdlgs_overview.htm) > [Spider Axis Systems](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_curve_general.htm) > [Curve and Category Definition](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_general.htm) > [Axis Parameters](../graph_dlg_spidersystem_tab/spider_definition_axisparameters_general.htm) > Spider Axis Definition: Axis Parameter » Numbers

Spider Axis Definition: Axis Parameter » Numbers

Use this dialog box to specify the font attributes for the axis scale for the category axes in a spider axis system.

#### Settings

The following settings are in the object-oriented script interface for DIAdem REPORT in the properties and methods of the [SpiderAxis](../../reportapi/objects/report_objects_irepspideraxisint.htm) object.

|  | Individual category axes | Specifies whether DIAdem configures the category axes individually. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Categories | Specifies the category whose axis is being configured. The displayed categories correspond with the texts you assigned to the categories on the Curve List tab. |
|  | Copy Definition | Opens the dialog box in which you copy the properties of other categories. |
|  | Font | Specifies the font of the axis scale. |
|  | Font size | Specifies the font size of the axis scale. |
|  | Font color | Specifies the color of the axis scale. |
|  | Highlighting color | Specifies the color with which you highlight the axis numbers. Use the Transparency setting to specify the highlighting intensity. |
|  | Format | Specifies the format of the axis scale. |
|  | Format Numbers | Opens the dialog box where you select or enter the format specification for the axis scale. |
|  | Bold | Specifies whether DIAdem uses bold font to display the axis scale. |
|  | Italics | Specifies whether DIAdem uses italic font to display the axis scale. |
|  | Underline | Specifies whether DIAdem uses underline font to display the axis scale. |
|  | Strikethrough | Specifies whether DIAdem uses strikethrough font to display the axis scale. |
|  | Frame | Specifies whether DIAdem frames each axis scale. |

|  |  | Note You can include subscript and superscript in text, format numbers, include variable contents, or use scripts for complex formats. Refer to the page on Formatting Text for more information. |
| --- | --- | --- |

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Create Model Hierarchy](../script_dlg_menu/dfse_modellhierarchy_dialog.htm) > Select Data Source

Select Data Source

Use this dialog box to open a connection to a DataFinder instance with a hierarchy, an NI ASAM server, or a Federation instance. 
Select a DataFinder instance with a hierarchy, an NI ASAM server, or a federation instance, and click **OK**.

| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Remove | Deletes the selected data source from the list. |
|  | Import | Imports a connection to a data source (*.urf). |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dfse_modellhierarchy_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00610: Create DataFinder Hierarchy

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dfse_modellhierarchy_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dfse_modellhierarchy_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > Create DataFinder Hierarchy

Create DataFinder Hierarchy

Use this dialog box to create a new DataFinder hierarchy. The DataFinder hierarchy specifies which properties the DataFinder displays and how the properties are arranged. The data preview displays the data in exactly the same way as a client, for example DIAdem, sees the data. The default model hierarchies that the DataFinder offers are Year - Month and Author - Year - Month. However, you can also specify your own DataFinder hierarchy.

#### Settings

|  | New DataFinder Hierarchy | Creates an empty DataFinder hierarchy. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Load DataFinder Hierarchy | Opens the dialog box where you load a DataFinder hierarchy (*.dfh). |
|  | Save DataFinder Hierarchy As | Opens the dialog box where you save a DataFinder hierarchy (*.dfh) under a new name. |
|  | Data Preview | Displays a preview of the data from the client view.Note The data preview is only available if your computer is connected with a server. |
|  | Note The data preview is only available if your computer is connected with a server. |  |
|  | Select Reference File... | Opens the dialog box where you can load a reference file that is typical for the files indexed by your server. |
|  | Select Active Data Source | Opens the dialog box where you select a data source for which you create or edit the hierarchy. |
|  | Active data source | Specifies the active data source. |
|  | File properties | Specifies that the Add Level dialog box displays all properties of the file level. |
|  | Group properties | Specifies that the Add Level dialog box displays all properties of the channel group level. |
|  | New Level Below | Opens the Add Level dialog box, where you add a new level to the existing DataFinder hierarchy. DIAdem always adds the new level below the selected level. You cannot add a new level below the test level. There must be at least one level above the test level to ensure the DataFinder hierarchy is valid. |
|  | Move Level Up | Moves a level one position up. |
|  | Move Level Down | Moves a level one position down. |
|  | Delete Level | Deletes a level. You cannot delete a level below the test level. |
|  | Property name | Specifies the name of the property selected in the overview. |
|  | Entity name | Specifies the name of the level selected in the overview. |
|  | Display mode | Specifies whether the DataFinder displays only the year or also the month for date/time properties. |
|  | Add waveform properties | Specifies whether or not the model contains waveform properties. The model contains waveform properties by default.Note This setting is not available for Federations. |
|  | Note This setting is not available for Federations. |  |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dlgautodefdlg_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00611: Generate Dialog Box Script

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dlgautodefdlg_dialog.htm`

## TOPIC 00612: Configure Recording Mode

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dlgautoheader_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dlgautoheader_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Scripts](../script_dlg_workspace/scripts_dlgs_overview.htm) > Configure Recording Mode

Configure Recording Mode

Use this dialog box to specify general settings for the recording mode.

#### Settings

| Author | Specifies the text that DIAdem inserts in the script header for the author. |
| --- | --- |
| Comment | Specifies the text that DIAdem inserts in the script header for the comment. |
| Only filename | Specifies that DIAdem only records the names of the files used, but not the paths. |
| Absolute path | Specifies that DIAdem records the names of the files used and the paths. |
| Path variable | Specifies that DIAdem declares the vector variable MyFolders in the recorded script and assigns the paths to this variable. DIAdem inserts this path variable in the command lines for loading or saving files, of the recorded script.DIAdem uses the paths assigned to the path variable only in the recorded script, without changing the default paths of the DIAdem settings. To use the script on a different computer, you just change the initialization of the path variable in the recorded procedure InitMyFolders. |

## TOPIC 00613: Edit DataPlugin Mapping

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_edit_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_edit_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Data Preparation Procedure: General](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm) > [Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm) > [Harmonize Property Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_main_dialog.htm) > Edit DataPlugin Mapping

Edit DataPlugin Mapping

Use this dialog box to assign a standardized identifier to the original identifier. The standardized identifier replaces the original identifier in the TDM file or TDMS file you want to create.

#### Settings

|  | Transfer Property Names | Transfers the property name from the column Original Identifier to the column Standardized Identifier. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Find and Replace | Opens the dialog box where you search for a text which you replace with a different text. |
|  | Delete Property Assignment | Deletes the standardized identifier in the selected row. The original identifier of the property remains in the Original Identifier column. |
|  | Root/Channel Group/Channel | Specifies the level on which you edit the DataPlugin mapping. |
|  | Standardized Identifier | Specifies the standardized name which replaces the original name of the property. |
|  | Original Identifier | Specifies the original name of the property. If you want to display the property in a group in the Data Portal, replace the separators in the original name with the tilde character. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_main_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00615: Harmonize Property Identifiers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_main_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_main_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Data Preparation Procedure: General](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm) > [Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm) > Harmonize Property Identifiers

Harmonize Property Identifiers

Use this dialog box to replace the property identifiers on file, channel group, or channel level for a specific DataPlugin. As soon as measurement data is loaded with the selected DataPlugin, the property identifiers in these files are replaced according to the mapping specified here. The page [Replace Values and Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_mapping.htm) describes how to replace values and identifiers in detail.

The dialog box contains for each level a separate tab on which DIAdem lists the original and the new identifier for each selected DataPlugin. In the dialog box you can use as many DataPlugins as you like in order to harmonize identifiers in the measurement files loaded by these DataPlugins.

In the **Add DataPlugin Mapping** dialog box, you select the DataPlugin matching the files in which you want to replace identifiers. After selecting the DataPlugin and closing the dialog box with **OK**, the subdialog box **Edit DataPlugin Mapping** opens, where you define the identifier replacement for this DataPlugin.

#### Settings

|  | New Mapping | Deletes all settings made in the dialog box Replace Property Identifiers and creates a new mapping. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Import Mapping | Imports a mapping file. You use mapping files with the filename extension *.tpim (Technical Property Identifier Mapping) to replace property identifiers. |
|  | Export Mapping | Exports a mapping file. |
|  | Edit Standardized Identifier | Opens the dialog box where you edit the identifier. |
|  | Delete Standardized Identifier | Deletes the selected row. |
|  | Add DataPlugin Mapping | Adds a new column with the name of the selected DataPlugin. |
|  | Copy DataPlugin Mapping | Transfers the properties of the selected column to a different DataPlugin. |
|  | Edit DataPlugin Mapping | Opens the dialog box where you edit the property identifiers for the DataPlugin. |
|  | Delete DataPlugin Mapping | Deletes the selected row. |
|  | Root/Channel Group/Channel | Specifies the level on which you replace the property identifiers. |
|  | DataPlugin Name | Specifies the name of the DataPlugin in whose measurement files you replace the property identifiers. |
|  | Standardized Identifier | Specifies the identifier of the selected DataPlugins that replaces the original identifier. |
|  | Original Identifier | Specifies the original identifier. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_searchandreplace_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00616: Find and Replace

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_searchandreplace_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_searchandreplace_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Data Preparation Procedure: General](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm) > [Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm) > [Harmonize Property Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_main_dialog.htm) > [Edit DataPlugin Mapping](../script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_edit_dialog.htm) > Find and Replace

Find and Replace

Use this dialog box to replace standardized identifiers of properties automatically. For example, you can replace a standardized identifier with a new identifier on the root, channel group, or channel level.

#### Settings

| Find | Specifies the text to be replaced. |
| --- | --- |
| Replace with | Specifies the replacement text for the text you want to find. |
| Match case | Enable this setting to find text that matches the case of the text you want to find. For example, if you search for Test, the dialog box does not replace the text test. |
| Match whole word only | Enable this setting to find exactly the text you entered. For example, if you search for Test, the dialog box does not replace the text Test_1. |
| Search upwards | Enable this setting to search upwards in the table. |
| Find Next | Searches for the next matching text in the table. |
| Replace | Replaces the text found in the table. |
| Replace All | Replaces all instances of the text found in the table in one step. |

Analysis Automation Procedure: Buttons

The buttons in the **Analysis Automation Procedure** dialog box are described in the following.

#### Settings

|  | New Analysis Automation Procedure | Opens the dialog box where you load a new analysis automation procedure. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Open Analysis Automation Procedure | Opens the dialog box where you load an analysis automation procedure. |
|  | Save Analysis Automation Procedure As | Opens the dialog box where you save an analysis automation procedure under a new name.As long as you do not modify the Identifier of the analysis automation procedure, you save a new version of the existing packet. In this case, the web interface of the analysis automation performs an update of the analysis automation procedure. |
|  | Test the Analysis Automation Procedure | Simulates the analysis automation procedure with the selected file. DIAdem displays the simulation result in the Data Portal. If you test the analysis automation procedure in DIAdem, DIAdem does not include a timeout. |
|  | Debug Analysis Automation Procedure | Simulates the analysis automation procedure with a debugger with the selected file. DIAdem displays the simulation result in the Data Portal. If you test the analysis automation procedure in DIAdem, DIAdem does not include a timeout. |
|  | Select Active Data Source | Opens the dialog box where you select a DataFinder or a Data Store. Open the data source in the NAVIGATOR panel. |
|  | Current data source | Displays the data source specified under Select Active Data Source. |
|  | Display Reduced Dialog Box | Reduces the dialog box to title bar and toolbar. |
|  | Display Extended Dialog Box | Expands the dialog box to allow you to make settings. |

#### Procedures

[Define Data Preparation Procedure for TDMS Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4tdms.htm) | [Define Data Preparation Procedure for XLSX Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4xlsx.htm) | [Defining the Configuration of an Analysis Automation Procedure](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_anp_diadem.htm) | [Definition of a SystemLink TDM Process Chain](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_overview.htm) | [Exploring Indexed Data with a Different Hierarchy View](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_hierarchy.htm)

Configure Analysis Automation Procedure: Parameter Definition

Use the **Parameter Definition** tab to define the analysis parameters. You specify the actual analysis in the [Analysis Script](../script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_config_analysescript_dialog.htm).

In the parameters, you can specify the settings for an analysis function, such as the window used for an FFT, or the result folder. You can change the values of the parameters when creating a task on the web interface of the analysis automation so that you can perform the same analysis with different parameters. In this dialog, you only specify the initialization values of the parameters.

Use the [Context object](../../tdmcontext/objects/ivbscontextas_objects_overview.htm) within the analysis script to access the parameters.

|  | Type | Specifies the data type of the parameter. |
|  | Initialization Value | Specifies the initialization value of the parameter. |
|  | Description | Specifies a text to describe the parameter. |

#### Further Settings

## TOPIC 00623: Analysis Automation Procedure: General Information

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_general.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_general.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > Analysis Automation Procedure: General Information

Analysis Automation Procedure: General Information

Use Analysis Automation in SystemLink to execute recurring, comparative or parallel analyses with similar data. Analysis Automation can save result data in new TDM files and can export reports as PDF documents or graphics. Select **Settings»SystemLink TDM»Analysis Automation Procedure** to edit and create analysis automation configurations.

Use the **Search Query** step to define a search query in order to find the data from a test or on a specific topic. You process this data in the analysis script. An analysis automation task uses this search query for the DataFinder you assigned to the task. First, click **Data filter enabled** in the **Search Query** step to show the search input area and the search results list.

Use the **Parameter Definition** tab to define the parameters for the analysis. You specify the actual analysis in the analysis script. In the parameters, you can specify the settings for a function, such as the window used for an FFT, or the result folder. For each task you can assign different values to these parameters on the web interface of the analysis automation. This way you can execute the same analysis with different parameters. Use the transferred [Context object](../../tdmcontext/objects/ivbscontextas_objects_overview.htm) to access the parameters within the analysis script.

Use the **Analysis Script** step to compile the analysis automation procedure.

In the central script Main.vbsa, you define the actual analysis. If Python is your evaluation environment, the script name is Main.py.

The analysis automation procedure must contain all files, such as layouts or more scripts, which you use in this analysis. The tree view in the lower part of the dialog box displays the files which are already in the analysis automation procedure. Use the respective buttons to import additional files or entire folders into the analysis automation procedure. During this process, the import creates a copy of the specified file and saves it in the analysis automation procedure. This means that you must first export a file from the analysis automation procedure in order to process it, and that you then must add this file to the analysis automation procedure again. In the process DIAdem replaces the previous file from the package.

The analysis script contains the procedures On_Initialize, On_RunAnalysisProcedure, and On_Finalize. Use [On_Initialize](../../tdmcontext/procedures/on_initialize.htm) and [On_Finalize](../../tdmcontext/procedures/on_finalize.htm) to initialize and complete a parallel procedure. Use [On_Run_AnalysisProcedure](../../tdmcontext/procedures/on_run_analysisprocedure.htm) to add user-defined program code with which the analysis automation procedure the elements from the search. The procedure is called several times in a parallel evaluation and only once in a comparative evaluation.

You can use virtually all DIAdem commands in the analysis script. However, you should avoid commands which require an interaction and also commands that control the DIAdem interface, the VIEW panel, Microsoft Office applications, or other applications. In the analysis script, you can record the error and analysis status of the transferred [Context object](../../tdmcontext/objects/ivbscontextas_objects_overview.htm) and access the exchange variables. Click **Edit** in the **Analysis Script** step to edit the analysis script in the DIAdem script editor.

Save the analysis automation procedure configuration as an ANP file after you defined the analysis in the steps **Search Query**, **Parameter Definition**, and **Analysis Script**. Before loading this file into the web interface of Analysis Automation and executing it there, you should test the analysis with the respective functions in the DIAdem dialog box. To do so, use the **Test Analysis Automation Procedure** or **Debug Analysis Automation Procedure** buttons.

|  | Note DIAdem saves the analysis automation procedure during configuration even if you do not explicitly save it. Therefore, the analysis automation procedure should be editable when you load and display it. To prevent DIAdem from overwriting the original file, you should load and edit a copy of the analysis automation procedure.You can load and edit analysis automation procedures (*.anp) from older DIAdem versions in DIAdem 2019. Analysis automation procedures created or edited in DIAdem 2019 can be used in SystemLink TDM 2019 or later. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note Microsoft does not support the server-side automation of Microsoft Office applications as client components, for example, with the CreateObject method. Office might become unstable in such an environment and applications may exclude each other. This does not only apply to Microsoft Office applications, but to all automation objects which require a user identification or which are designed for interaction with the desktop. Many applications issue success or error messages which need to be confirmed interactively. This is not possible with the server-side automation. |
| --- | --- |

#### Related Topics

[Buttons](../script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_config_dialog_buttons.htm)

## TOPIC 00625: Analysis Automation: Testing the Analysis Automation Procedure

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_simulation_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_simulation_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Analysis automation procedure: General Information](../script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_general.htm) > Analysis Automation: Testing the Analysis Automation Procedure

Analysis Automation: Testing the Analysis Automation Procedure

Use this dialog box to test the analysis automation procedure before it is packed and loaded onto the web interface of the analsis automation.

During the test, DIAdem does not include the timeout specified in the analysis automation procedure.

However, in the analysis script you should avoid commands which require an interaction and also commands that control the DIAdem interface, the VIEW panel, Microsoft Office applications, or other applications. The simulation executes these commands but the analysis automation cannot include them later. This means that the result of the simulation is not a hundred percent consistent with the result on the web interface of the analysis automation. Therefore, a final test of the analysis automation procedure on the web interface of the analysis automation is essential.

#### Settings

| Simulation File | Specifies the file that contains the simulation data. |
| --- | --- |
| Name | Displays the parameter name. |
| Type | Displays the data type of the parameter. |
| Value | Specifies the value of the parameter. |
| Description | Displays a text that describes the parameters. |

#### Related Topics

[Parameter Definition](../script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_config_parameter_dialog.htm) | [Parameter](../script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_config_parameter_dialog.htm) | [Analysis Script](../script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_config_analysescript_dialog.htm) | [Identification](../script_dlg_menu/tss_analysisserver_config_information_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Define Data Preparation Procedure for TDMS Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4tdms.htm) | [Define Data Preparation Procedure for XLSX Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4xlsx.htm) | [Defining the Configuration of an Analysis Automation Procedure](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_anp_diadem.htm) | [Definition of a SystemLink TDM Process Chain](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_overview.htm) | [Exploring Indexed Data with a Different Hierarchy View](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_hierarchy.htm)

Use this dialog box to test the analysis automation procedure before it is packed and loaded onto the server.

Data Preparation Procedure: Buttons

The buttons in the **Analysis Automation Procedure Configuration** dialog box are described in the following.

#### Settings

|  | New Data Preparation Procedure Configuration | Opens the dialog box where you load a new data prepartion procedure. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Open Data Preparation Procedure | Opens the dialog box where you load an data preparation procedure. |
|  | Save data preparation procedure as | Opens the dialog box where you save an data preparation procedure under a new name. |
|  | Test Data Preparation Procedure | Executes a data preparation simulation with the selected file.DIAdem displays the simulation result in the Data Portal. |
|  | Testing the Data Preparation Procedure with the Debugger | Executes with the selected file a data procedure procedure simulation with the internal debugger. If the external debugger is enabled, this button is disabled.DIAdem displays the simulation result in the Data Portal. |
|  | Select Active Data Source | Opens the dialog box where you select a DataFinder or a Data Store. The data preparation procedure uses the data source in the dialog box Replace Property Values to specify the level and the property name. Open the data source in the NAVIGATOR panel. |
|  | Current data source | Displays the data source specified under Select Active Data Source. |
|  | Display Reduced Dialog Box | Shows the reduced dialog box. |
|  | Display Extended Dialog Box | Shows the whole dialog box. |

## TOPIC 00630: Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Identifiers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Data Preparation Procedure: General](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm) > Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Identifiers

Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Identifiers

Use the **Replace Identifiers** tab to assign the same property identifiers to measurement files from different sources. Click the **Edit** button to open the dialog box where you specify the identifiers for root, channel group, and channel properties in the [Replace Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/navi_propidentifiermapping_main_dialog.htm) dialog box. The page [Replace Values and Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_mapping.htm) describes in detail how to replace values and identifiers of a property.

An identifier is the name of a property. If files from different measurement sources contain different identifiers for the source of a test, for example, source 1:
"Engine"; source 2: "Engine_Type"; source 3: "Fuel", you can now specify "Engine_Fuel_Type" as the standardized identifier. You harmonize the property, which may have different versions, on the tab [Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Values](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_valuemapping_dialog.htm). The page [Replace Values and Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_mapping.htm) describes how to replace values and identifiers in detail.

|  | Note If you want to replace identifiers and values of a property, always replace the identifier and then replace the value of the property with the then changed identifier. To check the mapping in the Test Mapping dialog box with a DataFinder, you must save the files created when the identifier was replaced in the search area of the DataFinder and optimize the specified new identifiers of the properties. |
| --- | --- |

#### Settings

| Buttons | Describes the general buttons in the dialog box. |
| --- | --- |
| Replace property identifiers | Specifies whether Data Preparation replaces the property identifiers of the root, channel group, and channel. |
| Edit | Opens the dialog box where you specify which identifiers from the original measurement files Data Preparation replaces with a standardized identifier. |

#### Further Settings

Replace Identifier | [Replace Values](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_valuemapping_dialog.htm) | [Convert Units](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_unitconversion_dialog.htm) | [Statistics](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_statistics_dialog.htm) | [V&V](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_vandv_dialog.htm) | [Convert File](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_fileconversion_dialog.htm) | [Identifier](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_information_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Define Data Preparation Procedure for TDMS Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4tdms.htm) | [Define Data Preparation Procedure for XLSX Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4xlsx.htm) | [Defining the Configuration of an Analysis Automation Procedure](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_anp_diadem.htm) | [Definition of a SystemLink TDM Process Chain](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_overview.htm) | [Exploring Indexed Data with a Different Hierarchy View](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_hierarchy.htm)

Use the **Statistics** tab to calculate the statistical characteristic values.

#### Settings

| Buttons | Describes the general buttons in the dialog box. |
| --- | --- |
| Calculate statistics | Specifies whether to calculate characteristic statistical values. |
| Edit | Opens the dialog box where you specify which characteristic statistical values to calculate. |

## TOPIC 00634: Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Values

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_valuemapping_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_valuemapping_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Data Preparation Procedure: General](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm) > Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Values

Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Values

Assign the original values of properties from measurement files of different sources on the **Replace Values** tab. Specify the values for file, channel group, and channel level in the dialog box **Harmonize Property Values**, which opens when you click the **Edit** button. The page [Replace Values and Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_mapping.htm) describes how to replace values and identifiers of a property in detail.

The contents of a property are called values and may be a string, integer, float, or time type. An identifier is the name of a property.

|  | Note If you want to replace identifiers and values of a property, always replace the identifier and then replace the value of the property with the then changed identifier. To check the mapping in the dialog box Test Mapping with a DataFinder, you must save the files created when the identifier was replaced in the search area of the DataFinder and optimize the specified new identifiers of the properties. |
| --- | --- |

#### Settings

| Buttons | Describes the general buttons in the dialog box. |
| --- | --- |
| Harmonize property values | Specifies whether Data Preparation replaces the identifier values of files, channel groups, and channels. |
| Edit | Opens the dialog box where you specify which values from the original measurement files Data Preparation replaces with a standardized value. |

#### Further Settings

[Replace Identifie](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm)r | Replace Values | [Convert Units](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_unitconversion_dialog.htm) | [Statistics](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_statistics_dialog.htm) | [V&V](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_vandv_dialog.htm) | [Convert File](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_fileconversion_dialog.htm) | [Identifier](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_information_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Define Data Preparation Procedure for TDMS Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4tdms.htm) | [Define Data Preparation Procedure for XLSX Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4xlsx.htm) | [Defining the Configuration of an Analysis Automation Procedure](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_anp_diadem.htm) | [Definition of a SystemLink TDM Process Chain](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_overview.htm) | [Exploring Indexed Data with a Different Hierarchy View](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_hierarchy.htm)

## TOPIC 00635: Configure Data Preparation Procedure: V&V

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_vandv_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_vandv_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > [Data Preparation Procedure: General](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm) > Configure Data Preparation Procedure: V&V

Configure Data Preparation Procedure: V&V

On the **V&V** tab you specify whether SystemLink TDM verifies and validates the data from the specified data source before saving the data with the TDM or the TDMS DataPlugin. To do so, create a script in the DIAdem script editor that tests your requirements for the data preparation procedure with data from the specified data source.

The script contains the procedure [On_ValidationAndVerification](../../tdmcontext/procedures/on_validationandverification.htm). Enter the program code, which the data preparation uses to check the data, into this procedure. You can use virtually all DIAdem commands in this script. However, you should avoid commands which require an interaction and also commands that control the DIAdem interface, the VIEW and REPORT panels, Microsoft Office applications, or other applications.

Use the transferred [Context object](../../tdmcontext/objects/tdmcontext_objects_ivbscontextvnv.htm) within this script to log the errors and the status of the test.

Use the buttons **Data Preparation Procedure Test** or **Data Preparation Test with Debugger** to test all the settings you made in the process chain. DIAdem displays the test result in the Data Portal.

|  | Note Go to Notes for Creating Scripts for Analysis Automation and Data Preparation to find important information on creating data preparation scripts. |
| --- | --- |

#### Settings

| Buttons | Describes the general buttons in the dialog box. |
| --- | --- |
| Validation and verification | Specifies whether SystemLink TDM verifies and validates the data from the specified data source with the procedure. |
| Edit | Opens the specified procedure in the DIAdem script editor.Note You can only save the open procedure in the script editor but you cannot save it under a different name or in a different folder. |

#### Further Settings

[Replace Identifier](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm) | [Replace Values](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_valuemapping_dialog.htm) | [Convert Units](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_unitconversion_dialog.htm) | [Statistics](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_statistics_dialog.htm) | V&V | [Convert File](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_fileconversion_dialog.htm) | [Identifier](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_information_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Define Data Preparation Procedure for TDMS Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4tdms.htm) | [Define Data Preparation Procedure for XLSX Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4xlsx.htm) | [Defining the Configuration of an Analysis Automation Procedure](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_anp_diadem.htm) | [Definition of a SystemLink TDM Process Chain](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_overview.htm) | [Exploring Indexed Data with a Different Hierarchy View](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_hierarchy.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00636: Data Preparation Procedure: General

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_general.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [SystemLink TDM](../script_dlg_menu/tss_overview.htm) > Data Preparation Procedure: General

Data Preparation Procedure: General

Use Data Preparation to harmonize measurement data from different file formats from different sources. Specify harmonization in a procedure you create under **Settings»SystemLinkTDM»Data Preparation** in DIAdem SCRIPT. Configure the settings in a process chain which transforms your data into a unified format, so that this data can be, for example, compared at a glance.

|  | Note You can load and edit data preparation procedures (*.dpp) from older DIAdem versions in DIAdem 2019. Data preparation procedures created or edited in DIAdem 2019 can be used in SystemLink TDM 2019 or later. |
| --- | --- |

**Identifiers**

If, for example, the files are from different sources in which the identifiers for the test engine are saved differently, such as source 1: "Engine", source 2: "Engine_Type", source 3: "Fuel", you can specify "Engine_Fuel_Type" as the harmonized identifier. Data Preparation assigns the identifier "Engine_Fuel_Type" to the different sources of the respective property.

|  | Source 1 | Source 2 | Source 3 | Standardized Identifier |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Identifier of the Property | "Engine" | "Engine_Type" | "Fuel" | "Engine_Fuel_Type" |

#### Values

If the files from the different sources also contain different values for the name of the engine to be tested, for example, source 1: "Diesel", source 2: "D", source 3: "Fuel_Diesel", you can specify "Diesel" as the default value. Data Preparation now assigns the value "Diesel" to the various properties from the different sources.

|  | Source 1 | Source 2 | Source 3 | Harmonized Value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Property Value | "Diesel" | "D" | "Fuel_Diesel" | "Diesel" |

Following the replacement, all sources have the property with the identifier "Engine_Fuel_Type" and the value "Diesel":

| Harmonised Property Identifier | Harmonized Property Value |
| --- | --- |
| "Engine_Fuel_Type" | "Diesel" |

#### Harmonizing Units

You can harmonize units in Data Preparation in a similar way. If a file uses, for example, the unit km/h, this unit cannot be compared to the unit mph of another file. In order to harmonize these units, you can specify in Data Preparation that the unit mph is converted to km/h and is displayed as km/h in the processed TDM or TDMS files.

#### Calculating Statistical Data

With Data Preparation you can also calculate the statistical values, as minimum value, maximum value, or the standard deviation from the data of individual files and display them in the converted TDM or TDMS file as properties.

#### Verification and Validation

Create a script to check the harmonized data for plausibility and completeness before you finally save the data. This can also include validation and verification of limit values.

Use the created data preparation procedure (*.dpp) to process your data on the **Data Preparation** web interface. Before loading this procedure onto the web interface of Data Preparation in SystemLink Server and executing it there, you should test the prepared data with the respective functions in the DIAdem dialog box.

#### Convert File

Saves the data preparation procedure with the TDM, TDMS or another DataPlugin that DIAdem can use to save data. After saving this configuration file, load it into the Data Preparation application in SystemLink Server, which uses the configuration you defined to edit the data and to save it in the raw data area for further analysis. The DataPlugin used in the configuration must also be installed and activated on SystemLink Server.

#### Identifier

Is used to view and edit the descriptive information in the data preparation procedure.

#### Related Topics

[Buttons](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_dialog_buttons.htm)

[Replace Identifier](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm) | [Replace Values](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_valuemapping_dialog.htm) | [Convert Units](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_unitconversion_dialog.htm) | [Statistics](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_statistics_dialog.htm) | [V&V](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_vandv_dialog.htm) | [Convert File](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_fileconversion_dialog.htm) | [Identifier](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_information_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Define Data Preparation Procedure for TDMS Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4tdms.htm) | [Define Data Preparation Procedure for XLSX Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4xlsx.htm) | [Defining the Configuration of an Analysis Automation Procedure](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_anp_diadem.htm) | [Definition of a SystemLink TDM Process Chain](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_overview.htm) | [Exploring Indexed Data with a Different Hierarchy View](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_hierarchy.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_mapping.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00637: Replacing Property Values and Property Identifiers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_mapping.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_mapping.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Identifiers](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_mapping_dialog.htm) | [Configure Data Preparation Procedure: Replace Values](../script_dlg_menu/tss_datapreprocessor_config_valuemapping_dialog.htm)) > Replacing Property Values and Property Identifiers

Replacing Property Values and Property Identifiers

Use the data preparation to configure the settings you need in order to unify your measurement data along a process chain. This way you can compare test stand results from different locations where the same tests were executed with different hardware. In different measurement devices the identifiers and the values of the properties are saved differently.

If files from different sources contain different identifiers for an engine you want to test, for example, source 1:
"Engine"; source 2: "Engine_Type"; source 3: "Fuel", you can now specify "Engine_Fuel_Type" as the default identifier in this dialog box. The data preparation now assigns the identifier “Engine_Fuel_Type” to all properties from the different sources.

|  | Source 1 | Source 2 | Source 3 | Standardized Identifier |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Identifier of the Property | "Engine" | "Engine_Type" | "Fuel" | "Engine_Fuel_Type" |

If files from different sources also contain different values for the name of the engine to be tested, for example, source 1: "Diesel"; source 2: "D"; source 3: "Fuel_Diesel", you can now specify "Diesel" as the default value in this dialog box. The data preparation now assigns the value “Engine_Fuel_Type” to all properties from the different sources.

|  | Source 1 | Source 2 | Source 3 | Standardized Value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Property Value | "Diesel" | "D" | "Fuel_Diesel" | "Diesel" |

After the replacement all sources have the value "Diesel" for the identifier "Engine_Fuel_Type":

| Standardized Identifier | Standardized Value |
| --- | --- |
| "Engine_Fuel_Type" | "Diesel" |

However, you cannot change all properties of data sets, channel groups, and channels.

You cannot alter the following properties of a **Data set**:channelgroups, children, datestring, datetime, environment, external_references, instance_attributes, parent_test, registercomments, sourceoriginalname, timestring, and wf_create_time.

The following properties of a **channel group** cannot be changed: channels, equipments, export_attributes, external_references, index, instance_attributes, measurement_begin, measurement_end, root, sequences, sourceoriginalname, submatrices, test, and units_under_test.

The following properties of a **channel** cannot be changed: channel, datatype, deletebehaviour, displaytype, empty, export_attributes, external_references, flagkey, group, groupindex, groupname, implicit_increment, implicit_start, instance_attributes, internal_params, internal_res1, internal_res2, length, lengthmax, local_columns, maximum, measurement, minimum, monotony, novaluekey, number, quantity, representation, sourcedatafilename, sourcedatafilepath, sourcegenparam1, sourcegenparam2, sourcehandle, sourceinstancekey, sourcename, sourceoriginalname, sourceparentname, sourcerepresentation, sourcetype, sourcevaluetype, status, unit, valuetype, waveform, wf_samples, and writeprotection.

#### Procedures

[Define Data Preparation Procedure for TDMS Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4tdms.htm) | [Define Data Preparation Procedure for XLSX Files](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_dpp_diadem4xlsx.htm) | [Defining the Configuration of an Analysis Automation Procedure](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_anp_diadem.htm) | [Definition of a SystemLink TDM Process Chain](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_overview.htm) | [Exploring Indexed Data with a Different Hierarchy View](../../procscript/proctdmserver/proctdmserver_hierarchy.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgscript/script_dlg_workspace/dlgsearch_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00638: Find and Replace

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_workspace/dlgsearch_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_workspace/dlgsearch_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Script Editor](../script_dlg_workspace/editor_overview.htm) > Find and Replace

Find and Replace

Use this dialog box to search for text in the script editor and to replace it by other text.

#### Settings

| Find | Specifies the text to search for. |
| --- | --- |
| Replace with | Specifies the text to be replaced. |
| Match case | Specifies whether DIAdem distinguishes between uppercase and lowercase. |
| Find in selection | Specifies whether DIAdem searches and replaces in the whole text or only in a selected section. |
| Match whole word only | Specifies whether DIAdem only searches for the text as a whole word. |
| Search up | Specifies that DIAdem searches in the direction of the file beginning. |
| Use regular expressions | Specifies whether DIAdem uses regular expressions. |
| Use wildcards | Specifies whether DIAdem uses wildcards. |
| Find Next | Specifies that DIAdem does not replace the text it finds, but keeps searching. |
| Replace | Specifies that DIAdem replaces the text when it is found. |
| Replace All | Specifies that DIAdem replaces all the text it finds. |
| Select All | Specifies that DIAdem marks all lines that contain the text, with a bookmark. |

|  | Note You also can open this dialog box with <Ctrl-F> or <Ctrl-H>. |
| --- | --- |
|  | Note Use the following Shortcuts to use further search mechanisms quickly. Ctrl + I Starts the incremented search. DIAdem searches for the text you enter after you use the shortcut. F3 Displays the next search result in the direction of the file end. Ctrl + F3 Defines a new search and displays the search result in the direction of the file end. If you select a text, this is the search text. If you do not select a text and if the cursor is in a comment, the complete comment is the search text. If you do not select a text and the cursor is within the quotation marks, the text within the quotation marks is the search text. Ctrl + Shift + F3 Defines the new search and displays the search result in the direction of the file beginning. |
| Ctrl + I | Starts the incremented search. DIAdem searches for the text you enter after you use the shortcut. |
| F3 | Displays the next search result in the direction of the file end. |
| Ctrl + F3 | Defines a new search and displays the search result in the direction of the file end. If you select a text, this is the search text. If you do not select a text and if the cursor is in a comment, the complete comment is the search text. If you do not select a text and the cursor is within the quotation marks, the text within the quotation marks is the search text. |
| Ctrl + Shift + F3 | Defines the new search and displays the search result in the direction of the file beginning. |

## TOPIC 00641: Registered Type Libraries

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgscript/script_dlg_workspace/typelibrary_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgscript/script_dlg_workspace/typelibrary_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem SCRIPT](../script_dlg_menu/script_dlgs_overview.htm) > [General](../script_dlg_menu/dlgscript_overview.htm) > Registered Type Libraries

Registered Type Libraries

Use this dialog box to enable and to display the type libraries installed on your computer.

#### Settings

| Available libraries | Displays the available type libraries.Click the selection field to register the respective type library in DIAdem for CodeCompletion. You must also define the related automation object with the Set statement and the CreateObject function in the script. If you press <Ctrl-Spacebar> in the script editor, DIAdem displays the associated objects for the registered libraries. If you enter a dot behind an object, DIAdem lists all methods and properties of this object. Refer to the related documentation for further information on the respective type libraries. |
| --- | --- |
| Name | Shows the designation of the selected type library. |
| ID | Shows the ID of the selected type library. |
| Version | Shows the version of the selected type library. |
| Path | Shows the path to the selected type library. |
| Name | Shows the name of the selected type library. |
| Add | Opens a dialog box where you can select a file-based library which you can add to the list of available libraries. |
| Copy | Copies two comment lines and the AutEdTypeLibAdd command to the clipboard. You only need to select the type library but do not need to click the selection field. You can then copy the contents of the clipboard into a script. The copied comment lines contain the name of the library and the folder where the library is saved. The copied line contains the AutEdTypeLibAdd command with the parameters AutEdTypeLibId and AutEdTypeLibVer. The AutEdTypeLibAdd command registers the type library in the VBS script environment. You can then access the constants defined in the library, for example, the constant ForWriting when you insert the Microsoft Scripting library. DIAdem does not show the constants in CodeCompletion.The copied text in this example is:' Microsoft Scripting Runtime ' C:\\WINDOWS\\system32\\scrrun.dll Call AutEdTypeLibAdd("420B2830-E718-11CF-893D-00A0C9054228", "1.0") |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Script»Type Libraries in DIAdem SCRIPT. |
| --- | --- |

#### Related Topics

[CodeCompletion](../../genscript/genscript/codecompletion.htm) | [Command: ScriptCMDRegister](../../comoff/scriptcmdregister.htm) | [Method: CreateObject for VBS](../../vbs/methods/vbs_method_createobject_globalobj.htm) | [Method: GetObject for VBS](../../vbs/methods/vbs_method_getobject_globalobj.htm)

## TOPIC 00642: Print

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/bilddef_drucken.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgshell/dlgshell/bilddef_drucken.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[General Dialog Boxes](../dlgshell/gendialogs_overview.htm) > Print

Print

Use this dialog box to print a worksheet.

#### Settings

| Printer | Displays which printer is being used. |
| --- | --- |
| Print to file | Specifies whether you print to a file or directly to the printer. |
| Copies | Specifies the number of copies to be printed. |
| Print quality | Specifies the resolution of the printout. |
| Selected format | Displays whether you print in portrait format or landscape format. |
| Left | Specifies the offset of the printout to the left margin of the sheet. |
| Top | Specifies the offset of the printout to the top margin of the sheet. |
| Width | Specifies the width of the printout. |
| Height | Specifies the height of the printout. DIAdem calculates the height depending on the height ratio and width ratio that are set in the Layout parameters. |
| Print range | Specifies the worksheets to be printed. |
| Printer | Opens the dialog box where you specify the printer to be used. |
| Min. Borders | Specifies the minimum margins for the selected printer and the specified page format. |

|  | Note If your report includes multipage tables, DIAdem prints only the visible table sheets. In order to print out all pages of the automatically expanding tables use the setting Print all pages with expanding tables completely in DIAdem Settings REPORT. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00643: Load DIAdem Settings

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/ddd_file_load_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgshell/dlgshell/ddd_file_load_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[General Dialog Boxes](../dlgshell/gendialogs_overview.htm) > Load DIAdem Settings

Load DIAdem Settings

Use this dialog box to load your [DIAdem settings](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_desktop.htm).

|  | Note After you load a new desktop file, DIAdem restarts. If you did not save your program settings and data, you will lose them. |
| --- | --- |

#### Settings

| Filename | Specifies the name of the desktop file that DIAdem is to load. |
| --- | --- |
| File type | Specifies the type of the file that DIAdem is to load. Desktop files have the file extension .ddd. |

Select **Settings»DIAdem Settings»Select Path** to predefine the paths from which DIAdem loads files or to which DIAdem saves files. As soon as you load a file from a different path into a load dialog box or save a file to a different path in a save dialog box, DIAdem changes the respective user paths. The default setting that DIAdem uses when the program launches remains unchanged.

|  | Note You cannot use this function in scripts. Use the Start parameter /D to load a desktop file when DIAdem launches. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»Load. |
| --- | --- |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgshell/dlgshell/ddd_file_save_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00644: Save DIAdem Settings As

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/ddd_file_save_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgshell/dlgshell/ddd_file_save_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[General Dialog Boxes](../dlgshell/gendialogs_overview.htm) > Save DIAdem Settings As

Save DIAdem Settings As

Use this dialog box to save your [DIAdem settings](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_desktop.htm).

|  | Note If you load DIAdem settings, DIAdem restarts automatically. Use the Start parameter /D to load a desktop file when DIAdem launches. |
| --- | --- |

#### Settings

| Filename | Specifies the name of the file that DIAdem is to save. |
| --- | --- |
| File type | Specifies which type of file DIAdem is to save. |

Select **Settings»DIAdem Settings»Select Path** to predefine the paths from which DIAdem loads files or to which DIAdem saves files. As soon as you load a file from a different path into a load dialog box or save a file to a different path in a save dialog box, DIAdem changes the respective user paths. The default setting that DIAdem uses when the program launches remains unchanged.

The desktop file has the extension .ddd. In the desktop file you save general default settings for DIAdem behavior, specific data formats, and properties of channels. You also save the parameters for the data area, settings for the logfile, and panel-specific default settings. When DIAdem saves the desktop file, DIAdem also creates files with the filename extension par, tuc,bdn, and tpr. DIAdem also creates a folder that has the same name as the desktop file. To be able to use a configuration on another computer, you must forward all the configuration files (*.ddd, *.par, *.tuc, *.bdn*, .tpr) and the subfolder that has the same name as the desktop file.

|  | Note The DeskDrv variable gives you the current desktop folder. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»Load. |
| --- | --- |

#### Script Call

[DeskSave](../../comoff/desksave.htm)

## TOPIC 00645: Template for Custom Properties

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/dlg_custproptemplate_dialog.htm`

- content_type: ``

[General Dialog Boxes](../dlgshell/gendialogs_overview.htm) > [DIAdem Settings](../dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm) > Template for Custom Properties

Template for Custom Properties

Use this the dialog box to define a template for custom properties for the data set, channel groups, and channels. As soon as you load new data to the Data Portal or create new channel groups or channels, DIAdem adds the associated custom properties from the template. If you create a new template for custom properties or modify existing custom properties from a template, the internal data store in the Data Portal is not affected.

#### Settings

|  | New Entry | Adds a new row to the overview where you can enter the name, the data type, and the first value for a new custom property. The tilde character is a separator which groups the custom properties in the Properties Display of the Data Portal. DIAdem combines custom properties containing the same text before the tilde character. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected custom property from the template. |
|  | Data Set/Group/Channel | Specifies whether you generate custom properties for the data set, the channel groups, or the channels. |
|  | Property | Specifies the name of the custom property. |
|  | Data Type | Specifies the data type of the custom property. |
|  | Initial Value | Specifies the first value of the custom property. |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»DIAdem Settings»General»Edit. First select the checkbox Template for custom properties. You save and load a template for custom properties in the General DIAdem Settings. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00648: DIAdem Settings: Path Selection

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselect_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselect_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[General Dialog Boxes](../dlgshell/gendialogs_overview.htm) > [DIAdem Settings](../dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm) > DIAdem Settings: Path Selection

DIAdem Settings: Path Selection

Use this dialog box to specify the default paths for the [User folders](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_directories.htm). The settings apply to the default settings of the load and save dialog boxes, immediately after DIAdem launches.

#### Settings

|  | Path behavior | Specifies whether you use the standard path behavior or the extended path behavior. In the Standard mode you can specify the path for the data and the path for all other documents. In the Extended mode you can specify all paths separately. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Synchronize paths | Specifies whether DIAdem hides or shows the additional column Synchronize Paths where you assign several paths to one group. |
|  | User paths | Specifies the default setting of the paths from which DIAdem loads files and into which DIAdem saves files. As soon as you load a file from a different path into a load dialog box or save a file to a different path in a save dialog box, DIAdem changes the respective user paths. The default setting that DIAdem uses when the program launches remains unchanged.The predefined user path is by default at C:\\Users\\Public\\. All users can read files from or write files into this path. |
|  | File type | Specifies the file type for which you specify the load path and the save path. The default setting has two paths. The first path specifies the data path and the second path specifies the path for all other files. Data files include files such as TDM files and DAT files. Other files, for example, are layouts for DIAdem VIEW and DIAdem REPORT, scripts, user dialog boxes, media such as graphics files and video files, and configuration files for search definitions and import filters and export filters. |
|  | Find | Opens the dialog box where you specify the user folder. |

|  | Note If you do not specify a drive, you can specify paths relative to the program path. For example, if DIAdem is installed on C:\\DIAdem and you specify the path MyPath\\Documents, DIAdem uses the path C:\\DIAdem\\MyPath\\Documents. |
| --- | --- |
|  | Note You cannot change the predefined paths with a script. |
|  | Note DIAdem saves the paths that are predefined in this dialog box in the Desktop file. The DIAdem standard desktop file uses the wildcard CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS in the path specification. This wildcard corresponds with the path to the folder Shared Documents. By default this path is at C:\\Users\\Public\\.In the path settings you can use all constants that are described in the SHGetFolderCSIDL and SHGetFolderPath variables. Enclose the constants in % signs, for example, %CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS%. You also can use Windows environment variables.Click here for a list of the most important path variables. |
|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»DIAdem Settings»Select Path. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm) | Path Selection | [Path Selection with Path Synchronization](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectsync_dialog.htm) | [Path Selection - Library Paths](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectlibr_dialog.htm) | [Path Selection with Path Synchronization - Library Paths](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectsynclibr_dialog.htm) | [Channel Properties](../dlgshell/dlgchnproperties_dialog.htm) | [External Editor](../dlgshell/dlgexternaleditor_dialog.htm) | [Logfile](../dlgshell/dlglogfile_dialog.htm) | [Data Area](../dlgshell/dlgconfdataarea_dialog.htm) | [Colors](../dlgshell/userdefinedcolors_dialog.htm) | [Compatibility](../dlgshell/dlgconfcompatibility64_dialog.htm) | [Preview Features](../dlgshell/dlgconffeatures_dialog.htm)

[NAVIGATOR](../../dlgnavigator/dlgnavigator/dlgconfdata_dialog.htm) | [VIEW](../../dlgview/dlgview/view_conf_dialog.htm) | [ANALYSIS](../../dlgmaths/calc_menu_dlg/dlgconfanalysis_dialog.htm) | [REPORT](../../dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlgconfgraph_dialog.htm) | [DAC/VISUAL](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_menu/dlgconfdac_dialog.htm) | [SCRIPT](../../dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dlgconfauto_dialog.htm)

- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselectlibr_dialog.htm`
