DIAdem Settings: Path Selection - Library Paths

Use this dialog box to specify the default paths for the [Library folders](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_directories.htm). The settings apply to the default settings of the load and save dialog boxes, immediately after DIAdem launches.

#### Settings

|  | Library paths | Specifies the library paths. In the standard configuration DIAdem loads the default files of the DIAdem panels from the library paths. If you specify a file without a path in a load command and if the file you want to load is not in the current user paths, DIAdem tries to load the file from the library path. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | File type | Specifies the file type for which you specify the load path and the save path. The default setting has two paths. The first path specifies the data path and the second path specifies the path for all other files. Data files include files such as TDM files and DAT files. Other files, for example, are layouts for DIAdem VIEW and DIAdem REPORT, scripts, user dialog boxes, media such as graphics files and video files, and configuration files for search definitions and import filters and export filters. |
|  | Find | Opens the dialog box where you specify the library folders. |

|  | Note If you do not specify a drive, you can specify paths relative to the program path. For example, if DIAdem is installed on C:\\DIAdem and you specify the path MyPath\\Documents, DIAdem uses the path C:\\DIAdem\\MyPath\\Documents. |
| --- | --- |
|  | Note You cannot change the predefined paths with a script. |
|  | Note DIAdem saves the paths that are predefined in this dialog box in the Desktop file. The DIAdem standard desktop file uses the wildcard CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS in the path specification. This wildcard corresponds with the path to the folder Shared Documents. By default this path is at C:\\Users\\Public\\.In the path settings you can use all constants that are described in the SHGetFolderCSIDL and SHGetFolderPath variables. Enclose the constants in % signs, for example, %CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS%. You also can use Windows environment variables.Click here for a list of the most important path variables. |
|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»DIAdem Settings»Library Paths. |

## TOPIC 00650: DIAdem Settings: Path Selection with Path Synchronization

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselectsync_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselectsync_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[General Dialog Boxes](../dlgshell/gendialogs_overview.htm) > [DIAdem Settings](../dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm) > DIAdem Settings: Path Selection with Path Synchronization

DIAdem Settings: Path Selection with Path Synchronization

Use this dialog box to specify the default paths for the [User folders](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_directories.htm). These settings apply to the default settings of the load and save dialog boxes, immediately after DIAdem launches. Some settings are only visible in the **Extended** mode when you enable **Path configuration**.

#### Settings

|  | Path behavior | Specifies whether you use the standard path behavior or the extended path behavior. In the Standard mode you can specify the path for the data and the path for all other documents. In the Extended mode you can specify all paths separately. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Synchronize paths | Specifies whether DIAdem hides or shows the additional column Synchronize Paths where you assign several paths to one group. |
|  | User paths | Specifies the default setting of the paths from which DIAdem loads files and into which DIAdem saves files. As soon as you load a file from a different path into a load dialog box or save a file to a different path in a save dialog box, DIAdem changes the respective user paths. The default setting that DIAdem uses when the program launches remains unchanged.The predefined user path is by default at C:\\Users\\Public\\. All users can read files from or write files into this path under Windows Vista. |
|  | File type | Specifies the file type for which you specify the load path and the save path. The default setting has two paths. The first path specifies the data path and the second path specifies the path for all other files. Data files include files such as TDM files and DAT files. Other files, for example, are layouts for DIAdem VIEW and DIAdem REPORT, scripts, user dialog boxes, media such as graphics files and video files, and configuration files for search definitions and import filters and export filters. |
|  | Load / Save | Specifies whether you set the load file or the save file. DIAdem assigns the load paths and the save paths to the same path. |
|  | Find | Opens the dialog box where you specify the user folder. |
|  | Synchronize paths | Specifies the group of which DIAdem synchronizes the paths. If you change a path of one group, DIAdem automatically adjusts all other paths of the same group to this path. You can assign several paths to one group. For example, if you assign the read layout path and the write layout file to the same group, DIAdem displays the same path, when loading or saving layouts, in the respective dialog boxes.DIAdem assigns the load paths and the save paths to the same group.This setting is visible in the Extended mode when you select Synchronize paths. |

|  | Note If you do not specify a drive, you can specify paths relative to the program path. For example, if DIAdem is installed on C:\\DIAdem and you specify the path MyPath\\Documents, DIAdem uses the path C:\\DIAdem\\MyPath\\Documents. |
| --- | --- |
|  | Note You cannot change the predefined paths with a script. |
|  | Note DIAdem saves the paths that are predefined in this dialog box in the Desktop file. The DIAdem standard desktop file uses the wildcard CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS in the path specification. This wildcard corresponds with the path to the folder Shared Documents. By default this path is at C:\\Users\\Public\\.In the path settings you can use all constants that are described in the SHGetFolderCSIDL and SHGetFolderPath variables. Enclose the constants in % signs, for example, %CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS%. You also can use Windows environment variables.Click here for a list of the most important path variables. |
|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»DIAdem Settings»Select Path. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm) | [Path Selection](../dlgshell/dlgpathselect_dialog.htm) | Path Selection with Path Synchronization | [Path Selection - Library Paths](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectlibr_dialog.htm) | [Path Selection with Path Synchronization - Library Paths](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectsynclibr_dialog.htm) | [Channel Properties](../dlgshell/dlgchnproperties_dialog.htm) | [External Editor](../dlgshell/dlgexternaleditor_dialog.htm) | [Logfile](../dlgshell/dlglogfile_dialog.htm) | [Data Area](../dlgshell/dlgconfdataarea_dialog.htm) | [Colors](../dlgshell/userdefinedcolors_dialog.htm) | [Compatibility](../dlgshell/dlgconfcompatibility64_dialog.htm) | [Preview Features](../dlgshell/dlgconffeatures_dialog.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselectsynclibr_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00651: DIAdem Settings: Path Selection with Path Synchronization - Library Paths

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselectsynclibr_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgshell/dlgshell/dlgpathselectsynclibr_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[General Dialog Boxes](../dlgshell/gendialogs_overview.htm) > [DIAdem Settings](../dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm) > [Path Selection with Path Synchronization](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectsync_dialog.htm) > DIAdem Settings: Path Selection with Path Synchronization - Library Paths

DIAdem Settings: Path Selection with Path Synchronization - Library Paths

Use this dialog box to specify the default paths for the [Library folders](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_directories.htm). These settings apply to the default settings of the load and save dialog boxes, immediately after DIAdem launches. Some settings are only visible if you select the **Extended** mode in the [Select Path](../dlgshell/dlgpathselect_dialog.htm) dialog box and also enable the **Synchronize paths setting**.

#### Settings

|  | Library paths | Specifies the library paths. In the standard configuration DIAdem loads the default files of the DIAdem panels from the library paths. If you specify a file without a path in a load command and if the file you want to load is not in the current user paths, DIAdem tries to load the file from the library path. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | File type | Specifies the file type for which you specify the load path and the save path. The default setting has two paths. The first path specifies the data path and the second path specifies the path for all other files. Data files include files such as TDM files and DAT files. Other files, for example, are layouts for DIAdem VIEW and DIAdem REPORT, scripts, user dialog boxes, media such as graphics files and video files, and configuration files for search definitions and import filters and export filters. |
|  | Find | Opens the dialog box where you specify the library folders. |
|  | Synchronize paths | Specifies the group of which DIAdem synchronizes the paths. If you change a path of one group, DIAdem automatically adjusts all other paths of the same group to this path. You can assign several paths to one group. For example, if you assign the read layout path and the write layout file to the same group, DIAdem displays the same path, when loading or saving layouts, in the respective dialog boxes.DIAdem assigns the load paths and the save paths to the same group.This setting is visible in the Extended mode when you select Synchronize paths. |

|  | Note If you do not specify a drive, you can specify paths relative to the program path. For example, if DIAdem is installed on C:\\DIAdem and you specify the path MyPath\\Documents, DIAdem uses the path C:\\DIAdem\\MyPath\\Documents. |
| --- | --- |
|  | Note You cannot change the predefined paths with a script. |
|  | Note DIAdem saves the paths that are predefined in this dialog box in the Desktop file. The DIAdem standard desktop file uses the wildcard CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS in the path specification. This wildcard corresponds with the path to the folder Shared Documents. By default this path is at C:\\Users\\Public\\.In the path settings you can use all constants that are described in the SHGetFolderCSIDL and SHGetFolderPath variables. Enclose the constants in % signs, for example, %CSIDL_COMMON_DOCUMENTS%. You also can use Windows environment variables.Click here for a list of the most important path variables. |
|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»DIAdem Settings»Library Paths. |

#### Further Settings

[General](../dlgshell/dlgconfshell_dialog.htm) | [Path Selection](../dlgshell/dlgpathselect_dialog.htm) | [Path Selection with Path Synchronization](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectsync_dialog.htm) | [Path Selection - Library Paths](../dlgshell/dlgpathselectlibr_dialog.htm) | Path Selection with Path Synchronization - Library Paths | [Channel Properties](../dlgshell/dlgchnproperties_dialog.htm) | [External Editor](../dlgshell/dlgexternaleditor_dialog.htm) | [Logfile](../dlgshell/dlglogfile_dialog.htm) | [Data Area](../dlgshell/dlgconfdataarea_dialog.htm) | [Colors](../dlgshell/userdefinedcolors_dialog.htm) | [Compatibility](../dlgshell/dlgconfcompatibility64_dialog.htm) | [Preview Features](../dlgshell/dlgconffeatures_dialog.htm)

[NAVIGATOR](../../dlgnavigator/dlgnavigator/dlgconfdata_dialog.htm) | [VIEW](../../dlgview/dlgview/view_conf_dialog.htm) | [ANALYSIS](../../dlgmaths/calc_menu_dlg/dlgconfanalysis_dialog.htm) | [REPORT](../../dlgpresent/graph_dlg_menu/dlgconfgraph_dialog.htm) | [DAC/VISUAL](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_menu/dlgconfdac_dialog.htm) | [SCRIPT](../../dlgscript/script_dlg_menu/dlgconfauto_dialog.htm)

Manage Worksheets

Use this dialog box to manage worksheets. You can also create, delete, and rename worksheets in the context menu of the tabs. Double-click on the right side of the last tab in the panel to create a new worksheet.

## TOPIC 00655: Table: Columns

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_column_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_column_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [Table](../dlgsud/table_dlgs_overview.htm) > Table: Columns

Table: Columns

Use this dialog box to specify the properties of the columns in a table in the dialog editor. Click **Columns** in the **Properties** tab to modify the properties of the table columns in the dialog editor..

The contents of a table can be read from or written into vector or matrix variables. In vector variables, each column in the table represents a vector. In matrix variables, you can use the table property [VerticalOrientation](../../sudref/properties/sud_property_verticalorientation_totablectrl.htm) to specify whether DIAdem fills table columns rowwise or columnwise.

#### Settings

| Columns | Displays an overview of all the columns in the table. |
| --- | --- |
| Title | Specifies the column title. |
| Column width | Specifies the column width. |
| Read-only | Specifies that the cells can be edited. |
| Column type | Specifies whether cells appear as edit boxes or selection boxes (read-only). |
| Variable | Specifies the vector variable or the matrix variable for a column. You can enter the variable name or select the variable name from the list. If you enter the variable name, DIAdem automatically opens the dialog box for Variable definitions. |
| Variable length | Specifies the number of variable elements. |
| Offset | Specifies the index that the column display starts at. |
| Row/column | Matrix variable: specifies whether the column or the row of a matrix is used. |
| Index | Matrix variable: specifies the displayed columns or rows within a matrix. |
| New Entry | Adds a column. |
| Entries | Deletes or inserts one or more columns. |
| Delete | Deletes a column. |
| Up/Down | Moves a column. |
| Cells | Specifies the value of table cells. |

|  | Note The Columns property returns the total of all the columns. |
| --- | --- |
|  | Note If you use the row and column to specify the position, you refer to the original table order. The order remains unchanged when you move columns or rows interactively, or when you use the Swap method. The DisplayedLocation property contains the position where the row or column is displayed in the table. |

## TOPIC 00656: Extended Table: Column Configuration

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_columns_xtable_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_columns_xtable_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [XTable](../dlgsud/xtable_dlgs_overview.htm) > Extended Table: Column Configuration

Extended Table: Column Configuration

Use this dialog box to generate or to delete the columns of an extended table in the dialog editor, or to modify the display. Click **Columns** on the **Properties** tab to configure the table columns.

The overview in this dialog box shows you the defined columns and the types of the controls that are assigned to the columns. You can assign the following types of controls to the columns of the extended table: [Butto](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tobtnrteob_xtable.htm)n, [CheckBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tocheckrt_xtable.htm), [ChnComboBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tochncomboboxctrl_xtable.htm), [ChnListBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tochnlistboxctrl_xtable.htm), [ComboBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tocombort_xtable.htm), [EditBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_toeditctrlob_xtable.htm), [ListBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tolistboxrt_xtable.htm), or [Text](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tostaticctrlrt_xtable.htm).

In the lower part of the dialog box you specify which of the controls is assigned the <Default> type.

Click **Add** or **Entries** to create more table columns. New columns always have the type <Default>. If you want to change the control type for a single column, select the respective line in the overview and then change the type and/or column width for this entry.

#### Settings

|  | Columns | Displays an overview of all the columns in the extended table. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Name | Specifies the name of the column that is selected in the overview. |
|  | Cell type | Specifies the type of the control that is assigned to the selected column in the overview. |
|  | Open Dialog Box | Opens the dialog box where you specify the properties of the control to be displayed. |
|  | Column width | Specifies the width of the column that is selected in the overview. |
|  | <Default> cell type | Specifies the type of the control that is assigned to all the columns that are type <Default>. |
|  | <Default> ... | Opens the dialog box where you specify the properties of the <Default> control. |
|  | <Default> column width | Specifies the width of the <Default> control. |
|  | Add | Adds a <Default> type column. |
|  | Entries | Opens the dialog box where you can add <Default> type columns to the extended table or where you can delete these columns. |
|  | Delete | Deletes a column. |
|  | Up/Down | Moves a column. |

#### Procedures

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_controls_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00657: Controls

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_controls_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_controls_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [General](../dlgsud/sud_general.htm) > Controls

Controls

User dialog boxes consist of [controls](../../sudref/objects/sud_control_overview.htm) such as buttons, entry fields, selection lists, or graphics. Define the appearance of the user dialog boxes in the dialog editor workspace. Take the controls from the control bar and adjust the position and size in the workspace. You can edit some of the control properties in the workspace, such as button labels. Use [properties](../../sudref/properties/sud_property_overview.htm) to specify the appearance and behavior of the controls. Use [ActiveX controls](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_togenericocx.htm) to integrate dialog box elements from other programs.

Controls respond to [events](../../sudref/events/sud_event_overview.htm) such as mouse clicks. When an event occurs, DIAdem calls a script to respond to the associated event. In this event procedure you can modify properties to hide controls, for example, and you can call [methods](../../sudref/methods/sud_method_overview.htm) to close the dialog box.

Use the [properties window](../dlgsud/sud_properties_dialog.htm) to make other control settings. The properties window contains a selection list with the names of all the controls in the user dialog box, a tab with the properties, and a tab with the events for the selected control. If you select several controls in the workspace, the words **Multi-selection** appear in the selection list instead of the name. When you make multiple selections, the properties window only shows the common properties.

Use the [catalog window](../dlgsud/sud_catalog_dialog.htm) to save controls or control groups. DIAdem saves controls with their properties and events, in the catalog. Use the context menu of the catalog to select and edit symbols, to select various catalog views, and to create, open, and close catalogs.

Click [here](../../sudref/objects/tosudviewobint_objects_overview.htm) to view the structure of the controls that are available in the dialog editor.

#### Procedures

## TOPIC 00658: Converting User Dialog Boxes

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_convert.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_convert.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [Script View of the Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_script_dialog.htm) > Converting User Dialog Boxes

Converting User Dialog Boxes

In DIAdem Version 2010 the configuration of the event procedures was changed. The definition of the This variable was moved to the parameter list of the event procedure. Now event procedures always receive the object that triggers this event as the first parameter. The following example shows the syntax of the event procedure for initializing the dialog box:

| Syntax before DIAdem 2010 | Syntax as of DIAdem 2010 |
| --- | --- |
| Sub_Dialog_EventIlnitialize Dim This : Set This = Dialog This.Color = RGB(255, 0, 0) End Sub | Sub Dialog_EventClick(ByRef This) This.Color = RGB(255, 0, 0) End Sub |

To open a dialog box file that was created with an earlier DIAdem version DIAdem must reconvert the scripts of all event procedures. During this conversion process DIAdem creates a logfile with the same name and the extension _log.hml. If you also have to manually adjust the scripts of the event procedures in the converted dialog box file, the logfile contains an additional note.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_customflex_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00659: Flex Properties

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_customflex_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_customflex_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [General](../dlgsud/sud_general.htm) > Flex Properties

Flex Properties

Use this dialog box to specify the change in the size and position of the control when you vertically scale a user dialog box during runtime.

The dialog box settings only have an effect if you assign the value 1 - Yes to the [Resizeable](../../sudref/properties/sud_property_resizeable_tosudviewob.htm) dialog box property.

If you assign different flex properties to the individual controls, the relative position of the controls changes when the user dialog box is scaled. For example, you can move buttons automatically to make room for a resizing textbox.

If a control is in a tab, the size, position, or flex properties change according to the TabPageCtrl control, not according to the user dialog box.

#### Settings

| Horizontal |  |
| --- | --- |

| None | The width of the control and the distance from the left edge of the user dialog box remain the same. |
| --- | --- |
| Shift | Moves the control horizontally, without scaling the width. The distance between the control and the right edge of the user dialog box does not change. |
| Expand | Scales the width of the control proportionally to the user dialog box, without modifying the distance from the control to the left edge of the user dialog box. |

| Customized | Scales and moves the control in horizontal direction in relation to the settings Left(%) and Right(%). |
| --- | --- |
| Vertical |  |
| None | The height of the control and the distance from the top edge of the user dialog box remain the same. |
| Shift | Moves the control vertically, without scaling the height. The distance between the control and the bottom edge of the user dialog box does not change. |
| Expand | Scales the height of the control proportionally to the user dialog box, without modifying the distance from the control to the top edge of the user dialog box. |

| Customized | Scales and moves the control in horizontal direction in relation to the settings Top(%) and Bottom(%). |
| --- | --- |
|  |  |
| Top (%) | Specifies how the change in the dialog box size influences, as a percentage, the property Top. |
| Left (%) | Specifies how the change in the dialog box size influences, as a percentage, the property Left. |
| Right (%) | Specifies how the change in the dialog box size influences, as a percentage, the property Right. |
| Bottom (%) | Specifies how the change in the dialog box size influences, as a percentage, the property Bottom. |

#### Procedures

[Checking a User Dialog Box Entry](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_input.htm) | [Creating a Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_dynamic.htm) | [Creating a Procedure in the Script of a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_declaration.htm) | [Creating a User Dialog Box without Linking Variables](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_withoutvar.htm) | [Creating an Extended Table](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_xtable.htm) | [Displaying Graphics in Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_picture.htm) | [Enabling Controls](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_enable.htm) | [Opening the Dialog Editor](../../procscript/procscript/procscript_generating_userdialog.htm) | [Responding to User Entries in User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_event.htm) | [Saving and Restoring the Last Dialog Box Position](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_savedlgpos.htm) | [Saving Control Groups for User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_catalog.htm) | [Specifying the Default Button](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_defaultbutton.htm) | [Tabulator Order in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_tab.htm) | [Using a Script to Fill a Selection List](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_fill.htm) | [Using Channel Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_chnbox.htm) | [Using Hotkeys in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_accelerator.htm) | [Using the Flex Properties](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_flex.htm)

#### Examples

## TOPIC 00662: The Dialog Editor

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_general.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_general.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > The Dialog Editor

The Dialog Editor

Use the dialog editor to create your own user dialog boxes. You can define [modal and non-modal user dialog boxes](../../genscript/genscript/sud_nonmodal.htm). Use the [SUDDlgShow](../../comoff/suddlgshow.htm) command to call a modal user dialog box and the [SUDDlgCreate](../../comoff/suddlgcreate.htm) command to call a non-modal dialog box. Use variables to connect user dialog boxes to DIAdem, to make default settings in the user dialog box, or to process the return values.

User dialog boxes consist of [controls](../../sudref/objects/sud_control_overview.htm) such as buttons, entry fields, selection lists, or graphics. Define the appearance of the user dialog boxes in the dialog editor workspace. Take the controls from the control bar and adjust the position and size in the workspace. You can edit some of the control properties in the workspace, such as button labels. Use [properties](../../sudref/properties/sud_property_overview.htm) to specify the appearance and behavior of the controls. Use [ActiveX controls](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_togenericocx.htm) to integrate dialog box elements from other programs.

Controls react to [events](../../sudref/events/sud_event_overview.htm), such as a mouse click. If an event occurs, DIAdem calls the associated event procedure to react to the event. In this event procedure you can modify properties to hide controls, for example, and you can call [methods](../../sudref/methods/sud_method_overview.htm) to close the dialog box.

Use the [properties window](../dlgsud/sud_properties_dialog.htm) to make other control settings. The properties window contains a selection list with the names of all the controls in the user dialog box, a tab with the properties, and a tab with the events for the selected control. If you select several controls in the workspace, the words **Multi-selection** appear in the selection list instead of the name. When you make multiple selections, the properties window only shows the common properties.

Use the [script view](../dlgsud/sud_script_dialog.htm) to edit the event procedure that DIAdem runs when the event occurs. First select the control and then the event. The properties window is not visible in the script view.

You can save several dialog boxes in one user dialog box file. Use the [dialog box overview](../dlgsud/sud_dialogoverview_dialog.htm) to view the list of all the user dialog boxes a dialog box file, and to display or to delete individual dialog boxes. If you want to open a dialog box file created with DIAdem version 11.1 or earlier in the dialog box editor, DIAdem must first [convert](../dlgsud/sud_convert.htm) this file.

Use the [catalog window](../dlgsud/sud_catalog_dialog.htm) to save controls or control groups. DIAdem saves controls with their properties and events, in the catalog. Use the context menu of the catalog to select and edit symbols, to select various catalog views, and to create, open, and close catalogs.

Select **Dialog Box»Copy** to copy the dialog box with all the controls, properties, and methods to the clipboard. Select **Dialog Box»Paste** to paste the dialog box from the clipboard. The pasted dialog box is then in the dialog box overview.

#### Procedures

[Checking a User Dialog Box Entry](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_input.htm) | [Creating a Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_dynamic.htm) | [Creating a Procedure in the Script of a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_declaration.htm) | [Creating a User Dialog Box without Linking Variables](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_withoutvar.htm) | [Creating an Extended Table](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_xtable.htm) | [Displaying Graphics in Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_picture.htm) | [Enabling Controls](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_enable.htm) | [Opening the Dialog Editor](../../procscript/procscript/procscript_generating_userdialog.htm) | [Responding to User Entries in User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_event.htm) | [Saving and Restoring the Last Dialog Box Position](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_savedlgpos.htm) | [Saving Control Groups for User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_catalog.htm) | [Specifying the Default Button](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_defaultbutton.htm) | [Tabulator Order in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_tab.htm) | [Using a Script to Fill a Selection List](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_fill.htm) | [Using Channel Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_chnbox.htm) | [Using Hotkeys in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_accelerator.htm) | [Using the Flex Properties](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_flex.htm)

#### Examples

[Analyzing and Displaying Channels Section by Section](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewdisplaychnparts.htm) | [Checking Dialog Box Entries](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av16.htm) | [Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av11.htm) | [Translating User Dialog Boxes](../../exploff/examples/example_sud_translate.htm) | [User Dialog Box for Entering Text and Numbers](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av2.htm) | [User Dialog Box for Sequence Control](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av13.htm) | [User Dialog Box in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewcreatecurve.htm) | [User Dialog Box in VIEW for the Calculation of the FFT and Harmonic Frequencies](../../exploff/examples/view_fft_analysis.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Changing Background Color](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av9.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Curve Preview and Slider Control](../../exploff/examples/expl_curve2dpreview.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Extended Table](../../exploff/examples/expl_weather_info.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Internet Explorer](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av22.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Scalable Table](../../exploff/examples/expl_zoom_xtable_example.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Selection Lists](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av7.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Selection Lists](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av8.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Subdialog Boxes](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av12.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Tables](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av10.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Tree](../../exploff/examples/expl_treecontrol.htm) | [Wizard for Tolerance Evaluation](../../exploff/examples/expl_tolerance.htm)

Dialog Editor

Dialog Editor

## TOPIC 00664: Grid Settings

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_grid_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_grid_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [General](../dlgsud/sud_general.htm) > Grid Settings

Grid Settings

Use this dialog box to set the grid and the guides for positioning controls in the dialog editor.

#### Settings

| Display grid | Makes the grid visible or invisible. |
| --- | --- |
| Snap controls to grid | Aligns new controls to grid. |
| Guides | Specifies the distance from the guides to the edge in pixels. If you enter 0, the guide is invisible. |
| Width | Specifies the grid width in pixels. |
| Height | Specifies the grid height in pixels. |

|  | Note If you press <Ctrl> and the arrow keys, DIAdem moves the control in grid steps. If you press <Alt> and move the mouse, DIAdem moves the control freely, not in grid steps. If you press <Shift> and the arrow keys, DIAdem zooms the controls in and out. If you press the keys <Ctrl> or <Shift>, DIAdem zooms the control in or out when you press the arrow keys in grid steps. If you press <Ctrl> and move the control with the mouse, DIAdem copies the control. |
| --- | --- |

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_layer_dialog.htm`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [General](../dlgsud/sud_general.htm) > Layer

Layer

Use this dialog box to organize controls at different layers in the dialog editor. You can hide layers or controls while you work in the dialog editor.

#### Settings

| Layer | Lists all layers of the user dialog box. |
| --- | --- |
| Name | Specifies the name of the selected layer. |
| Visible | Switches the view of the selected layer on and off. You cannot make entries in invisible layers. |
| Add | Adds a new layer. |
| Delete | Deletes the selected layer. |
| Up/Down | Changes the order of the layers. |
| Select | Selects all the objects of the specified layer to show which objects belong to this layer. The selection is cancelled when you make a new selection or close the dialog box. |

|  | Note The dialog editor inserts new controls in the selected layer. When the selected layer is locked, you cannot add controls. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note Use the Layer property to make each layer visible or invisible during run time. |
| --- | --- |

| Delete | Deletes the selected entry. |
| Up/Down | Moves the position of an entry in the list. |

## TOPIC 00667: Picture Definition

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_picturedefinition_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_picturedefinition_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [Picture](../dlgsud/picture_dlgs_overview.htm) > Picture Definition

Picture Definition

Use this dialog box to load a graphic from a file, to paste a graphic from the clipboard, or to generate a graphic, in the dialog editor. This dialog box opens when you insert a graphic into a user dialog box or click **Picture** in the dialog editor.

#### Settings

| Filename | Shows the filename and the path. |
| --- | --- |
| Transparency | Specifies the transparency color. DIAdem displays the transparent color in the color of the dialog box background. If you load a graphics file, in which one color is defined as transparent, you can select Automatic transparency. |
| Embed picture | Embeds a graphic or saves a reference to the file. |
| Copy | Copies the current graphic into the clipboard. |
| Paste | Inserts a graphic from the clipboard. |
| Load | Opens the dialog box for loading a graphic. You can load the following file formats for graphics: *.EMF, *.WMF, *.ICO, *.BMP, *.DIP, *.TIF, *.JPG, *.PNG, *.PCX, *.PSD, *.TGS, *.RAS, *.EPS, *.WPG, *.PCT, and *.GIF. Note On Windows, you can set the screen scaling or DPI value to another value than 100%, such as 150% or 200%. With higher scaling under Windows, graphics in DIAdem dialog boxes might be very small. To display graphics in DIAdem with the screen scaling in the correct size, you can save these graphics in the same folder as the original file, but with the same file name and the postfix _pct150 or _pct200 . DIAdem automatically selects the appropriate file depending on the Windows scaling factor. The graphics in these files must be scaled according to the scaling factor set under Windows.For example, if the screen scaling is 150 % and you select the file image.jpg in the Picture Definition dialog box and the same folder also contains the file image_150pct.jpg for a scaling factor of 150%, DIAdem automatically uses the file image_pct150.jpg instead of the initially selected file image.jpg. The picture must not be embedded. |
|  | Note On Windows, you can set the screen scaling or DPI value to another value than 100%, such as 150% or 200%. With higher scaling under Windows, graphics in DIAdem dialog boxes might be very small. To display graphics in DIAdem with the screen scaling in the correct size, you can save these graphics in the same folder as the original file, but with the same file name and the postfix _pct150 or _pct200 . DIAdem automatically selects the appropriate file depending on the Windows scaling factor. The graphics in these files must be scaled according to the scaling factor set under Windows.For example, if the screen scaling is 150 % and you select the file image.jpg in the Picture Definition dialog box and the same folder also contains the file image_150pct.jpg for a scaling factor of 150%, DIAdem automatically uses the file image_pct150.jpg instead of the initially selected file image.jpg. The picture must not be embedded. |
| Delete | Deletes the current graphic. |
| Edit | Opens a dialog box for editing a graphic. |

|  | Note You can embed graphics into the user dialog box or save them as a file reference. You can use both absolute paths, for example, c:\\sud\\test.bmp, or relative paths, ..\\sud\\test.bmp. If you do not enter a path, DIAdem browses the following paths: Path of the dialog box file DIAdem SCRIPT user path DIAdem SCRIPT library path DIAdem program path |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note In the dialog editor, you only can scale a graphic if the Layout property has the value 3 - Stretch. Press <Shift> to keep the height-width ratio when scaling. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00668: Properties and Events Window

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_properties_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_properties_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [General](../dlgsud/sud_general.htm) > Properties and Events Window

Properties and Events Window

Use the **Properties** tab in the properties window to modify size, position, and display settings for a control. You can modify most [properties](../../sudref/properties/sud_property_overview.htm) in scripts while the user dialog box is running, and in the dialog editor when you generate the user dialog box. To initialize a control, you preset the variable that is assigned to the control before you open the user dialog box, or you assign a value to the control in the [EventInitialize](../../sudref/events/sud_event_eventinitialize.htm) event. The properties window always displays the properties of the selected control. If you select several controls in the workspace, the properties window only displays the common properties.

Use the **Events** tab in the properties window to assign [Events](../../sudref/events/sud_event_overview.htm) to a control. For example, the events might respond to mouse-clicks or to mouse movements. These events also may enable a certain control in a script, or hide a control.

Use the **ActiveX** tab in the properties window to modify special properties of an [ActiveX control](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_togenericocx.htm).

#### Procedures

[Checking a User Dialog Box Entry](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_input.htm) | [Creating a Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_dynamic.htm) | [Creating a Procedure in the Script of a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_declaration.htm) | [Creating a User Dialog Box without Linking Variables](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_withoutvar.htm) | [Creating an Extended Table](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_xtable.htm) | [Displaying Graphics in Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_picture.htm) | [Enabling Controls](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_enable.htm) | [Opening the Dialog Editor](../../procscript/procscript/procscript_generating_userdialog.htm) | [Responding to User Entries in User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_event.htm) | [Saving and Restoring the Last Dialog Box Position](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_savedlgpos.htm) | [Saving Control Groups for User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_catalog.htm) | [Specifying the Default Button](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_defaultbutton.htm) | [Tabulator Order in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_tab.htm) | [Using a Script to Fill a Selection List](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_fill.htm) | [Using Channel Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_chnbox.htm) | [Using Hotkeys in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_accelerator.htm) | [Using the Flex Properties](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_flex.htm)

#### Examples

[Analyzing and Displaying Channels Section by Section](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewdisplaychnparts.htm) | [Checking Dialog Box Entries](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av16.htm) | [Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av11.htm) | [Translating User Dialog Boxes](../../exploff/examples/example_sud_translate.htm) | [User Dialog Box for Entering Text and Numbers](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av2.htm) | [User Dialog Box for Sequence Control](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av13.htm) | [User Dialog Box in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewcreatecurve.htm) | [User Dialog Box in VIEW for the Calculation of the FFT and Harmonic Frequencies](../../exploff/examples/view_fft_analysis.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Changing Background Color](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av9.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Curve Preview and Slider Control](../../exploff/examples/expl_curve2dpreview.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Extended Table](../../exploff/examples/expl_weather_info.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Internet Explorer](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av22.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Scalable Table](../../exploff/examples/expl_zoom_xtable_example.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Selection Lists](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av7.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Selection Lists](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av8.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Subdialog Boxes](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av12.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Tables](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av10.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Tree](../../exploff/examples/expl_treecontrol.htm) | [Wizard for Tolerance Evaluation](../../exploff/examples/expl_tolerance.htm)

## TOPIC 00669: Bitmap Sizes

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_resizebitmap_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_resizebitmap_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [Picture](../dlgsud/picture_dlgs_overview.htm) > Bitmap Sizes

Bitmap Sizes

Use this dialog box to edit the size and the color depth for graphics in the dialog editor.

#### Settings

| Width | Specifies the width in pixels. |
| --- | --- |
| Height | Specifies the height in pixels. |
| Reduce to selection | Reduces the size to the selected area. |
| Colors | Specifies the color depth. |

|  | Note The picture definition dialog box appears when you insert a graphic into a user dialog box and click Edit in the picture definition. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00670: Table: Rows

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_row_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_row_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [Table](../dlgsud/table_dlgs_overview.htm) > Table: Rows

Table: Rows

Use this dialog box to specify the properties of the rows in a table in the dialog editor. Click **Rows** on the **Properties** tab to modify the table row properties in the dialog editor.

#### Settings

| Rows | Displays an overview of all the rows in the table. |
| --- | --- |
| Title | Specifies the title of the row. |
| Width | Specifies the column width if rows and columns are exchanged. Use the VerticalOrientation property to exchange rows and columns. |
| New Entry | Adds a row. |
| Entries | Deletes or inserts one or more rows. |
| Delete | Deletes a row. |
| Up/Down | Moves a row. |
| Cells | Specifies the value of table cells. |

|  | Note The Rows property returns the total of all the rows. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note If you use the row and column to specify the position, you refer to the original table order. The order remains unchanged when you move columns or rows interactively, or when you use the Swap method. The DisplayedLocation property contains the position where the row or column is displayed in the table. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00671: Script View of the Dialog Editor

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_script_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_script_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > Script View of the Dialog Editor

Script View of the Dialog Editor

Use the script view of the dialog editor to create event procedures. To open the script view double-click the dialog box or a control, or select **View»Script View**.

By default the event view is in the right area of the script view. You can hide or show the event view via **View»Events**. The events view shows a tree view of the dialog box, the controls, and the events. Use the plus and minus signs or select **Collapse All Sub-Levels** and **Expand All Sub-Levels** from the context menu to show or to hide the events in the tree view.

Each control is assigned events that the control responds to. Each event is connected to an event procedure. Event procedures always receive the object as the first parameter in the This variable. If an event occurs, DIAdem performs the associated event procedure. The events respond to user actions such as a mouse-move, a mouse-click, or changing a value in a control. DIAdem also has events that respond when you initialize a dialog box or close a dialog box. Event procedures can execute calculations or actions, change properties, or call other events. You also can access DIAdem variables and commands in an event procedure. For example, use the [ScriptInclude](../../comoff/scriptinclude.htm) command in an event procedure in order to use the functions of existing scripts.

To connect a control to an event select the event in the tree view, select **Create Event** from the context menu, and fill the associated procedure with statements. DIAdem displays the events for which an event procedure is defined in bold. To open the associated event procedure in the script editor double-click the event in the tree view. The context menu also contains functions to create, open, and delete events.

[CodeCompletion](../../genscript/genscript/codecompletion.htm) supports you when you define the event procedures. If you press <Ctrl-Spacebar>, DIAdem displays all the objects, commands, and procedures that are available at this point in the script. You can use the increment/decrement arrow buttons to move up and down in the list. If you type a dot behind the name of an object, DIAdem displays all [properties](../../sudref/properties/sud_property_overview.htm) and [methods](../../sudref/methods/sud_method_overview.htm) that this object supports. Select the methods and properties from this list to use them in the editor. DIAdem displays further information on the selected identifier in the SmartInfo. You modify the presentation and the behavior of a control in the properties window. You use the methods to get values or to run actions. If DIAdem does not offer CodeCompletion for an ActiveX control, select in DIAdem SCRIPT **Script»Type Libraries** and enable the associated library in the [Registered Type Libraries](../../dlgscript/script_dlg_workspace/typelibrary_dialog.htm) dialog box which opens. After you have made changes in this dialog box you must restart the dialog editor.

Use the SmartInfo for information about DIAdem commands, variables, objects, properties, and methods. If you move the mouse across a DIAdem term or a DIAdem term from the CodeCompletion list, DIAdem displays the type, the parameters, and a short description in the SmartInfo. Click **Display Help on This Subject** in the SmartInfo to open the Help page. The displayed SmartInfo depends on the respective context. For example, DIAdem displays different SmartInfos for methods, which have the same names, but which are used in different object structures. DIAdem also displays the SmartInfo for user-defined variables to which DIAdem objects were assigned. If you can configure a command, a method, or a property, DIAdem displays the SmartInfo for the first parameter, after the opening parenthesis. DIAdem automatically displays SmartInfos on further parameters after you enter a comma. You can temporarily disable the SmartInfo display by pressing <Ctrl + Shift + T>. If you want to set the SmartInfo display permanently, use the [Properties](../../dlgscript/script_dlg_workspace/dlgfolderproperties_dialog.htm) dialog box. To access this dialog box, select **Settings»DIAdem Settings** in DIAdem SCRIPT and click **Properties**.

Also use the **Properties** dialog box to specify the general properties and the color display of the script editor. After you have made changes in this dialog box you must restart the dialog editor.

Select **View»Script- Bar** to show or to hide the bar that contains the editing functions of the event procedures. The script bar includes functions for searching and replacing text, for defining bookmarks, for commenting text, and also for showing the collapsed or expanded view of the script.

You can combine event procedures you need often in a separate script. You can access the separated event procedures in the script with the command ScriptInclude.

You can delete event procedures you no longer need. To do so, select the function **Delete Event** from the context menu in the event view or use the delete symbol on the left side of the event on the **Events** tab in the properties window. In both cases DIAdem comments out all lines of the event procedure in the script with an identifier. To delete these text lines permanently click **Delete the Lines Marked for Deletion** on the script bar.

If you only select the event procedure and press <Del> to delete the event procedure within the script, the event is preserved. If the event is called and an error occurs because DIAdem does not know the associated event procedure, an error message appears. DIAdem marks these events additionally in the event view with a blue exclamation mark. DIAdem also identifies events with a blue exclamation mark when the associated event procedure is in a different script and is integrated with the command ScriptInclude.

#### Procedures

[Checking a User Dialog Box Entry](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_input.htm) | [Creating a Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_dynamic.htm) | [Creating a Procedure in the Script of a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_declaration.htm) | [Creating a User Dialog Box without Linking Variables](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_withoutvar.htm) | [Creating an Extended Table](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_xtable.htm) | [Displaying Graphics in Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_picture.htm) | [Enabling Controls](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_enable.htm) | [Opening the Dialog Editor](../../procscript/procscript/procscript_generating_userdialog.htm) | [Responding to User Entries in User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_event.htm) | [Saving and Restoring the Last Dialog Box Position](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_savedlgpos.htm) | [Saving Control Groups for User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_catalog.htm) | [Specifying the Default Button](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_defaultbutton.htm) | [Tabulator Order in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_tab.htm) | [Using a Script to Fill a Selection List](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_fill.htm) | [Using Channel Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_chnbox.htm) | [Using Hotkeys in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_accelerator.htm) | [Using the Flex Properties](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_flex.htm)

#### Examples

[Analyzing and Displaying Channels Section by Section](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewdisplaychnparts.htm) | [Checking Dialog Box Entries](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av16.htm) | [Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av11.htm) | [Translating User Dialog Boxes](../../exploff/examples/example_sud_translate.htm) | [User Dialog Box for Entering Text and Numbers](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av2.htm) | [User Dialog Box for Sequence Control](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av13.htm) | [User Dialog Box in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewcreatecurve.htm) | [User Dialog Box in VIEW for the Calculation of the FFT and Harmonic Frequencies](../../exploff/examples/view_fft_analysis.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Changing Background Color](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av9.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Curve Preview and Slider Control](../../exploff/examples/expl_curve2dpreview.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Extended Table](../../exploff/examples/expl_weather_info.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Internet Explorer](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av22.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Scalable Table](../../exploff/examples/expl_zoom_xtable_example.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Selection Lists](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av7.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Selection Lists](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av8.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Subdialog Boxes](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av12.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Tables](../../exploff/examples/expl_script_av10.htm) | [User Dialog Box with Tree](../../exploff/examples/expl_treecontrol.htm) | [Wizard for Tolerance Evaluation](../../exploff/examples/expl_tolerance.htm)

## TOPIC 00673: Extended Table: Cell Type

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_type_columns_xtable_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_type_columns_xtable_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > [XTable](../dlgsud/xtable_dlgs_overview.htm) > Extended Table: Cell Type

Extended Table: Cell Type

In the [Configure columns](../dlgsud/sud_columns_xtable_dialog.htm) dialog box you assign a cell type to a column of the extended table. The cell type specifies what type of control is assigned to a column. [Button](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tobtnrteob_xtable.htm), [CheckBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tocheckrt_xtable.htm), [ChnComboBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tochncomboboxctrl_xtable.htm), [ChnListBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tochnlistboxctrl_xtable.htm), [ComboBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tocombort_xtable.htm), [EditBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_toeditctrlob_xtable.htm), [ListBox](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tolistboxrt_xtable.htm), or [Text](../../sudref/objects/sud_objects_tostaticctrlrt_xtable.htm) are valid cell types.

Two controls of the selected type are always assigned to a column in the extended table. The user dialog box uses the first control in the display mode of the extended table and the second control in the entry mode.

Use this dialog box to configure the properties of the two controls for the display mode and the entry mode. The properties list shows only the control properties that are useful in the display mode or in the entry mode in the extended table.

|  | Note You must use the ListItems property in the display mode and in the entry mode, to specify the selection terms for the controls ComboBox and ListBox. |
| --- | --- |
|  | Note Use the events EventColCtrlPreset and EventDefaultColCtrlPreset to initialize the controls in the script context. |

#### Settings

| Display control | Shows the properties that are available for the control in the display mode. |
| --- | --- |
| Entry control | Shows the properties that are available for the control in the entry mode. |

|  | Note Refer to the the DIAdem help for information on the properties, methods, and events of the controls. The control properties, which you also can set in this dialog box of the extended table, are identified accordingly in the DIAdem help. |
| --- | --- |

## TOPIC 00674: DIAdem Variables

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_variabledefinition_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgsud/dlgsud/sud_variabledefinition_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Dialog Editor](../dlgsud/sud_genoverview.htm) > DIAdem Variables

DIAdem Variables

Use this dialog box to display the properties of the registered variable, to enter new variables, or to delete existing variables. Click **New Entry** and enter any number of variables, which you can then use in the control properties. You assign a variable to a control in the properties window. Controls connected to these variables read their start values from the variables or write their input values into the variables. In user dialog boxes, you also can use vector variables and matrix variables. Use the properties VariableColIndex and VariableRowIndex to access these variables. The [WriteVariables](../../sudref/properties/sud_property_writevariables_tosudviewobint.htm) property of the user dialog box specifies the conditions under which modifications to the variable values are transferred to DIAdem.

#### Settings

| Storage mode | Specifies whether a variable is saved as a scalar, a vector, or a matrix. During dialog box runtime, the storage mode must be the same as the DIAdem storage mode. The dialog editor supports variables with a maximum of two dimensions (matrix). |
| --- | --- |
| Type | Specifies the type of variable. During the dialog box runtime, the type must be the same as the DIAdem variable type. |
| Name | Specifies the name of the variable that must exist in DIAdem during dialog box runtime. |
| In use | Specifies whether a control in the user dialog box uses the selected variable. |
| New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you define a new variable. |
| Edit | Opens the dialog box where you redefine the variable selected in the overview. |
| Delete | Deletes the selected variable. |
| Up/Down | Moves the position of the selected variable in the overview. |
| Redetermine | Connects to DIAdem and restores the default values for type, storage mode, dimensions, and reset behavior for DIAdem variables. DIAdem variables are all current internal variables, global variables, and variables from a user variable definition file. |

|  | Note You can use only DIAdem variables in the variable properties for the controls. In the properties for a control, you only can insert the variables that are the same data type as the control. For example, the dialog editor does not accept any real type variables for ComboBoxes. Refer to the page on Variable Types for Controls for a list of the variable types that you can assign to the various controls. |
| --- | --- |

[Checking a User Dialog Box Entry](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_input.htm) | [Creating a Dynamic User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_dynamic.htm) | [Creating a Procedure in the Script of a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_declaration.htm) | [Creating a User Dialog Box without Linking Variables](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_withoutvar.htm) | [Creating an Extended Table](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_xtable.htm) | [Displaying Graphics in Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_picture.htm) | [Enabling Controls](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_enable.htm) | [Opening the Dialog Editor](../../procscript/procscript/procscript_generating_userdialog.htm) | [Responding to User Entries in User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_event.htm) | [Saving and Restoring the Last Dialog Box Position](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_savedlgpos.htm) | [Saving Control Groups for User Dialog Boxes](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_catalog.htm) | [Specifying the Default Button](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_defaultbutton.htm) | [Tabulator Order in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_tab.htm) | [Using a Script to Fill a Selection List](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_fill.htm) | [Using Channel Selection Lists](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_chnbox.htm) | [Using Hotkeys in a User Dialog Box](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_accelerator.htm) | [Using the Flex Properties](../../procsud/procsud/procsud_flex.htm)

## TOPIC 00675: Add Unit Dimensions

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_create_unitdimension_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_create_unitdimension_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Units Catalog](../dlgunitcatalog/unitcatalog_dlgoverview.htm) > [Units](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_units_dialog.htm) > Add Unit Dimensions

Add Unit Dimensions

Use this dialog box to create a new dimension for the selected [physical quantity](../../genshell/genshell/genunitcatalog_basics.htm). DIAdem displays existing dimensions in gray with a filled square in the **Add** column. Select the empty square in the **Add** column to define a new dimension.

#### Settings

| Quantity | Specifies the physical quantity for which you create a new dimension. |
| --- | --- |
| Factor | Specifies the factor by which you multiply the base unit of the selected physical quantity. |
| Add | Specifies the name of the dimension. Select this checkbox to create a new dimension. |
| Symbol | Specifies the symbol of the new unit. To edit the symbol, double-click the cell. |
| Name | Specifies the name of the new unit. To edit the name, double-click the cell. |
| Description | Specifies the description of the new unit. To enter a new description, double-click the cell. |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»Units in any DIAdem panel, click the Units tab, and click the New Dimensions button. You must select the Display all defined units of the quantity checkbox before you click the button. |
| --- | --- |

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_delete_quantity_dialog.htm`

- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Units Catalog](../dlgunitcatalog/unitcatalog_dlgoverview.htm) > [Quantities](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_quantities_dialog.htm) > Delete Quantity

Delete Quantity

Use this dialog box to delete the assignment of a physical quantity to a [unit set](../../genshell/genshell/genunitcatalog.htm) or to delete a physical quantity from the units catalog entirely.

#### Settings

| Delete only the assignment to unit set | Deletes the assignment of the selected physical quantity to the unit set. The physical quantity remains in the units catalog and can be assigned to a different unit set. DIAdem displays this physical quantity if you select the Display all defined quantities checkbox on the Quantities tab. |
| --- | --- |
| Delete definition of the quantity with all unit set assignments and all associated units and symbols. | Deletes the selected physical quantity and all the associated units and symbols entirely from the units catalog. |

DIAdem displays the default symbol in all the dialog boxes in the units catalog if you select the associated unit. |
|  | Unit | Specifies the unit that the symbol is assigned to. |
|  | Size | Specifies the physical quantity that the unit symbol is assigned to. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_dimension_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00679: Edit Dimension

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_dimension_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_dimension_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Units Catalog](../dlgunitcatalog/unitcatalog_dlgoverview.htm) > [Quantities](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_quantities_dialog.htm) > Edit Dimension

Edit Dimension

Use this dialog box to specify the dimension of a physical quantity in relation to the base units in the [SI unit system](../../genshell/genshell/genunitcatalog_basics.htm). A dimension consists of the exponents of the seven SI base units.

#### Settings

| Size | Specifies the physical quantity that has the dimensions that you edit. |
| --- | --- |
| Exponent of length [m] | Specifies the exponent of the SI unit for length. |
| Exponent of mass [kg] | Specifies the exponent of the SI unit for mass. |
| Exponent of time [s] | Specifies the exponent of the SI unit for time. |
| Exponent of current [A] | Specifies the exponent of the SI unit for current. |
| Exponent of temperature [K] | Specifies the exponent of the SI unit for temperature. |
| Exponent of amount of substance [mol] | Specifies the exponent of the SI unit for amount of substance. |
| Exponent of luminous intensity [cd] | Specifies the exponent of the SI unit for luminous intensity. |
| Category | Specifies the category that the physical quantity is assigned to. You can select an existing category or enter your own category. |

|  | Note You create a new physical quantity from the seven basic SI quantities, with an integer exponent. The seven basic SI quantities are length, mass, time, current, thermodynamic temperature, amount of substance, and luminous intensity. For example, the surface consists of the length with the exponent 2 and the mass, time, current, thermodynamic temperature, amount of substance, and luminous intensity, with the exponent 0.Several categories can belong to one dimension. For example, radioactivity and angular velocity both have the same dimension (0,0,-1,0,0,0,0) but different categories. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»Units in any DIAdem panel, click the Quantities tab, and double-click the column Dimensions. |
| --- | --- |

#### Procedures

[Adding an Unknown Unit Symbol to the Units Catalog](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unit_dialog.htm) | [Converting Channel Units in DIAdem ANALYSIS](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_calculate_units.htm) | [Converting Channel Units with a Script](../../procauto/procauto/procauto_calculate_channelunits.htm) | [Converting Channels According to a Unit Set](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_convert_unitset.htm) | [Creating a New Unit Set](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unitset.htm) | [Creating a Physical Quantity in the Units Catalog](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unit.htm) | [Extending the Units Catalog with a Script](../../procauto/procauto/procauto_add_units.htm) | [Replacing and Converting Channel Units in the Input Help](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_convert_units.htm)

#### Examples

[Converting Units](../../exploff/examples/unitcalcandreport.htm)

- source_path: `dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_quantities_dialog.htm`

- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Units Catalog](../dlgunitcatalog/unitcatalog_dlgoverview.htm) > Edit Units Catalog»Quantities

Edit Units Catalog»Quantities

Use this dialog box to edit the [physical quantities](../../genshell/genshell/genunitcatalog_basics.htm) of a [unit set](../../genshell/genshell/genunitcatalog.htm) from the units catalog.

#### Settings

|  | Load | Opens the dialog box where you load a units catalog. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Save As | Opens the dialog box where you save the current configuration settings in a units catalog. |
|  | Unit set | Specifies the name of the unit set that is selected on the Unit Sets tab. |
|  | Size | Specifies the name of the physical quantity that is selected in the overview. |
|  | Unit | Specifies the name of the unit that is selected on the Units tab. |
|  | New Entry | Opens the Create New Quantity dialog box where you create a new physical quantity. |
|  | Link Quantities to Unit Set | Opens the Add Quantities to Unit Set dialog box, where you add a physical quantity to the unit set that is selected on the Unit Sets tab. |
|  | Delete Entry | Opens the Delete Quantity dialog box, where you add a physical quantity to the unit set that is selected on the Unit Sets tab. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected physical quantity one position up. The physical quantities then appear in all the dialog boxes in the units catalog in the order you specify here. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected physical quantity one position down. The physical quantities then appear in all the dialog boxes in the units catalog in the order you specify here. |
|  | Sort Values in Alphabetical Order | Sorts the physical quantities in alphabetical order. If sorting is enabled, you cannot move any physical quantities within the overview. |
|  | No. | Specifies a serial number. |
|  | Name | Specifies the display name of the physical quantity. To enter a new name, double-click the cell. |
|  | Base symbol | Specifies the base symbol of the physical quantity. |
|  | Dimension | Specifies the dimension of the physical quantity in the SI unit system. The dimension consists of the exponents of the seven SI base units. Double-click a cell to modify the dimension of the physical quantity in the Edit Dimension dialog box. When you assign a category to the physical quantity in the Edit Dimension dialog box, the category appears in the cell as an additional entry. |
|  | Number of Units | Specifies the number of units that the selected physical quantity contains. |
|  | Description | Specifies the description of the physical quantity. To enter a new description, double-click the cell. |
|  | Display all defined quantities | Specifies whether DIAdem displays all the physical quantities of the entire units catalog in the overview, or only the quantities of the unit set that is selected on the Unit Sets tab. |

[Unit Sets](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_sets_dialog.htm) | Quantities | [Units](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_units_dialog.htm) | [All Symbols](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_allsymbols_dialog.htm)

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings» Units in any DIAdem panel and open the Quantities tab. |

## TOPIC 00681: Edit Units Catalog»Unit Sets

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_sets_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_sets_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Units Catalog](../dlgunitcatalog/unitcatalog_dlgoverview.htm) > Edit Units Catalog»Unit Sets

Edit Units Catalog»Unit Sets

Use this dialog box to edit the [unit sets](../../genshell/genshell/genunitcatalog.htm) in the units catalog.

#### Settings

|  | Load | Opens the dialog box where you load a units catalog. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Save As | Opens the dialog box where you save the current configuration settings in a units catalog. |
|  | Unit set | Specifies the name of the unit set that is selected in the overview. |
|  | Size | Specifies the name of the physical quantity that is selected on the Quantities tab. |
|  | Unit | Specifies the name of the unit that is selected on the Units tab. |
|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you create a new unit set. |
|  | Copy Entry | Creates a copy of the selected unit set. DIAdem gives the copy the original name and adds an underline and a number. The copy of the unit set contains the same physical quantities, units, and symbols as the original unit set. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected unit set. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected unit set one position up. The unit sets then appear in all the dialog boxes in the units catalog in the order you specify here. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected unit set one position down. The unit sets then appear in all the dialog boxes in the units catalog in the order you specify here. |
|  | No. | Specifies a serial number. |
|  | Name | Specifies the display name of the unit set. To enter a new name, double-click the cell. |
|  | Enabled | Specifies whether the unit set is enabled. DIAdem displays the enabled unit set as the default unit set, in all dialog boxes of the units catalog. |
|  | Number of Quantities | Specifies the number of physical quantities that the selected unit set contains. |
|  | Description | Describes the unit set. To enter a new description, double-click the cell. |

|  | Note To select a unit set, click the appropriate row. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, select Settings»Units in any DIAdem panel and open the Unit Sets tab. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

Units| [Quantities](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_quantities_dialog.htm) | [Units](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_units_dialog.htm) | [Alls Symbols](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_allsymbols_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Adding an Unknown Unit Symbol to the Units Catalog](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unit_dialog.htm) | [Converting Channel Units in DIAdem ANALYSIS](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_calculate_units.htm) | [Converting Channel Units with a Script](../../procauto/procauto/procauto_calculate_channelunits.htm) | [Converting Channels According to a Unit Set](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_convert_unitset.htm) | [Creating a New Unit Set](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unitset.htm) | [Creating a Physical Quantity in the Units Catalog](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unit.htm) | [Extending the Units Catalog with a Script](../../procauto/procauto/procauto_add_units.htm) | [Replacing and Converting Channel Units in the Input Help](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_convert_units.htm)

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_load_result_dialog.htm`

- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Units Catalog](../dlgunitcatalog/unitcatalog_dlgoverview.htm) > [Unit sets](../dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_edit_sets_dialog.htm) > Load Result

Load Result

Use this dialog box to get an overview of the elements of a units catalog that were added or overwritten in a units catalog.

#### Settings

| Added | Specifies the elements that were added to the previous units catalog by loading the new units catalog. |
| --- | --- |
| Overwritten | Specifies the elements of the units catalog which were overwritten by loading elements that have the same name. |
| Type | Specifies the element type. A type can be a unit set, a physical dimension, or a symbol. |
| Name | Specifies the element name. If the display name was overwritten, the tooltip shows the previous name. |
| Reference | Specifies the element reference. |

|  | Note Press <Ctrl-Shift-C> to copy a script to the clipboard. The script displays the changes produced by the loading. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note To open this dialog box select Contents»Retain in the Load Units Catalog dialog box and click OK. |
| --- | --- |

#### Settings

|  | Unit | Specifies the unit of which you edit the symbols. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you add a new symbol to the selected unit. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected symbol. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected symbol one position up in the list. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected symbol one position down in the list. |
|  | No. | Specifies a serial number. |
|  | Notation | Specifies the notation of the unit symbol. You use this text to access the unit in DIAdem. To change the notation, double-click the cell. |
|  | Enabled | Specifies whether the symbol is the enabled symbol of the associated unit. DIAdem displays the enabled symbol by default in all the dialog boxes in the units catalog if you select the associated unit. |
