## TOPIC 00685: Waveform X-Unit: Symbol Input Help

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_wfxunit_assistant_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog/dlgunitcatalog_wfxunit_assistant_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[Units Catalog](../dlgunitcatalog/unitcatalog_dlgoverview.htm) > Waveform X-Unit: Symbol Input Help

Waveform X-Unit: Symbol Input Help

Use this dialog box to assign a new unit and a new unit symbol to the waveform channel you select in the Data Portal or in a channel table in DIAdem VIEW. If the x-unit of the waveform channel belongs to the same physical quantity as the target unit, you also can convert the channel values into the new unit in this dialog box.

#### Settings

| Symbol | Specifies the symbol of the unit of the waveform channel. If the waveform channel has no unit, this area remains blank. If you select a new unit in the bottom part of the dialog box, DIAdem displays the unit. |
| --- | --- |
| Unit set | Specifies the unit set from which you select the physical quantities and the units. By default, DIAdem displays the enabled unit set. If the unit of the input channel is known but does not exist in this unit set, DIAdem displays <All units> here. |
| Size | Specifies the physical quantity from which you select the unit and the symbol that you assign to the input channel. |
| Units | Specifies the symbol and the associated unit, which you assign to the values of the waveform channel. |
| Replace | Replaces the unit and the symbol of the waveform channel. DIAdem does not modify the channel values. |
| Convert | Replaces the unit and the symbol of the waveform channel and converts the channel values into the new unit. DIAdem enables this button only if the physical quantity that is selected in the dialog box is the same as the physical quantity of the waveform channel. |

|  | Note If you open the symbol input help from the Data Portal and you have selected several waveform channels, DIAdem replaces or converts the units of all the channels. |
| --- | --- |

|  | Note To open this dialog box, click the Waveform x-unit cell of a waveform channel in the properties display in the Data Portal or in a channel table in DIAdem VIEW, and then click the ... button. |
| --- | --- |

#### Procedures

[Adding an Unknown Unit Symbol to the Units Catalog](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unit_dialog.htm) | [Converting Channel Units in DIAdem ANALYSIS](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_calculate_units.htm) | [Converting Channel Units with a Script](../../procauto/procauto/procauto_calculate_channelunits.htm) | [Converting Channels According to a Unit Set](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_convert_unitset.htm) | [Creating a New Unit Set](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unitset.htm) | [Creating a Physical Quantity in the Units Catalog](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_create_unit.htm) | [Extending the Units Catalog with a Script](../../procauto/procauto/procauto_add_units.htm) | [Replacing and Converting Channel Units in the Input Help](../../procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog/procunitcatalog_convert_units.htm)

#### Examples

[Converting Units](../../exploff/examples/unitcalcandreport.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgview/dlgview/view_blockoperations_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00688: Block Operations

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_blockoperations_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_blockoperations_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Channel Table](../dlgview/view_channels_tab_columns_dialog.htm) > [Operations in Channel Tables](../dlgview/view_channeltable_operations.htm) > Block Operations

Block Operations

Use this dialog box to carry out block operations in a channel table.

#### Settings

| Copy data | Specifies that DIAdem copies a data block to another place in the channel table. DIAdem overwrites the data at the target position. The source block and the target block must not overlap. |
| --- | --- |
| Insert data | Specifies that DIAdem copies a data block to another place in the channel table. At the target position DIAdem moves the existing data down. The source block and the target block must not overlap. |
| Append data | Specifies that DIAdem copies a data block to another place in the channel table. DIAdem inserts the data at the end of the target channel. The source block and the target block must not overlap. |
| Insert value | Specifies that DIAdem inserts a data block with the specified numeric value in the channel table. At the target position DIAdem moves the existing data down. The source block and the target block must not overlap. |
| Overwrite value | Specifies that DIAdem overwrites a data block in the channel table with the specified numeric value. |
| First channel | Specifies the first channel of the block. |
| First row | Specifies the first row of the block. |
| Last channel | Specifies the last channel of the block. |
| Last row | Specifies the last row of the block. |
| Channel | Specifies the target channel. |
| Row | Specifies the target row. |
| Value | Specifies the numeric value which DIAdem inserts into the channel table or with which DIAdem overwrites channel values. |

#### Script Call

[DataBlCopy](../../comoff/datablcopy.htm)

[DataBlInsert](../../comoff/datablinsert.htm)

[DataBlAppend](../../comoff/datablappend.htm)

[DataBlInsertVal](../../comoff/datablinsertval.htm)

#### Further Settings

[Select Block](../dlgview/view_selectblock_dialog.htm) | Block Operations | [Generate Channel Contents](../dlgview/view_generate_dialog.htm) | [Go to Channel Value / Find Channel Value](../dlgview/view_gotovalue_dialog.htm) | [Go to Row](../dlgview/view_goto_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Block Operations in Channel Tables](../../procview/procview/procview_block_operations_extended.htm) | [Changing a Table Display](../../procview/procview/procview_table_settings.htm) | [Cutting, Copying, and Pasting Data Blocks into Channel Tables](../../procview/procview/procview_block_operations.htm) | [Deleting Channel Table Columns](../../procview/procview/procview_table_columns.htm) | [Displaying All Channels in One Channel Table](../../procview/procview/procview_channel_tables.htm)

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_bodecurvedefinition_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_bodecurvedefinition_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > Bode Axis System

Bode Axis System

Use this dialog box to generate or to delete curve pairs in a [Bode Axis System](../../genview/genview/view_bode.htm) or to modify their appearance.

#### Settings

|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you generate a new curve pair. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Copy Entry | Copies the selected entry. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected entry. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected entry up in the overview. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected entry down in the overview. |
|  | Curve List | Displays an overview of the curves. Select the curve pair you want to modify. |
|  | Display curve | Specifies that DIAdem plots the curves in both axis systems. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the curve pair. |
|  | X-channel | Specifies the data channel containing the x-values. You do not need to specify the x-channel if the y-channel is a waveform channel or if the y-channel is an xy-channel and you have selected the When plotting xy-channels, automatically determine x-channel if not populated setting in the General DIAdem Settings. |
|  | Phase | Specifies the data channel containing the phase values. |
|  | Amplitude | Specifies the data channel containing the amplitude values. |
|  | Display axis labels | Specifies that DIAdem displays the axis labels. |
|  | Scale phase manually | Specifies that you can determine the phase axis in the top axis system manually. If you do not select this setting, DIAdem scales the phase axis automatically according to the largest and smallest value of the selected channel. |
|  | Begin | Specifies the start value of the phase axis. |
|  | End | Specifies the end value of the phase axis. |
|  | Scale amplitude manually | Specifies that you can determine the amplitude axis in the bottom axis system manually. If you do not select this setting, DIAdem scales the amplitude axis automatically according to the largest and smallest value of the selected channel. |
|  | Begin | Specifies the first value on the amplitude axis. |
|  | End | Specifies the last value on the amplitude axis. |
|  | Division ratio | Specifies how much space the bottom axis system takes up in the Bode axis system as a percentage. |
|  | Cursor Synchronization | Opens the dialog box where you assign the cursor dimensions. |

#### Script Call

[ShowCurvesDlg](../../scriptview/methods/view_method_showcurvesdlg_itobodechartint.htm)

#### Procedures

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgview/dlgview/view_cascade_3dcurve_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00690: Add Curve: Order Line

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_cascade_3dcurve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_cascade_3dcurve_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Cascade](../dlgview/view_cascade_dialog.htm) > Add Curve: Order Line

Add Curve: Order Line

Use this dialog box to generate a order line in a [Cascade Display](../../genview/genview/view_cascade.htm). In a contour display you can define only one waterfall curve, but several order lines. You cannot generate order lines until you have defined a waterfall curve.

#### Settings

| X-channel | Specifies for the Order line display type the channel with the x-values of the line. |
| --- | --- |
| Y-channel | Specifies for the Order line display type the channel with the y-values of the line. |
| Color | Specifies the color of the line. |

#### Procedures

Cascade: Axes

Use this dialog box to specify the axis display in a [cascade display](../../genview/genview/view_cascade.htm).

#### Settings

| Label channel | Specifies which channel labels the track axis. |
| --- | --- |
| Scale y-axis automatically | Specifies whether you specify the value range for the y-scaling, or whether DIAdem specifies the value range automatically. |
| Y-begin | Specifies the start value of manual y-scaling. |
| Y-end | Specifies the end value of manual y-scaling. |
| Inclination angle: Vertical | Specifies the vertical inclination angle. The greater the vertical inclination angle, the more you view the cascade display from above. |
| Inclination angle: Horizontal | Specifies the horizontal inclination angle. The greater the horizontal inclination angle, the greater the horizontal shear of the cascade display. |

## TOPIC 00692: Cascade: Curves

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_cascade_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_cascade_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > Cascade: Curves

Cascade: Curves

Use this dialog box to generate, to delete, or to change the display of a waterfall curve and one or more order lines in a [Cascade Display](../../genview/genview/view_cascade.htm).

In a cascade display you can define only one waterfall curve, but several order lines. You cannot generate order lines until you have defined a waterfall curve. If you delete a waterfall curve, you also delete the order lines.

#### Settings

|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you generate a Waterfall curve or a new Order line. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Copy Entry | Copies the selected entry. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected entry. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected entry up in the overview. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected entry down in the overview. |
|  | No. | Displays the number of the curve. Click the number to select a curve. |
|  | Type | Specifies the display mode of the curve. Depending on the display mode, you specify different channels and structures. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
|  | Channels | Displays the channels of the curve. You change the curve channels at the bottom of the dialog box. |
|  | Channel cascade XYXY / Channel cascade XYYY/Matrix | Specifies in the Waterfall display mode whether the data is available as x/y channel pairs, an x-channel and n y-channels, or as a matrix. |
|  | X-channel | Specifies for the Waterfall display type with the Matrix data structure, the channel with the x-values of the curve. |
|  | Y-channels | Specifies for the Waterfall display type with the Matrix data structure, the channels which span the y-matrix. Click ... to select the channels. |
|  | Track | Specifies for the Waterfall display type with the Matrix data structure, the channel with the track values of the curve. |
|  | 1st X-channel | Specifies for the Waterfall display type with the data structures Channel cascade XYXY or Channel cascade XYYY the first channel with the x-values of the curve. |
|  | 1st Y-channel | Specifies for the Waterfall display type with the data structures Channel cascade XYXY or Channel cascade XYYY the first channel with the y-values of the curve. |
|  | Number | Specifies the number of tracks for the Waterfall display type with the data structures Channel cascade XYXY or Channel cascade XYYY. |
|  | X-channel | Specifies for the Order line display type the channel with the x-values of the line. |
|  | Y-channel | Specifies for the Order line display type the channel with the y-values of the line. |
|  | Order channel | Specifies the order channel for the Waterfall display mode. The order channel receives the fundamental oscillation for each track and must have the same unit as the x-channel (frequency channel). The fundamental oscillation in an engine is normally the same as the rpm. You must specify an order channel in order to display order lines or dynamic order lines. |
|  | Additional Order Lines | Opens the dialog box for the Waterfall display mode, where you can specify additional order lines. |
|  | Limit track count | Specifies for the Waterfall display mode, whether DIAdem limits the maximum number of displayed tracks. |
|  | Maximum number of tracks | Specifies for the Waterfall display mode the maximum number of displayed tracks. |
|  | Cursor Synchronization | Opens the dialog box where you assign the cursor dimensions. |

#### Further Settings

Display | [Axes](../dlgview/view_cascade_axis_dialog.htm)

#### Script Call

[ShowCurvesDlg](../../scriptview/methods/view_method_showcurvesdlg_itocascadechartint.htm)

#### Procedures

[Configuring a Map Display](../../procview/procview/procview_map.htm) | [Configuring a Text Box Display](../../procview/procview/procview_textfield_parametrize.htm) | [Deleting Curve Sections and Interpolating over Specified Points](../../procview/procview/procview_flags_interpolate_point.htm) | [Displaying 2D Axis Systems with Several Y-Axes](../../procview/procview/procview_axissystems_multiple_axes.htm) | [Displaying Images in DIAdem VIEW](../../procview/procview/procview_show_graphics.htm) | [Displaying Properties in the Legend of a Curve](../../procview/procview/procview_legend_properties.htm) | [Displaying the Curve Coordinates](../../procview/procview/procview_coordinates.htm) | [Displaying Videos and Data Synchronously](../../procview/procview/procview_video_synchronize.htm) | [Finding Values in Channel Tables](../../procview/procview/procview_goto_values.htm) | [Interpolating Curve Points](../../procview/procview/procview_flags.htm) | [Setting the Leading Curve](../../procview/procview/procview_setting_leadingcurve.htm) | [Transferring VIEW Layouts to DIAdem REPORT](../../procview/procview/procview_transfer_report.htm) | [Viewing Data as Curves](../../procview/procview/procview_curve.htm) | [Zooming and Scrolling Curve Areas](../../procview/procview/procview_scrolling.htm)

#### Settings

|  | Channel cascade XYXY / Channel cascade XYYY/Matrix | Specifies, whether the data is available as x/y channel pairs, an x-channel and n y-channels, or as a matrix. |

|  | X-channel | Specifies for the Matrix data structure the channel with the x-values of the curve. |
|  |  |  |
|  | Y-channels | Specifies, for the Matrix data structure, the data channels which span the y-matrix. |
|  | Channel Selection | Opens the dialog box where you select the y-channels. |
|  | Track | Specifies for the Matrix data structure the channel with the track values of the curve. |
|  | 1. X-channel | Specifies for the data structures Channel cascade XYXY or Channel cascade XYYY the first channel with the x-values of the curve. |
|  | 1. Y-channel | Specifies for the data structures Channel cascade XYXY or Channel cascade XYYY the first channel with the y-values of the curve. |
|  | Number | Specifies for the data structures Channel cascade XYXY or Channel cascade XYYY the number of tracks. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the curve. |

|  | Color | Specifies the color of the isoline. |
|  | Minimum | Displays the smallest value of the color palette. |
|  | Maximum | Displays the greatest value of the color palette. |

## TOPIC 00699: Cursor Parameters » Play

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_cursor_prop_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_cursor_prop_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [DIAdem VIEW - Settings](../dlgview/view_conf_dialog.htm) > Cursor Parameters » Play

Cursor Parameters » Play

Use this dialog box to specify for the current worksheet the area in which DIAdem moves the cursor when the video plays, and to specify the speed of the cursor.

#### Settings

| Velocity | Specifies the factor by which DIAdem plays a video and by which DIAdem moves the cursor along the x-range. If the factor is one, DIAdem plays a video at the original speed. If you want to run a high-speed video at half the speed, for example, you must enter 0.5. If you want to run a video at twice the speed, you must enter 2. |
| --- | --- |
| Specify play range automatically | Specifies automatically the maximum range in which DIAdem plays a video and in which DIAdem moves the cursor along the x-range. |
| Begin | Specifies the beginning of the play range. |
| Begin, Cursor position, Apply | Specifies the beginning of the play range from the current cursor position. If you use the band cursor, the left band cursor specifies the beginning of the play range and the right band cursor specifies the end of the play range. |
| End | Specifies the end of the play range. |
| End, Cursor position, Apply | Specifies the end of the play range from the current cursor position. |
| Interpolate if x-channels are not the same/Use point numbers | Specifies whether DIAdem interpolates the coordinates of all the curves to correspond to the x-values of the leading curve when DIAdem moves the curve cursor, or whether DIAdem uses the point numbers of the x-channels instead of the x-values, to synchronize the cursor in various axis systems. |
| Keep delta-x and delta-y constant | Specifies whether DIAdem keeps the dX and dY intervals of the cursor lines constant for a band cursor or a frame cursor, or whether DIAdem keeps the second cursor line on the curve points. |

|  | Note To open this dialog box in DIAdem VIEW, select Settings»Cursor Parameters. |
| --- | --- |

#### Further Settings

Play | [Synchronization](../dlgview/view_cursor_sync_dialog.htm) | [Number](../dlgview/view_cursor_additional_dialog.htm) | [Colors](../dlgview/view_cursor_color_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[3D Interpolation](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_3d_map.htm) | [Bird's Eye View Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_birds_eye_view_example.htm) | [Overlaying Objects in Videos](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_video_objects_austin_example.htm) | [Planetary Motion](../../exploff/examples/expl_planets_example.htm) | [Recording Video and Measurement Data](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_video.htm) | [Synchronizing Maps, Videos, and Measurement Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_austin_drive.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av4.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av4.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Waveform Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av5.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Waveform Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av5.htm) | [Various Display Modes in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/example_example_view.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgview/dlgview/view_map_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00707: Map

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_map_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_map_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > Map

Map

Use this dialog box to select which maps and channels DIAdem uses to synchronize the [Map](../../genview/genview/view_map.htm) view. The channels for the synchronization track, the longitude, the latitude, and the color should all have the same length to ensure that DIAdem displays the track correctly on the map.

You can assign a cursor dimension to the synchronization track, the longitude, and the latitude. Select the setting [New](../dlgview/view_cursor_sync_dialog.htm) as the cursor dimension in order to open the dialog box where you define a new cursor dimension.

Refer to the Help page [Cursor Synchronization](../../genview/genview/view_synchronisation.htm) for further information.

#### Settings

| Map source | Specifies which maps DIAdem uses for the map display.The OpenStreetMap map source accesses OpenStreetMap maps through an internet connection. The Cache map source uses the maps stored locally, which you can also use without internet connection. The user-defined map source accesses maps from a user-defined server. |
| --- | --- |
| Zoom level | Specifies the zoom level of the map view. |
| Show track | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the value pairs for longitude and latitude as polyline. The display of the polyline can slow down the display. This is particularly so if the longitude and latitude channels contain many value pairs, or if the available geographical data is distributed all over the world. |
| Map moving mode | Specifies how DIAdem moves the map section when using cursor synchronization. |
| Save map data in cache | Specifies whether DIAdem uses a cache for the map data. |
| Cache path | Specifies the path DIAdem uses to cache the map data. |
| Channel |  |
| Synchronization track | Specifies the data channel with the values for synchronizing the map display. |
| Longitude | Specifies the data channel with the longitudes. |
| Latitude | Specifies the data channel with the latitudes. |
| Color | Specifies which channel DIAdem uses to color the track. DIAdem divides the colors of the palette between the largest and the smallest value of the color channel. The applied palette looks like the following and cannot be changed: |
| Cursor dimension |  |
| Synchronization track | Specifies the cursor dimension for the synchronization channel. |
| Longitude | Specifies the cursor dimension for the longitude. |
| Latitude | Specifies the cursor dimension for the latitude. |

#### Examples

[Bird's Eye View Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_birds_eye_view_example.htm) | [Map Display in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewmap.htm) | [Synchronizing Maps, Videos, and Measurement Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_austin_drive.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgview/dlgview/view_polarcurvedefinition_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00710: Polar Axis System

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_polarcurvedefinition_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_polarcurvedefinition_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > Polar Axis System

Polar Axis System

Use this dialog box to generate or to delete curves in a [polar axis system](../../genview/genview/view_polar.htm) or to modify the curve.

#### Settings

|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you generate a new curve. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Copy Entry | Copies the selected entry. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected entry. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected entry up in the overview. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected entry down in the overview. |
|  | Curve List | Displays an overview of the curves. Select the curve you want to modify. |
|  | Display curve | Specifies that DIAdem plots the curve in the axis system. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
|  | Angle | Specifies the data channel that contains the angles of the polar curve. You do not need to specify the angle channel if the radius channel is a waveform channel or if the radius channel is an xy-channel and you have selected the When plotting xy-channels, automatically determine x-channel if not populated setting in the General DIAdem Settings. |
|  | Radius | Specifies the data channel that contains the radii of the polar curve. |
|  | Properties | Opens the dialog box where you specify the parameters for curve markers and curve labels. |
|  | Display axis labels | Specifies that DIAdem displays the axis labels. |
|  | Scale radial axis manually | Specifies that you can determine the value range for the radial axis manually. If you do not select this setting, DIAdem scales the radial axis automatically according to the largest and smallest value of the selected channel. |
|  | Begin | Specifies the start value for the radial axis. |
|  | End | Specifies the end value for the 2D axis. |
|  | Counter clockwise | Specifies that DIAdem plots the curve counter clockwise. |
|  | Clockwise | Specifies that DIAdem plots the polar curve clockwise. |
|  | Zero angle alignment | Specifies the position of the zero point in the full circle. The default value of this setting is 0, so that the zero point is on the right horizontal. Values greater than zero rotate the polar axis system counterclockwise. |
|  | Cursor Synchronization | Opens the dialog box where you assign the cursor dimensions. |

#### Further Settings

Display | Curve Properties: [Markers](../dlgview/view_polarcurveprop_dialog.htm) | Curve Properties: [Labels](../dlgview/view_polarcurveprop_label_dialog.htm)

#### Script Call

[ShowCurvesDlg](../../scriptview/methods/view_method_showcurvesdlg_itopolarchartint.htm)

#### Procedures

## TOPIC 00711: Polar Axis System: Curve Properties » Markers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_polarcurveprop_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_polarcurveprop_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Polar Axis System](../dlgview/view_polarcurvedefinition_dialog.htm) > Polar Axis System: Curve Properties » Markers

Polar Axis System: Curve Properties » Markers

Use this dialog box to specify the display of symbols on the curve of a polar axis system.

#### Settings

| Marker style | Specifies the symbol for the markers on the curve. |
| --- | --- |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the markers. |
| Size | Specifies the size of the marker. |
| Marker color | Specifies the frame color of the marker symbols.Use the setting Same color as curve so that DIAdem displays the frame of the marker symbols in the same color as the curve. |
| Filling color | Specifies the filling color of the markers.Use the setting Same color as curve so that DIAdem displays the filling of the marker symbols in the same color as the curve. |
| Repeat marker | Specifies the frequency of the markers. |
| n: Every n points | Specifies after how many curve points DIAdem plots the next marker symbol. |
| n: Every n percent | Specifies the distance of the curve after which DIAdem plots the next marker symbol on the curve, as a percentage.To do this, DIAdem specifies the length of the diagonal of the axis system. DIAdem applies n percent of this diagonal along the curve and plots the marker symbols at the next point. |
| n: Maximum n points | Specifies the maximum number of marker symbols which DIAdem plots evenly along the curve. |
| Marker at curve begin | Specifies that DIAdem displays a marker at the beginning of the curve. |
| Marker at curve end | Specifies that DIAdem displays a marker at the end of the curve. |
| Display curve in legend | Specifies that DIAdem shows the curve in the legend of the axis system. If you do not select this setting, you cannot select the curve as the leading curve in the legend. |

#### Further Settings

[Display](../dlgview/view_polarcurvedefinition_dialog.htm) | Curve Properties: Markers | Curve Properties: [Labels](../dlgview/view_polarcurveprop_label_dialog.htm)

#### Procedures

[Configuring a Map Display](../../procview/procview/procview_map.htm) | [Configuring a Text Box Display](../../procview/procview/procview_textfield_parametrize.htm) | [Deleting Curve Sections and Interpolating over Specified Points](../../procview/procview/procview_flags_interpolate_point.htm) | [Displaying 2D Axis Systems with Several Y-Axes](../../procview/procview/procview_axissystems_multiple_axes.htm) | [Displaying Images in DIAdem VIEW](../../procview/procview/procview_show_graphics.htm) | [Displaying Properties in the Legend of a Curve](../../procview/procview/procview_legend_properties.htm) | [Displaying the Curve Coordinates](../../procview/procview/procview_coordinates.htm) | [Displaying Videos and Data Synchronously](../../procview/procview/procview_video_synchronize.htm) | [Finding Values in Channel Tables](../../procview/procview/procview_goto_values.htm) | [Interpolating Curve Points](../../procview/procview/procview_flags.htm) | [Setting the Leading Curve](../../procview/procview/procview_setting_leadingcurve.htm) | [Transferring VIEW Layouts to DIAdem REPORT](../../procview/procview/procview_transfer_report.htm) | [Viewing Data as Curves](../../procview/procview/procview_curve.htm) | [Zooming and Scrolling Curve Areas](../../procview/procview/procview_scrolling.htm)

#### Examples

[Analyzing and Displaying Channels Section by Section](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewdisplaychnparts.htm) | [Automatic Display of Harmonic Frequencies](../../exploff/examples/view_harmonic_cursor.htm) | [Background Segments in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/expl_viewsegment.htm) | [Calculating a Tangent to a Curve](../../exploff/examples/expl_tangentcursor.htm) | [Creating and Viewing Long Data Channels](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av3.htm) | [Dynamic Display of Statistical Characteristic Values in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/view_statistic_init.htm) | [Overlaying Objects in Videos](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_video_objects_austin_example.htm) | [User Dialog Box in VIEW for the Calculation of the FFT and Harmonic Frequencies](../../exploff/examples/view_fft_analysis.htm) | [Vibration Data Analysis with Parallel Processing](../../exploff/examples/expl_rotatingshaftanalysis.htm) | [Viewing and Automatically Analyzing Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av1.htm)

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgview/dlgview/view_segment_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00712: Color Background Segments

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_segment_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_segment_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [2D Axis System](../dlgview/view_2dcurvedefinition_dialog.htm) > Color Background Segments

Color Background Segments

Use this dialog box to create, to delete, or to edit background segments in a [2D axis system](../dlgview/view_2dcurvedefinition_dialog.htm).

Use segments to display Boolean states. A segment corresponds to a colored area where the state is larger 0 which is a Boolean value unequal False. DIAdem plots the segments in the background of the axis system. Match the transparency of the segments so that the segment at the bottom stays visible when the segments overlap.

If you want to display segments vertically, select the X type and specify in the position of the segments in the x-channel and specify the states in the y-channel. 
To display segments horizontally select the Y type. In this case the x-channel must contain the states and the y-channel the positions of the segments.

#### Settings

|  | New Entry | Opens the dialog box where you create segments. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Copy Entry | Copies the selected entry. |
|  | Delete Entry | Deletes the selected entry. |
|  | Move Entry Up | Moves the selected entry up in the overview. |
|  | Move Entry Down | Moves the selected entry down in the overview. |
|  | Type | Specifies whether DIAdem displays segments in vertical or in horizontal direction. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the segments. |
|  | X-channel | Specifies the data channel that contains the x-values of the segments. |
|  | Y-channel | Specifies the data channel that contains the y-values of the segments. |
|  | Transparency | Specifies the transparency of the segments in a 2D axis system as a percentage. |

#### Examples

[Contour Display in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/example_view_contour.htm) | [Various Display Modes in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/example_example_view.htm)

## TOPIC 00716: Shaft Centerline: Shaft & Bearing

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurvedefinition_shaft_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurvedefinition_shaft_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Shaft centerline](../dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurvedefinition_dialog.htm) > Shaft Centerline: Shaft & Bearing

Shaft Centerline: Shaft & Bearing

Use this dialog box to specify the shaft and bearing.

#### Settings

| Counter clockwise | Specifies that the shaft rotates counter-clockwise and that DIAdem therefore plots a left-turning curve. |
| --- | --- |
| Clockwise | Specifies that DIAdem plots the curve clockwise. |
| X-sensor [°] | Specifies the position of the x-sensor. DIAdem displays the position of the two sensors in the axis system. |
| Y-sensor [°] | Specifies the position of the y-sensor. DIAdem displays the position of the two sensors in the axis system. |
| Aperture angle [°] | Displays the angle between the x-sensor and the y-sensor. The angle must be between 0° and 180°. |
| Horizontal | Specifies the horizontal diameter of the maximum bearing clearance. DIAdem displays the maximum bearing clearance as a circle in the axis system. |
| Vertical | Specifies the vertical diameter of the maximum bearing clearance. |
| Shaft resting position | Specifies the position of the shaft before it rotates. |

#### Further Settings

[Curves](../dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurvedefinition_dialog.htm) | Curve Properties: [Markers](../dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurveprop_dialog.htm) | Curve Properties: [Labels](../dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurveprop_label_dialog.htm) | Shaft & Bearing

## TOPIC 00717: Curves: Curve Properties » Markers

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurveprop_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurveprop_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Shaft centerline](../dlgview/view_shaftcenterlinecurvedefinition_dialog.htm) > Curves: Curve Properties » Markers

Curves: Curve Properties » Markers

Use this dialog box to specify the display of symbols on the curve of a shaft centerline axis system.

#### Settings

| Marker style | Specifies the symbol for the markers on the curve. |
| --- | --- |
| Line width | Specifies the line width of the markers. |
| Size | Specifies the size of the marker. |
| Marker color | Specifies the frame color of the marker symbols.Use the setting Same color as curve so that DIAdem displays the frame of the marker symbols in the same color as the curve. |
| Filling color | Specifies the filling color of the markers.Use the setting Same color as curve so that DIAdem displays the filling of the marker symbols in the same color as the curve. |
| Repeat marker | Specifies the frequency of the markers. |
| n: Every n points | Specifies after how many curve points DIAdem plots the next marker symbol. |
| n: Every n percent | Specifies the distance of the curve after which DIAdem plots the next marker symbol on the curve, as a percentage.To do this, DIAdem specifies the length of the diagonal of the axis system. DIAdem applies n percent of this diagonal along the curve and plots the marker symbols at the next point. |
| n: Maximum n points | Specifies the maximum number of marker symbols which DIAdem plots evenly along the curve. |
| Marker at curve begin | Specifies that DIAdem displays a marker at the beginning of the curve. |
| Marker at curve end | Specifies that DIAdem displays a marker at the end of the curve. |
| Display curve in legend | Specifies that DIAdem shows the curve in the legend of the axis system. If you do not select this setting, you cannot select the curve as the leading curve in the legend. |

#### Further Settings

## TOPIC 00718: Video: Synchronization

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_video_syncprop_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_video_syncprop_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Video](../dlgview/view_video_fileopen_dialog.htm) > Video: Synchronization

Video: Synchronization

Use this dialog box to specify how to play back this [video](../../genview/genview/view_video.htm). If you use a [video channel](../../genshell/genshell/genshell_channeltypes.htm) to select the video, you cannot change the frame rate and start time in the dialog box. DIAdem then determines the frame rate and the start time from the corresponding properties of the video channel or, if these channel properties have the NoValue value, DIAdem determines the settings from the video file.

#### Settings

| Number of frames | Displays the number of frames. |
| --- | --- |
| Frame rate | Specifies how many frames DIAdem displays per second. |
| Start time | Specifies after how many seconds the video starts. If you want to synchronize the video with data that has an absolute time reference, you must specify the value of the minimum of the corresponding time channel as the start time in seconds. For example, you can obtain this value by executing the following VBS script line for the corresponding time channel.Call LogfileWrite(Data.Root.ChannelGroups(TimeGroupName).Channels(TimeChannelName).Minimum) |
| Duration | Shows how long the video runs. |
| Cursor Synchronization | Opens the dialog box where you assign the time axis of the video to a cursor dimension. |

#### Further Settings

[Video](../dlgview/view_video_fileopen_dialog.htm) | Synchronization  | [Object List](../dlgview/view_videoobjects_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[3D Interpolation](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_3d_map.htm) | [Bird's Eye View Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_birds_eye_view_example.htm) | [Overlaying Objects in Videos](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_video_objects_austin_example.htm) | [Planetary Motion](../../exploff/examples/expl_planets_example.htm) | [Recording Video and Measurement Data](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_video.htm) | [Synchronizing Maps, Videos, and Measurement Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_austin_drive.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av4.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av4.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Waveform Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av5.htm) | [Synchronizing Videos and Waveform Data](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_av5.htm) | [Various Display Modes in DIAdem VIEW](../../exploff/examples/example_example_view.htm)

## TOPIC 00719: Overlay Object Properties

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgview/dlgview/view_videoobjectsproperties_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgview/dlgview/view_videoobjectsproperties_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem VIEW](../dlgview/view_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Video](../dlgview/view_video_fileopen_dialog.htm) > [Object List](../dlgview/view_videoobjects_dialog.htm) > Overlay Object Properties

Overlay Object Properties

Use this dialog box to specify the properties of Overlay objects in a [video](../../genview/genview/view_video.htm).

#### Settings

| Object size | Specifies the size of the Overlay object. If you specify the width, height, or size with a channel, DIAdem ignores this value. |
| --- | --- |
| Color channel | Specifies the data channel containing the colors of the Overlay object. The color corresponds to the index of the ColorLst variable. |
| Label channel | Specifies the data channel containing the labels of the Overlay object. |
| Width channel | Specifies the data channel with the horizontal positions of the Overlay object in the shape of a rectangle as a percentage of the video width. |
| Height channel | Specifies the data channel with the vertical positions of the Overlay object in the shape of a rectangle as a percentage of the video height. |
| Size channel | Specifies the data channel containing the sizes of the Overlay object. |
| Marker style | Specifies the marker style of the Overlay object. |

#### Examples

[Bird's Eye View Display](../../exploff/examples/expl_birds_eye_view_example.htm) | [Overlaying Objects in Videos](../../exploff/examples/expl_view_video_objects_austin_example.htm) | [Planetary Motion](../../exploff/examples/expl_planets_example.htm)

## TOPIC 00721: Slider Control: Manual Instrument

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgmansliderpoti_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgmansliderpoti_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([Manual Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_instruments_general.htm) | [Simulation Inputs](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_input_simulation/dac_dlgssinglevalues_simulationinputs_overview.htm)) > Slider Control: Manual Instrument

Slider Control: Manual Instrument

Use the slider control to generate a data signal.

#### Settings

| Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- |
| From | Specifies the lower limit of the display range. |
| To | Specifies the upper limit of the display range. |
| Step width | Specifies the interval between two values. |
| Initialization value | Specifies the value that the slider control outputs when the measurement starts. |
| Remote control | Specifies that you remote control the slider control through a data input. If you enable this setting, the dialog box also displays Data inputs and a Remote control inputs. The remote control is only activated when an active control signal is at the remote control input. You can only disable this setting if no signal is connected to the remote control input. You cannot remote control and manually control a manual instrument simultaneously.The slider control outputs the data input values as long as the values are within the display range of the slider control. The slider control outputs the respective limit values for values within the display range. |
| Signal Name | Specifies the name of the created signal. |

#### Further Settings

Manual Instrument | [Parameters](../dlgvis/dlgmansliderlay_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframe_dialog.htm) | [Label](../dlgvis/dlgvislabelscale_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainp_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopremote_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»System](../dlgvis/dlgvissysinp_dialog.htm) | [Outputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdataoutp_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Manual Input](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av27.htm)

## TOPIC 00722: Slider Control: Manual Instrument

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgmanswitch_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgmanswitch_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([Manual Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_instruments_general.htm) | [Simulation Inputs](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_input_simulation/dac_dlgssinglevalues_simulationinputs_overview.htm)) > Slider Control: Manual Instrument

Slider Control: Manual Instrument

Use the switch to generate a data signal manually. A push button outputs a signal as long as it is pressed, whereas a switch outputs data until it is pressed again.

#### Settings

| Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- |
| Return value |  |
| On | Specifies the return value that DIAdem displays when a switch is on or when a button is pressed. |
| Off | Specifies the return value that DIAdem displays when a switch is off or when a button is not pressed. |
| Function |  |
| Switch | Specifies that the manual instrument behaves like a switch. A switch outputs a data signal as long as it is switched on. Click or press the associated function key to switch off the switch. |
| Push button | Specifies that the manual instrument behaves like a push button. A push button outputs an impulse as soon as you click the push button or the respective function key. |
| Function key | Specifies with which function key you operate the switch. |
|  |  |
| Remote control | Specifies that you remote control the switch through a data input. If you enable this setting, the dialog box also displays Data inputs and a Remote control inputs. The remote control is only activated when an active control signal is at the remote control input. You can only disable this setting if no signal is connected to the remote control input. You cannot remote control and manually control a manual instrument simultaneously.If the switch is remote controlled, it also outputs return values. Only if the value 0 is at the data input, the switch returns the value for Off. |
| Signal Name | Specifies the name of the created signal. |

#### Further Settings

Manual Instrument | [Parameters](../dlgvis/dlgmanswitchlay_dialog.htm) » [Font](../dlgvis/dlgvisfont_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframe_dialog.htm) | [Label](../dlgvis/dlgvislabel_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainp_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopremote_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»System](../dlgvis/dlgvissysinp_dialog.htm) | [Outputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdataoutp_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[Manual Input](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av27.htm)

## TOPIC 00724: Text

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgrtf_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgrtf_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > Text

Text

Use a text display, for example to display a description or a note in relation to an event.

Select a text and format it with the following settings:

#### Settings

|  | Cut | Cuts out the selected text and adds it to the Windows clipboard. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Copy | Copies the selected text to the Windows clipboard. |
|  | Paste | Inserts the contents of the Windows clipboard into the text area. You also can insert formatted text from other applications. |
|  | Undo | Undoes the last editing step. |
|  | Font | Specifies the font for the selected text. |
|  | Font size | Specifies the font size for the selected text. |
|  | Text color | Specifies the font color for the selected text. |
|  | Bold | Displays the selected text in bold. |
|  | Italics | Displays the selected text in italics. |
|  | Underline | Underlines the selected text. |
|  | Align left | Aligns the text flush left. |
|  | Centered | Aligns the text to the center. |
|  | Align right | Aligns the text flush right. |
|  | Enumeration characters | Inserts an enumeration character to the selected paragraph. |
|  | Reduce indent | Decreases the indentation of the selected paragraph. |
|  | Increase indent | Increases the indentation of the selected paragraph. |
|  | Background color | Specifies the color of the text area. |
|  | Text | Specifies the text.Enter formula expressions and variables, for example, @@CurrTime@@ for the current time as well as text. |

#### Further Settings

Text | [Layout](../dlgvis/dlgrtf_layout_dialog.htm) » [Position](../dlgvis/dlgrtf_position_dialog.htm) | [Parameters](../dlgvis/dlgrtfparameter_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

## TOPIC 00725: Text: General Layout

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgrtf_layout_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgrtf_layout_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > [Text](../dlgvis/dlgrtf_dialog.htm) > Text: General Layout

Text: General Layout

Use this dialog box to specify the layout of a text display.

#### Settings

| Horizontal | Specifies the title of the text display. |
| --- | --- |
| Font | Opens the dialog box where you specify the font attributes of the title. |
| Frame filling | Displays the frame color. |
| Frame filling: Color | Opens the dialog box where you specify the frame color. |
| Label | Displays the title color. |
| Label: Color | Opens the dialog box where you specify the title color. |

#### Further Settings

DIAdem VISUAL

DIAdem VISUAL

The following topics describe the dialog boxes in the [DIAdem VISUAL](../../genvis/genvis/visual_general.htm) panel. You use these dialog boxes to make your settings for visualizing measured data or data that is calculated online.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisbar_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00727: Bars: Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisbar_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisbar_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > [Bars](../dlgvis/dlgvislistbar_dialog.htm) > Bars: Parameters

Bars: Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the bar display.

#### Settings

| Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- |
| Horizontal | Specifies that the bars move up and down. |
| Vertical | Specifies that the bars move from left to right. |
| Display refresh | Specifies the frequency at which DIAdem redisplays the measured values. |
| Unit | Specifies the unit of the display clock. |
| Change color when limits are exceeded | Specifies that DIAdem displays the complete bar in the colors of the warning and alarm range when limit values are exceeded. If you do not select this setting, DIAdem displays only the part of the bar that is outside the limits in another color. |
| Display grid lines | Specifies that DIAdem displays grid lines inside the display area. |
| Reference point [%]: | Specifies the beginning of the bar as a percentage of the entire display. The reference line specifies whether the bars display on one side or on both sides of the axis. If the value is 0, the bar starts below or left and if the value is 50 in the center.If the alignment is vertical, DIAdem displays the bars from the reference point upwards if the measured value is greater than the reference point, and downwards if the measured value is less than the reference point. If the alignment is horizontal, DIAdem displays the bar to the right and left of the reference point. |
| Y-axis | Specifies the display mode of the bars.You can choose between one y-axis and several y-axes, and between a display that is a percentage of the display area and a display of the physical values. |

#### Further Settings

Signal List | [Parameters](../dlgvis/dlgvisbar_dialog.htm) | [Limit Values](../dlgvis/dlgvislimitdef_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframebgrd_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../dlgvis/dlgvislabellegscale_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainps_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopreset_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[3D Interpolation](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_3d_map.htm) | [Automatic Dynamic Visualization](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av7.htm) | [Comparing Automatic Scalings](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_script_autoscaling1.htm) | [Different Offset Corrections](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_autoscaling_offset.htm) | [Display Instruments](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av17.htm) | [GPS Visualization](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_ab6.htm) | [Manual Dynamic Visualization](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av8.htm) | [Manual Input](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av27.htm) | [Message Display](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av15.htm) | [Monitoring a Facility Using Visualization Levels and Radio Buttons](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_facilit4_2.htm) | [Monitoring a Facility with Visualization Points](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_ab3.htm) | [Numeric and Tabular Display](../../explonl/explonl/exponl_num_tab_extended.htm) | [Numeric Display with Scroll Bar and Bar Display](../../explonl/explonl/exponl_example_dac.htm) | [Recording Video and Measurement Data](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_video.htm) | [Remote Control of Manual Instruments](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av16.htm) | [Scaling Several Curves Automatically](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_script_autoscaling2.htm) | [Scatter Display](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_scatter.htm) | [Start Interval of the Offset Correction](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_autoscaling_offsetnv.htm) | [Visualizing Measurement Data from a Car Race](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_ab5.htm)

## TOPIC 00728: Inputs»Control

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpreset_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpreset_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

[DIAdem DAC](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgs_overview.htm) > [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm) > [Simulation Inputs](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_input_simulation/dac_dlgssinglevalues_simulationinputs_overview.htm) > [Read Channel from Data Portal](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_input_simulation/dlgsimchn_dialog.htm) > Inputs»Control

Inputs»Control

Use this dialog box to specify the incoming control signal for resetting. The control input only impacts the block if you connect a control signal.

Refer to [Block Terminals in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/block_general.htm) for more information on block terminals. Refer to the page [Buses in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/wires.htm) for more information on the buses that you use to connect blocks.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Connect Signal | Connects the signal that is selected in the list to the terminal. |
|  | Disconnect Signal | Disconnects the signal that is selected in the list from the terminal. |
|  | Signal Name | Specifies the name of the connected signal. |
|  | Signal Connected | Shows that a signal is connected at the terminal. |
|  | Signal Disconnected | Shows that a signal is disconnected from the terminal. |
|  | Terminal Name | Specifies the terminal name. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinps_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00729: Inputs»Control

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinps_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinps_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([Formula](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_processing/dlgformula_dialog.htm) | [Formula](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_control/dlgcndformula_dialog.htm) | [Save in Variables](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_system/dlgvari_dialog.htm)) > Inputs»Control

Inputs»Control

Use this dialog box to specify, to connect, and to disconnect incoming control signals for starting. The control inputs only have an impact if you connect control signals. If you do not connect a control signal, the inputs do not impact the function of the block. The block starts then when the measurement starts.

Refer to [Block Terminals in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/block_general.htm) for more information on block terminals. Refer to the page [Buses in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/wires.htm) for more information on the buses that you use to connect blocks.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Connect Signals | Connects the signals that are selected in the list to the terminal. You also can select and connect one or more signals. |
|  | Disconnect Signals | Disconnects the signals that are selected in the list from the terminal. You also can select and disconnect one or more signals from the terminal. |
|  | Extend List | Adds a signal to the end of the list. |
|  | Reduce List | Deletes the signal at the end of the list. |
|  | List Length | Opens the dialog box where you specify the number of possible signals at one block. |
|  | Signal Name | Specifies the name of the signal. |
|  | Signal Connected | Shows that a signal is connected at the terminal. |
|  | Signal Disconnected | Shows that a signal is disconnected from the terminal. |
|  | Terminal Name | Specifies the terminal name. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpsjckr_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00730: Inputs»Control

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpsjckr_dialog.htm`

Inputs»Control

Use this dialog box to specify the incoming control signal for setting, resetting, and clocking the [JK FlipFlop](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_control/dlgcndjk_dialog.htm).

Refer to [Block Terminals in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/block_general.htm) for more information on block terminals. Refer to the page [Buses in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/wires.htm) for more information on the buses that you use to connect blocks.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Connect Signal | Connects the signal that is selected in the list to the terminal. |
|  | Disconnect Signal | Disconnects the signal that is selected in the list from the terminal. |
|  | Set | Specifies the control signal for static setting. |
|  | J | Specifies the control signal for dynamic setting. |
|  | Clock | Specifies the control signal for clocking J and K. |
|  | K | Specifies the control signal for dynamic resetting. |
|  | Reset | Specifies the control signal for static resetting. |
|  | Signal Name | Specifies the name of the connected signal. |
|  | Signal Connected | Shows that a signal is connected at the terminal. |
|  | Signal Disconnected | Shows that a signal is disconnected from the terminal. |
|  | Terminal Name | Specifies the terminal name. |

| --- | --- |
| Output Name | Specifies the name of the signal to be output. |
| Inverted Output Name | Specifies the name of the inverted signal to be output. |
| Inverted output | Specifies that DIAdem adds an inverted output to the block. The inverted control output has the reciprocal value of the control output. |

## TOPIC 00735: General Layout » Frame

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisframe_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisframe_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([Binary](../dlgvis/dlgvislistbinary_dialog.htm) | [Checkbox](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_control/dlgmancndcheck_dialog.htm) | [Color Matrix](../dlgvis/dlgvislistmatrix_dialog.htm) | [Dial](../dlgvis/dlgmanrotarypoti_dialog.htm) | [Gauge](../dlgvis/dlgvislistgauge_dialog.htm) | [Numeric Input](../dlgvis/dlgmankeyboard_dialog.htm) | [Polar](../dlgvis/dlgvislistpolar_dialog.htm) | [Push Button](../dlgvis/dlgmanbutton_dialog.htm) | [Push Button](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_control/dlgcndfctkey_dialog.htm) | [Radio Button](../dlgvis/dlgmanradio_dialog.htm) | [Radio Button](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlg_control/dlgmancndradio_dialog.htm) | [Slider Control](../dlgvis/dlgmansliderpoti_dialog.htm) | [Status](../dlgvis/dlgvisliststate_dialog.htm) | [Switch](../dlgvis/dlgmanswitch_dialog.htm)) > General Layout » Frame

General Layout » Frame

Use this dialog box to specify the frame of display and manual instruments.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Frame |  |  |
|  | Display 3D frame | Specifies that DIAdem frames the instrument. |
|  | Frame filling | Specifies the frame color. If you select Filling Effects instead of a color, DIAdem opens the Color Shading dialog box. |
|  | Graphics file | Shows the name and the path of the loaded graphics file. DIAdem uses this graphic to fill the frame of a display instrument. |
|  | Browse | Opens the dialog box where you select a graphics file. |
|  | Keep aspect ratio | Specifies that DIAdem maintains the width-to-height ratio of an image. |
|  | Display graphic | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the graphic. If you do not select this setting, DIAdem hides the loaded graphic. |
|  |  |  |
|  | VISUAL Page | Specifies the VISUAL page. Use VISUAL pages to show or to hide various displays simultaneously during the layout phase, or to block parameter modification for these displays. |

#### Further Settings

Frame | [Labels](../dlgvis/dlgvislabel_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

## TOPIC 00736: General Layout » Frame

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisframebgrd_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisframebgrd_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([Bars](../dlgvis/dlgvislistbar_dialog.htm) | [Container](../dlgvis/dlgvislistcont_dialog.htm) | [Curve](../dlgvis/dlgvislistcurve_dialog.htm) | [Cylinder Tachometer](../dlgvis/dlgvislistdrum_dialog.htm) | [Digits](../dlgvis/dlgvislistnumber_dialog.htm) | [Map Display](../dlgvis/dlgvislistmap_dialog.htm) | [Message](../dlgvis/dlgvislistmessag_dialog.htm) | [Recorder](../dlgvis/dlgvislistscroll_dialog.htm) | [Scatter](../dlgvis/dlgvislistscatterdisp_dialog.htm) | [Spike](../dlgvis/dlgvislistspike_dialog.htm) | [Table](../dlgvis/dlgvislisttable_dialog.htm) | [Wiper](../dlgvis/dlgvislistwiper_dialog.htm) | [XY-Display](../dlgvis/dlgvislistxy_dialog.htm)) > General Layout » Frame

General Layout » Frame

Use this dialog box to specify the frame and the background of display and manual instruments.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Frame |  |  |
|  | Display 3D frame | Specifies whether DIAdem plots a 3D frame around the display. |
|  | Frame filling | Specifies the frame color. If you select Filling Effects instead of a color, DIAdem opens the Color Shading dialog box. |
|  | Graphics file | Shows the name and the path of the loaded graphics file. DIAdem uses this graphic to fill the frame of a display instrument. |
|  | Browse | Opens the dialog box where you select a graphics file. |
|  | Keep aspect ratio | Specifies that DIAdem maintains the width-to-height ratio of an image. |
|  | Display graphic | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the graphic. |
| Background Display |  |  |
|  | Background filling | Specifies the background color of the display instrument. If you select Filling Effects instead of a color, DIAdem opens the Color Shading dialog box. |
|  | Graphics file | Shows the name and the path of the loaded graphics file. DIAdem uses this graphic as the background of a display instrument. |
|  | Browse | Opens the dialog box where you select a graphics file. |
|  | Keep aspect ratio | Specifies that DIAdem maintains the width-to-height ratio of an image. |
|  | Display graphic | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the graphic. |
|  | VISUAL Page | Specifies the VISUAL page. Use VISUAL pages to show or to hide various displays simultaneously during the layout phase, or to block parameter modification for these displays. |

## TOPIC 00738: Gauge: Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisgauge_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisgauge_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > [Gauge](../dlgvis/dlgvislistgauge_dialog.htm) > Gauge: Parameters

Gauge: Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the gauge display.

#### Settings

| Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- |
| Instrument | Specifies the display mode for the instrument.The Analog Instrument uses a quadrant, the Gauge Display uses a semicircle, and the Tacho Display uses a three-quarter circle as the scale that the gauge moves in. |
| Aperture angle | Specifies the circular surface of the scale. |
| Direction angle | Specifies the position of the smallest value. The starting point is at the top and DIAdem moves this point anti clockwise. |
| Display refresh | Specifies the frequency at which DIAdem redisplays the measured values. |
| Unit | Specifies the unit of the display clock. |
| Display signal names | Specifies that DIAdem displays the signal name in VISUAL. |
| Y-Axis | Specifies the display mode of the gauge displays. You can select one instrument with several gauges or several instruments with one gauge. You can choose between a scale with the percentages of the display area, or a scale with the physical values. |
| Number of miniticks | Specifies the number of miniticks between two ticks. |

#### Further Settings

[Signal List](../dlgvis/dlgvislistgauge_dialog.htm) | Parameters | [Limit Values](../dlgvis/dlgvislimitdef_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframe_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../dlgvis/dlgvislabellegscale_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainps_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopreset_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00740: Curve: Signal List

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvislistcurve_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvislistcurve_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > Curve: Signal List

Curve: Signal List

Use the curve display to display the measurement values as a curve over time. When the curve reaches the right side of the display window, DIAdem deletes the curve and starts plotting a new curve from the left side.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Extend List | Adds a signal to the end of the list. |
|  | Reduce List | Deletes the signal at the end of the list. |
|  | List Length | Opens the dialog box where you specify the number of possible signals at one block. |
|  | Combined Settings | Opens the dialog box where you enter the curve color, the line width, and the display range for the selected signals. |
|  | Display Signal | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the signal in the display instrument. |
|  | Signal Name | Specifies the name of the signal. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color of the curve. |
|  | Width | Specifies the line width of the curve. |
|  | From | Specifies the lower limit of the display range. |
|  | To | Specifies the upper limit of the display range. |
|  | Terminal Name | Specifies the terminal name. |

#### Further Settings

Signal List | [Parameters](../dlgvis/dlgviscurve_dialog.htm) | [Limit Values](../dlgvis/dlgvislimitdef_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframebgrd_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../dlgvis/dlgvislabellegscale_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainps_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopreset_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00742: Gauge: Signal List

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvislistgauge_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvislistgauge_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > Gauge: Signal List

Gauge: Signal List

Use the gauge display to display the current measurement value with a gauge.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Extend List | Adds a signal to the end of the list. |
|  | Reduce List | Deletes the signal at the end of the list. |
|  | List Length | Opens the dialog box where you specify the number of possible signals at one block. |
|  | Combined Settings | Opens the dialog box where you enter the display color for the display range for the selected signals. |
|  | Display Signal | Specifies whether DIAdem displays the signal in the display instrument. |
|  | Signal Name | Specifies the name of the signal. |
|  | Color | Specifies the color for the scale and the gauge. |
|  | From | Specifies the lower limit of the display range. |
|  | To | Specifies the upper limit of the display range. |
|  | Terminal Name | Specifies the terminal name. |

#### Further Settings

Signal List | [Parameters](../dlgvis/dlgvisgauge_dialog.htm) | [Limit Values](../dlgvis/dlgvislimitdef_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframe_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../dlgvis/dlgvislabellegscale_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainps_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopreset_dialog.htm)

## TOPIC 00745: Recorder: Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisscroll_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisscroll_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > [Recorder](../dlgvis/dlgvislistscroll_dialog.htm) > Recorder: Parameters

Recorder: Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the recorder display.

#### Settings

| Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- |
| Horizontal | Specifies that the recorder plots the curve from right to left. |
| Vertical | Specifies that the recorder plots the curve from top to bottom. |
| Range | Specifies the display range of the time axis. |
| Block width [%] | Specifies the percentage of the time range, by which DIAdem moves the curve when it reaches the edge of the window. |
| History depth | Specifies the past time range that you can view using the recorder. |
| Scaling | Specifies the display mode of the time axis.Use the Delta t setting to display on the time axis the range from zero to the value you specify as the Range. This scale does not change during the measurement.Use the Scrolling setting to continue the time axis when it reaches the edge of the window.Use the Absolute time setting to display the current time. |
| Unit | Specifies the unit of the time axis. |
| Use time range for hardware clock | Specifies that DIAdem uses the specified time domain of the time axis if the measurement is set to the Hardware clock mode. If you do not enable this setting, DIAdem can adjust the time domain in order to optimize the speed. |
| Display grid lines | Specifies that DIAdem displays grid lines inside the display area. |
| Allow manual changes to the value range | Specifies that you can change the scale of the display manually during a measurement. Refer to the Help page Manual Axis Scaling for further information. |
| Y-axis | Specifies the display mode for the y-axis. You can choose between one y-axis and several y-axes, and between a display that is a percentage of the display area and a display of the physical values. |
| Y-scaling | Specifies whether y-axis scaling is automatic or manual.If you select Manual, DIAdem uses the signal list settings.If you select automatic scaling, you can specify a minimum range, a fixed range, or an automatic scaling with peak hold. DIAdem checks the value range in the specified time domain and if necessary, adjusts the value range. If a measurement value exceeds or undershoots the value range at a different point in time, DIAdem adjusts the value range directly. |
| Y-scale format | Specifies the format specification of the y-scales. By specifying a format, you can prevent DIAdem from truncating the scales following changes to the value range. If you do not enter a value, DIAdem automatically specifies the scales above the specified value range. |

#### Further Settings

[Signal List](../dlgvis/dlgvislistscroll_dialog.htm) | Parameters | [Limit Values](../dlgvis/dlgvislimitdef_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframebgrd_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../dlgvis/dlgvislabellegscale_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainps_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopreset_dialog.htm)

#### Examples

[3D Interpolation](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_3d_map.htm) | [Automatic Dynamic Visualization](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av7.htm) | [Comparing Automatic Scalings](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_script_autoscaling1.htm) | [Different Offset Corrections](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_autoscaling_offset.htm) | [Display Instruments](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av17.htm) | [GPS Visualization](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_ab6.htm) | [Manual Dynamic Visualization](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av8.htm) | [Manual Input](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av27.htm) | [Message Display](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av15.htm) | [Monitoring a Facility Using Visualization Levels and Radio Buttons](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_facilit4_2.htm) | [Monitoring a Facility with Visualization Points](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_ab3.htm) | [Numeric and Tabular Display](../../explonl/explonl/exponl_num_tab_extended.htm) | [Numeric Display with Scroll Bar and Bar Display](../../explonl/explonl/exponl_example_dac.htm) | [Recording Video and Measurement Data](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_video.htm) | [Remote Control of Manual Instruments](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_av16.htm) | [Scaling Several Curves Automatically](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_script_autoscaling2.htm) | [Scatter Display](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_scatter.htm) | [Start Interval of the Offset Correction](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_autoscaling_offsetnv.htm) | [Visualizing Measurement Data from a Car Race](../../explonl/explonl/explonl_dac_ab5.htm)
