Spike: Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the spike display.

#### Settings

| Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- |
| Range | Specifies the display range of the time axis. |
| Unit | Specifies the unit of the time axis. |
| Start time | Specifies the time after which DIAdem starts plotting the curve. The BlInstrUnit variable specifies the unit of the time span. |
| Scaling | Specifies the display mode of the time axis.Use the Delta t setting to display on the time axis the range from zero to the value you specify as the Range. This scale does not change during the measurement.Use the Scrolling setting to continue the time axis when it reaches the edge of the window.Use the Absolute time setting to display the current time. |
| Use time range for hardware clock | Specifies that DIAdem uses the specified time domain of the time axis if the measurement is set to the Hardware clock mode. If you do not enable this setting, DIAdem can adjust the time domain in order to optimize the speed. |
| Display grid lines | Specifies that DIAdem displays grid lines inside the display area. |
| Allow manual changes to the value range | Specifies that you can change the scale of the display manually during a measurement. Refer to the Help page Manual Axis Scaling for further information. |
| Y-axis | Specifies the display mode for the y-axis. You can choose between one y-axis and several y-axes, and between a display that is a percentage of the display area and a display of the physical values. |
| Y-scaling | Specifies whether y-axis scaling is automatic or manual.If you select Manual, DIAdem uses the signal list settings.If you select automatic scaling, you can specify a minimum range, a fixed range, or an automatic scaling with peak hold. DIAdem checks the value range in the specified time domain and if necessary, adjusts the value range. If a measurement value exceeds or undershoots the value range at a different point in time, DIAdem adjusts the value range directly. |
| Y-scale format | Specifies the format specification of the y-scales. By specifying a format, you can prevent DIAdem from truncating the scales following changes to the value range. If you do not enter a value, DIAdem automatically specifies the scales above the specified value range. |

## TOPIC 00748: Status: Parameters»Status

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisstatedef_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgvisstatedef_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > [Status](../dlgvis/dlgvisliststate_dialog.htm) > [Parameters](../dlgvis/dlgvisstate_dialog.htm) > Status: Parameters»Status

Status: Parameters»Status

Use this dialog box to specify the number of statuses and their properties.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Status up To | Specifies the upper limit of the status. |
|  | Color | Specifies which color to display. |
|  | Audio file | Specifies which WAV file play. Double-click the entry field to load a WAV file. |
|  | Audio file | Opens the dialog box where you select an audio file. |
|  | Text | Specifies the text to be displayed. Double-click the input field and enter a text. Specify the text display in the Font dialog box.To access this setting you must select More in the Parameters dialog box. |
|  | Graphics file | Specifies the graphic to be displayed. Double-click the entry field to load a graphics file.To access this setting you must select More in the Parameters dialog box. |
|  | Graphics file | Opens the dialog box where you select a graphics file. |

#### Further Settings

Input » System

Use this dialog box to specify the incoming system signal for clocking. Use the system input to clock the block separately from the default system clock.

Refer to [Block Terminals in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/block_general.htm) for more information on block terminals. Refer to the page [Buses in DIAdem DAC](../../gendacsv/dac_general/wires.htm) for more information on the buses that you use to connect blocks.

#### Settings

|  | Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Connect Signal | Connects the signal that is selected in the list to the terminal. |
|  | Disconnect Signal | Disconnects the signal that is selected in the list from the terminal. |
|  | Signal Name | Contains the name of the connected signal. |
|  | Signal Connected | Shows that the signal is connected at the terminal. |
|  | Signal Disconnected | Shows that the signal is disconnected from the terminal. |
|  | Terminal Name | Specifies the terminal name. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=diadem path=dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgviswiper_dialog.htm language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00750: Wiper: Parameters

- bundle_id: `diadem`
- source_path: `dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgviswiper_dialog.htm`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/diadem/raw/resource/enus/dlgvis/dlgvis/dlgviswiper_dialog.htm
- source_language: `enus`
- document_id: `diadem`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: ``

([DIAdem VISUAL](../dlgvis/dlgvis_general.htm) | [Single Point Processing Dialog Boxes](../../dlgdacsv/dac_dlgssinglevalues_overview.htm)) > [Display Instruments](../dlgvis/dlgvis_signaldisplay_general.htm) > [Wiper](../dlgvis/dlgvislistwiper_dialog.htm) > Wiper: Parameters

Wiper: Parameters

Use this dialog box to specify the wiper display.

#### Settings

| Name | Specifies the unique block name in the block diagram. |
| --- | --- |
| Range | Specifies the display area of the time axis. |
| Unit | Specifies the unit of the time axis. |
| Start time | Specifies the time after which DIAdem starts plotting the curve. The BlInstrUnit variable specifies the unit of the time span. |
| Scaling | Specifies the display mode of the time axis.Use the Delta t setting to display on the time axis the range from zero to the value you specify as the Range. This scale does not change during the measurement.Use the Scrolling setting to continue the time axis when it reaches the edge of the window.Use the Absolute time setting to display the current time. |
| Use time range for hardware clock | Specifies that DIAdem uses the specified time domain of the time axis if the measurement is set to the Hardware clock mode. If you do not enable this setting, DIAdem can adjust the time domain in order to optimize the speed. |
| Display grid lines | Specifies that DIAdem displays grid lines inside the display area. |
| Allow manual changes to the value range | Specifies that you can change the scale of the display manually during a measurement. Refer to the Help page Manual Axis Scaling for further information. |
| Y-axis | Specifies the display mode for the y-axis. You can choose between one y-axis and several y-axes, and between a display that is a percentage of the display area and a display of the physical values. |
| Y-scaling | Specifies whether y-axis scaling is automatic or manual.If you select Manual, DIAdem uses the signal list settings.If you select automatic scaling, you can specify a minimum range, a fixed range, or an automatic scaling with peak hold. DIAdem checks the value range in the specified time domain and if necessary, adjusts the value range. If a measurement value exceeds or undershoots the value range at a different point in time, DIAdem adjusts the value range directly. |
| Y-scale format | Specifies the format specification of the y-scales. By specifying a format, you can prevent DIAdem from truncating the scales following changes to the value range. If you do not enter a value, DIAdem automatically specifies the scales above the specified value range. |

#### Further Settings

[Signal List](../dlgvis/dlgvislistwiper_dialog.htm) | Parameters | [Limit Values](../dlgvis/dlgvislimitdef_dialog.htm) | [Frame](../dlgvis/dlgvisframebgrd_dialog.htm) | [Labels](../dlgvis/dlgvislabellegscale_dialog.htm) | [Position](../dlgvis/dlgvispos_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Data](../dlgvis/dlgvisdatainps_dialog.htm) | [Inputs»Control](../dlgvis/dlgvisctrlinpstartstopreset_dialog.htm)
